/ /dpal sa skya pa'i yab chos kyi nying khu 'khor lo sdom pa'i dam pa'i chos byung ba'i tshul legs par bshad pa bde mchog chos kun gsal ba'i nyin byed ces bya ba bzhugs so//

rgya gar skad du/ shrI wan tsakra samba ra tsa bhaTTa raka sanggu ru tri kA la dznya siddhi shwadya pra bi dwanpa na kha a ru Na rasmi dwa pa de pra Na mya ra ti tsitti na
a nu grihNantu/ bod skad du/ dpal ldan 'khor lo sdom pa dang rje btsun bla ma dam pa dus gsum mkhyen pa rab tu mkhas shing grub pa'i dbang phyug gang gi zhabs sen dmar ba'i
'od can la ni rtag tu 'dud do dgyes pa'i thugs kyis rjes su 'dzin par shog brtan g.yo kun khyab 'khor 'das bdag po he ru ka /bde stong dbyer med mchog la rol pa'i lhag
pa'i lha/ /de nyid gsum ldan rdo rje 'dzin pa'i skur bstan pa'i/ /kho bo'i 'dren pa skyabs gnas kun 'dus bla ma rgyal/ /gzhan las ches zab rnal 'byor gsang mtha'i lam/ /'phags
pa'i yul dang bod yul gangs khrod 'dir/ /

spel zhing dar bar mdzad pa'i bka' drin can/ /skyes mchog paN grub lo tsA che rnams bsngags/ /khyad par yongs rdzogs bstan pa'i rgyal srid la/ /dbang bsgyur chos kyi rgyal
po sa skya pa/ /bla chen kun dga' snying po yab sras dang / /paN chen khu dbon brgyud par bcas la 'dud/ /thub dbang rgyal tshab skyes chen de dag gi /bzhed srol mdo sngags
bstan 'dzin mchog rnams dang / /lhag par nges don bstan pa'i srog shing che/ /kun mkhyen kun dga' bzang po phyag gi gnas/ /sa skya'i yab chos kun gyi snying po'i bcud/
/'khor lo bde mchog rgyud dang man ngag gi /bstan pa bshad sgrub sgo nas 'dzin pa la/ /'gran bral mus chen sems dpa' che der dad/ /dam pa de nyid slob tshogs dang bcas pa/
/ma rgyud bstan la mkhas pa'i grags dkar gyis/ /deng sang dus kyang phyogs de'i bstan 'dzin rnams/ /bde mchog bdag po kun gyis bstod cing mchod/ /gzhan yang bod yul dbus
kyi dpal

sa skyar/ /snyigs dus bstan pa'i me ro gso ba la/ /gzhan dang mtshungs pa med pa'i mdzad 'phrin can/ /sngags 'chang sprul pa'i sku der phyag bgyi'o/ /de sras grub pa'i khyu
mchog dbang po'i mtshan/ /yab rje sbas pa'i sangs rgyas la sogs pa/ /bka' drin mnyam med rnams la gus btud nas/ /bde mchog dam chos byung tshul 'chad la spro/ /rgyu rgyud
rang sems dri bcas bde ba'i mchog /thabs rgyud dri ma sel byed bde mchog lam/ /'bras rgyud dri bral bde stong zung 'jug mchog /mngon du gyur pa chos 'di'i gnas lugs yin/
/e ma rgya bod skyes chen bgrang yas pa/ /mkha' spyod do rar gshegs pa'i nye lam mchog /dpal ldan 'khor lo bde mchog gsang mtha' yis/ /lam srol 'di la 'jug pa skal ba bzang
/ /bla ma'i drin las chos 'di'i zab mo'i gnad/ /mang po'i don la kho bo'i blo gsal yang / /'dir ni dam chos byung tshul mdo tsam zhig /'chad par 'gyur gyi mkha' 'gros
skabs phye shig /ces mchod par brjod cing bshad par dam bcas nas/ 'dir dpal sa skya pa'i yab chos kyi nying khu 'khor lo sdom pa'i dam pa'i chos byung ba'i tshul legs par
bshad pa bde mchog chos kun gsal ba'i nyin byed ces bya ba 'di 'chad pa la don gnyis te/ spyir rgyud sde sgo drug tu dbye ba'i tshul mdor bsdus bstan pa/ sgo drug po de'i
chos skor byung tshul rgyas par bshad pa'o/ /dang po ni/ rje btsun birWa pa yab sras kyis kyai rdo rje'i rgyud la brten nas rgyud sde bzhir dbye ba mdzad pa dang / rje
'gos kyis ye shes rdo rje kun las btus kyi rgyud la brten nas gsang ba 'dus pa'i skabs su rgyud sde lngar mdzad pa ni rang rang gi rgyud

la brten nas rgyud sde'i rnam gzhag mdzad pa yin pas shin tu legs pa yin la/ de bzhin du 'dir yang rtsa rgyud le'u lnga bcu rtsa gcig pa las/ ji srid mdo bya spyod pa ni/ /rnal
'byor gsang mtha'i dbye ba yis/ /sems can mos pa sna tshogs pa/ /de dang de la dga' ba yin/ /zhes gsungs pa la brten nas mdo sde rtog pa'i rgyud/ bya ba'i rgyud/ spyod
pa'i rgyud/ rnal 'byor gyi rgyud/ gsang ba'i rgyud/ rnal 'byor gsang mtha'i rgyud de rgyud sde sgo drug tu mdzad la/ de yang rtsa ba'i rgyud las/ rgod dang blta ba lag
bcang dang / /gnyis gnyis 'khyud la sogs pa'i bdag /rgyud rnams kun tu ma gsungs te/ /de nyid bsdus pa 'khor sdom pa/ /gsang ba'i rdo rje 'jigs byed las/ /dkyil 'khor rnams
kyi mchog 'di ni/ /ma byung 'byung bar mi 'gyur ro/ /zhes gsungs pas bstan te/ rgod pa dag pa bya rgyud/ blta ba dag pa spyod rgyud/ lag bcang dag pa rnal 'byor gyi rgyud
dang / gnyis gnyis 'khyud pa dag pa bla med gzhan las kyang ma gsungs pa'i don cig 'dir ston pas/ gsang ba'i mtha' zhes bla med spyi las zab par grub la/ de yang rnal
'byor rgyud kyi mtshan gzhi de nyid 'dus pa dang / ma rgyud kyi mtshan gzhi 'khor lo sdom pa ni sangs rgyas mnyam sbyor sogs yin zhing / pha rgyud kyi mtshan gzhi gsang
ba 'dus pa dang / rdo rje 'jigs byed las kyang ma gsungs zhes pa'i don yin la/ de'i dang po rtog pa'i rgyud ni bya rgyud kyi nang tshan las tshogs gtso bor ston pa rnams
so/ /bya ba'i rgyud ni bdag nyid tha mal du gnas nas/ mdun du ras bris la ye shes pa spyan drangs pa la/ dka'

thub dang gtsang sbra sogs kyi sgo nas dngos grub bsgrub pa ste/ legs grub dang dpung bzang la sogs pa'o/ /spyod pa'i rgyud ni bdag nyid kyang lhar bskyed/ mdun du ye shes
pa spyan drangs te bdag la mi bstim pa grogs po lta bu'i sgo nas dngos grub bsgrub pa ste/ rnam snang mngon byang la sogs pa'o/ /rnal 'byor gyi rgyud ni bdag nyid kyang lhar
bskyed/ de la ye shes kyi 'khor lo dgug gzhug byas nas/ phyag rgya bzhi'i rgyas btab ste cho ga zin nas ye shes pa gshegs/ rang dam tshig pa rkyang pa'i nga rgyal du
gnas pa'i sgo nas dngos grub bsgrub pa ste/ de nyid 'dus pa la sogs pa'o/ /rnal 'byor gsang ba'i rgyud las rnal 'byor chen mo ma'i rgyud dang / pha'i rgyud gnyis su yod cing
/ 'di gnyis kyi khyad par la rje 'gos lo tsA bas/ pha rgyud gsang ba 'dus pa sogs ni zab pa dang rgya che ba gnyis ka ston pas brjod bya rgya che ba yin la ma rgyud las
ni pho nya'i lam la brten nas dbang gi mtshon pa'i ye shes skyong ba tsam zhig ston pas brjod bya rgya chung bas na/ pha rgyud khyad par du 'phags zhes bzhed kyang / 'dir
ni pha rgyud las ma rgyud zab cing / zab khyad la bla ma gong ma mang pos/ /brjod byed tshig gi khyad par/ brjod bya don gyi khyad par sogs rnam grangs mang du gsungs
kyang / zab khyad dngos ni/ rim pa gnyis kyi nang nas bskyed rim dngos bstan brjod bya'i gtso bor byas nas ston pa dang / rdzogs rim dngos bstan brjod bya'i gtso bor byas
nas ston pa gnyis la 'jog par slob dpon nag po spyod pa bas gsungs par bshad do/ /de lta bu'i pha rgyud la yang / 'dod chags zhe sdang gti mug gi /rgyud kyang rnam pa gsum
du 'gyur/ /zhes pa

ltar/ 'dod chags lam du byed pa gsang ba 'dus pa'i skor/ zhe sdang lam du byed pa gshin rje gshed kyi skor/ gti mug lam du byed pa rnam snang sgyu dra'i skor dang gsum du yod
do/ /ma rgyud la ni/ rgyud sde sgo drug tu yod par bshad pa'i/ dang po he ru ka'i rigs kyi rgyud ni/ kyai rdor gyi rgyud rnams dang / sangs rgyas thod pa dang / ma hA
mA ya la sogs pa rnams yin la/ rgyud sde bzhir 'byed pa'i tshe gsang mtha'i rgyud rnams kyang 'di'i khongs su gtogs so/ gnyis pa rnam snang gi rigs kyi rgyud ni/ mi g.yo
bla med kyi rgyud dang / rdo rje gdan bzhi'i rgyud dang / de'i bshad rgyud mantra aM sa ste thams cad gsang ba'i rgyud rnams so/ /gsum pa rin 'byung gi rigs kyi rgyud ni/
rdo rje bdud rtsi'i rgyud de/ 'di la phreng bar/ rdo rje bdud rtsi rtsa ba'i dkyil 'khor dngos su bshad cing / rdo rje bdud rtsi 'khyil ba/ rdo rje bdud rtsi khro bo ste
gsum du yod par rgyud las gsungs so/ /

bzhi pa 'od dpag med kyi rigs kyi rgyud ni ku ru kulle'i rtog pa dang / rigs kyi 'jig rten mgon po lnga bcu pa rnams so/ /lnga pa don yod grub pa'i rigs kyi rgyud la/ mgon
po mngon 'byung dang / sgrol ma bla med kyi rgyud dang / phur pa rtsa dum dang gsum las/ dang po la paNDi ta sa manta shri'i sgrub dkyil dang / dbang bka' rong pa las brgyud
pa yod par bshad do/ /gnyis pa la nyi ma sbas pas sgrol ma lha nyi shu rtsa gcig so so'i sgrub thabs dang / spyi'i sgrub thabs/ nyi shu rtsa gcig lus la bkod pa lus dkyil
gyi sgrub thabs/ lha bcu gnyis ma'i sgrub thabs/ sbyin sreg gi cho ga rnams yod par gsungs so/ /drug pa rdo rje bdud rtsi'i rigs kyi rgyud ni/ ji bzhin mnyes pa nam
mkha' dang mnyam pa'i rgyud la sogs pa'o/ /rnal 'byor gsang mtha'i rgyud ni/ rtsa rgyud rgyas pa nam mkha' dang mnyam pa le'u 'bum pa dang / 'bring po sho lo ka 'bum pa/
rtsa rgyud bsdus pa le'u lnga bcu rtsa gcig pa dang / de dag gi bshad rgyud he ru ka mngon 'byung / rdo rje mkha' 'gro/ rnal 'byor ma kun spyod sambu Ti/ nges brjod bla ma
rnams yin la/ 'khor lo bde mchog gsang mtha' ba'i skabs 'dir bshad rgyud lnga po der nges pa yin no/ /slob dpon skar rgyal zla ba'i 'grel par/ 'byung dang mkha' 'gro kun
spyod dang / /kha sbyor rgyud dang bla ma ste/ /bshad rgyud rnam pa lngar 'dod do/ /ces gsungs pa dang / rgyu mtshan gzhan yang 'di'i lugs kyi nyams len gyi gtso bo bsdu
na/ smin byed kyi dbang dang / grol byed kyi lam rim pa gnyis las/ smin byed kyi dbang ni rtsa rgyud las cung zad bshad cing / gsang mtha' ba'i lugs kyi thun mong ma yin
pa'i dkyil 'khor gyi cho ga ni he ru ka mngon 'byung gis ston/ grol byed bskyed pa'i rim pa ni rtsa rgyud las/ ba glang lhas kyi steng lding dang / /lhag ma skom byed rtsa
gnas so/ /zhes pas 'byung ba lugs ldog gi mngon rtogs bstan/ yang na rus sbal dag gi so/ /zhes pas 'byung ba lugs 'byung gi mngon rtogs bstan cing / 'di gnyis kyi ming
gi rnam grangs gzhan yang / a bhi dha las/ mngal skyes kyi mngon par rtogs pa dang / sgong skyes kyi mngon par rtogs pa zhes gsungs la/ de gnyis kyi khyad par yang / mngal
skyes glu yi sbyor ba yis/ /sgra dang sgra min rnam par brtag /sgong

skyes glu ni med pa dang / /sgra dang sgra min spangs pa'o/ /zhes gsungs pa ltar yin la/ de la rtsa rgyud dang rdo rje mkha' 'gro rtsa bshad du sbrel ba la brten nas/ mngal
skyes kyi mngon par rtogs pa ston/ rtsa rgyud dang rnal 'byor ma kun spyod rtsa bshad du sbrel ba la brten nas sgong skyes kyi mngon par rtogs pa ston/ rtsa ba'i rgyud du
bcom ldan 'das kyi mtshan tsam dang / 'khor gyi lha rnams kyi ming tsam las zhal phyag la sogs pa gsal bar ma gsungs pas/ de nyid a bhi dha na nas gsal bar bstan/ bskyed
rim gyi lam gyi yan lag sngags kyi bzlas pa dang / grogs dam tshig dang sdom pa bskyangs pa dang / rigs ldan ma mchod pa dang / sbyin sreg gi cho ga dang / las tshogs rab
'byams rnams ni rtsa ba'i rgyud nyid du bstan/ bskyed rim mngal sgong gnyis char gyi lus dkyil rnams dang / rdzogs pa'i rim pa phyag rgya bzhi'i nang nas chos kyi phyag
rgya gtum mo 'khor lo bzhi'i rnal 'byor de kha sbyor gyis bstan to/ /phyag rgya bzhi la/ las kyi phyag rgya rdo rje rigs kyi g.yung mo la sogs pa ni rtsa rgyud las dngos
su bstan/ dam rgya dang por las rgya la brten nas skyes pa'i bde ba phyis rang 'od kyi rig ma la brten nas skyong bar byed pa ni cung zad tsam bshad/ chos rgya rtsa rgyud
las dngos su ma gsungs kyang / drag po'i sbyin sreg dang / chos 'byung gi nang du A li kA li bkod pa las sngags btu ba de nyid sambu Tir nges don du bshad pa des bstan/
phyag rgya chen po ni/ de la brten nas mtshon bya don gyi ye shes skyes pa'o/ /rgyu mtshan des na gsang mtha'

ba'i lugs kyi smin grol yan lag dang bcas pa ma tshang ba med par yongs su rdzogs pa zhig rtsa rgyud nyung ngu le'u lnga bcu rtsa gcig pa dang / bshad ma thag pa'i bshad rgyud
lnga yod/ de dag rtsa bshad du sdebs pas thon cing / bshad rgyud lnga po de la gzhan mi dgos pas na lngar nges pa yin la/ yang thams cad mkhyen pa bu ston rin po ches
gong du drangs pa'i slob dpon mi thub zla ba'i lung de'i don la/ 'byung dang zhes pas sdom 'byung dang / he ru ka mngon 'byung / phag mo mngon 'byung dang gsum zin/ mkha'
'gro zhes pas/ rdo rje mkha' 'gro dang / mkha' 'gro rgya mtsho gnyis/ kha sbyor zhes pas/ sambu Ti dang rnal 'byor ma bzhi'i kha sbyor bstan pas bshad rgyud dgur yod gsungs
so/ /de ni lung de tshad mar bzhed na slob dpon de'i grangs kyang ma dgongs par song ste/ bshad rgyud dgur yod pa lung de'i tshig gong ma rnams kyis bstan nas/ slar
bshad rgyud rnams lngar 'dod do/ /zhes bshad pa'i phyir ro/ /tshad mar mi mdzad na khyed rang gis rang dgar bshad rgyud dgur bzhed par song bas/ lung des tshig 'di'i don
'di zin zhes lung don bshad pa la don med de/ lung de tshad mar mi bzhed pa'i phyir ro zhes bla ma gong ma'i gsung las 'byung ngo // ! //spyi don gnyis pa sgo drug po de'i
chos skor byung tshul rgyas par bshad pa la/ ston pa sangs rgyas ji ltar byon pa'i tshul/ byon nas ston pas dam chos ji ltar gsungs pa'i tshul dang gnyis/ dang po la yang
sangs rgyas gang la 'byon pa'i bskal pa'i rnam gzhag spyir bskal pa gang la sangs rgyas gang 'byon pa'i tshul/ bye

brag tu bskal pa bzang po'i sangs rgyas byon pa'i tshul/ khyad par mi mjed 'jig rten du ston pa nyid ji ltar byon pa'i tshul dang bzhi las/ dang po ni mngon pa mdzod las/ bskal
pa rnam pa mang bshad pa/ /'jig pa'i bskal pa dmyal ba yis/ /srid pa med nas snod zad pa/ /chags pa dang po rlung nas ni/ /dmyal ba'i srid pa'i bar du'o/ /bar gyi bskal
pa dpag med nas/ /tshe lo bcu pa'i bar du'o/ /de nas yar skye mar 'grib pa'i/ /bskal pa gzhan ni bco brgyad dang / /yar skye ba ni gcig yin te/ /de dag tshe ni brgyad
khri'i bar/ /de ltar 'jig rten chags pa 'di/ /bar gyi bskal pa nyi shu gnas/ /chags pa dang ni 'jig pa dang / /zhig nas 'dug pa dag mnyam mo/ /de dag brgyad cu la bskal
chen/ /zhes pa ltar dang / 'jig tshul yang / me yis bdun no chu yis gcig /de ltar chu bdun thal nas kyang / /me yis bdun no de nas ni/ /mjug tu rlung gis 'jig pa yin/ /zhes
gsungs pa ltar 'jig chags kyi bskal pa drug cu rtsa bzhi zo chun gyi rgyud ltar 'khor ba mtha' med du 'khor ba'i tshul gsungs pa dang / de dag brgyad cu la bskal chen/
/de grangs med gsum la sangs rgyas/ /'byung ngo mar ni 'grib pa yis/ /brgya yi bar la de dag 'byung / /rang sangs rgyas rnams gnyis ka la/ /bse ru bskal pa brgya yi rgyus/
/'khor los bsgyur rgyal 'byung ba ni/ /stong phrag brgyad cu las mi mchi/ /gser dngul zangs lcags 'khor lo can/ /de dag gling bzhi gling gnyis dang / /gsum dang bzhi la
mas rim bzhin/ /lhan cig gnyis min sangs rgyas

bzhin/ /phas bsu rang 'gro g.yul bsham dang / /mtshon brtsams pas rgyal gnod pa med/ /thub mtshan yul na gnas pa dang / /gsal la rdzogs pas 'phags pa yin/ /zhes bshad pa ltar
dang / 'jig rten chags gnas 'jig gsum sogs bskal pa'i rnam gzhag rgyas par kho bos gsung ngag chos 'byung chen mor bshad zin pas der blta'o/ /gnyis pa bskal pa gang la
byon pa'i tshul ni/ spyir yang dag par rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas kyi gsung rab dag las/ bskal pa gang la sangs rgyas gang byon tshul mtha' yas pa zhig gsungs pa yin yang /
mdo sde skal bzang las gsungs pa ltar/ bskal pa la sgron ma'i bskal pa dang / mun pa'i bskal pa gnyis las/ dang po ni sangs rgyas byon pa'i bskal pa dang / phyi ma ni sangs
rgyas mi byon pa'i bskal pa yin la/ de yang sgron bskal bskal pa bzang po la sangs rgyas stong dang lnga 'byung / de nas mun bskal drug cu re lnga 'byung / de nas sgron
bskal grags pa chen mo'i snyan pa chen po la sangs rgyas khri 'byung / de nas mun bskal brgyad cu 'byung / de nas sgron bskal dpe skar ma lta bu la sangs rgyas brgyad
khri 'byung / de nas mun bskal sum brgya 'byung / de nas sgron bskal yon tan bkod pa la sangs rgyas brgyad khri bzhi stong 'byung bar gsungs pa yin no/ /gsum pa bye brag
tu bskal pa bzang po'i sangs rgyas 'byon pa'i tshul ni/ snying rje padma dkar po'i rjes su 'brangs nas stong dang lnga 'byon pa'i lugs dang / gsang ba bsam gyis mi khyab
pa la sogs pa'i

rjes su 'brangs te sangs rgyas stong 'byon pa'i lugs dang gnyis tsam yod pa las/ dang po ni sngon byung ba 'das pa'i dus na 'jig rten gyi khams 'dir bskal pa chen po 'jig rten
pa zhes bya ba la gling bzhi pa 'di nyid du 'khor los bsgyur ba'i rgyal po rtsibs kyi mu khyud ces bya ba byung ngo / /de la sras rgyal bu mig mi 'dzum pa sogs stong
dang / rgyal phran brgyad khri bzhi stong dang bcas pa/ de'i mdun na 'don gyi gtso bo bram ze rgya mtsho'i rdul zhes bya ba sras brgyad cu dang / slob ma bram ze stong dang
bcas pa zhig yod pa de'i sras bram ze rgya mtsho'i snying po zhes bya ba sangs rgyas pa'i mtshan rin chen snying po zhes par gyur/ de nas 'khor los bsgyur ba'i rgyal po
rtsibs kyi mu khyud kyi zla ba gsum sangs rgyas de la bsnyen bkur byas shing / de nas de'i sras stong po de dag gis zla ba gsum gsum bsnyen bkur byas te lo nyis brgya dang
zla ba gsum 'das pa na/ sangs rgyas de'i yab bram ze rgya mtsho'i rdul gyis lo bdun bsnyen bkur byas chos mnyan cing rmi lam brtags pas/ rgyal po rtsibs kyi mu khyud
de stag la sogs pa'i gcan gzan gdug pa can srog chags kyis bsad par gyur pa dang / blon po kha cig shing rta bde ba la bzhon nas lam gol par 'gro ba rmis/ tshul de sangs
rgyas la zhus pas/ rgyal po rgyal rigs la chags shing mi dge ba spyad pas phyi ma ngan song du skye ba dang / blon po de dag nyan rang du 'gyur bar lung bstan/ gzhan mang
po sangs rgyas par lung bstan pa na/ bram ze rgya mtsho'i rdul gyis rgyal po la/ rgyal po chen po mir gyur pa yang rnyed dka'/ sangs rgyas

'jig rten du 'byung ba'ang rnyed par dka'/ dam pa'i chos nyan pa'ang rnyed par dka' yi bla med byang chub tu thugs skyed cig ces bskul bas/ kho bo bla na med pa'i byang chub
tu 'tshang rgya bar mi 'dod do zhes rgyu mtshan dang bcas gsungs te rgyal po sems bskyed du ma 'dod pa la/ slar yang bram zes yang yang bskul bas/ sangs rgyas pa'i zhing
bzang po byung na sems bskyed do zhes khas blangs/ de nas sangs rgyas des ting nge 'dzin la snyoms par zhugs nas sangs rgyas kyi zhing gi bkod pa bsam gyis mi khyab pa
bstan te/ gang bzang ba rgyal por 'dam du bcug pas/ rgyal po'ang dad de rang gi sangs rgyas kyi zhing bzang ba'i phyir khab tu bzhugs nas skye bo'i 'grul bcad de sems par
byed do/ /rgyal bu stong yang de bzhin du byed do/ /de'i bar la bram ze rgya mtsho'i rdul gyis srog chags mang po dge ba chen po la bkod do/ /de ltar lo bdun 'das pa dang
/ rgyal po sras bcas lhas bskul te/ sangs rgyas kyi spyan sngar rang rang gi sangs rgyas kyi zhing du sems bskyed pas/ yab rgyal po bde ba can gyi zhing du sangs rgyas
tshe dpag med du lung bstan/ sras kyi thu bo mig mi 'dzum sangs rgyas 'od zer kun nas 'phags pa dpal brtsegs kyi rgyal po/ bu gnyis pa mthu chen thob sangs rgyas rab tu brtan
pa yon tan nor bu brtsegs pa'i rgyal po/ gsum pa 'jam dpal te sangs rgyas kun tu gzigs/ bzhi pa kun tu bzang po/ lnga pa padma dam pa/ drug pa dbang bsgyur dbang phyug
rgyal po/ bdun pa snang ba rdul bral spos mthong

dbang phyug rgyal po/ brgyad pa ye shes rdo rje rnal 'byor 'gyings pa'i dbang phyug rnams su lung bstan/ de nas bar skabs 'dir srog chags khri sangs rgyas su lung bstan to/
/de nas sras dgu pa sangs rgyas mi 'khrugs pa/ bcu pa gser gyi me tog bcu gcig pa rgyal ba'i zla ba dang / de bzhin du rgyal bu gzhan rnams kyang sangs rgyas re re lung
bstan/ de nas rgyal phran brgyad khri bzhi stong / srog chags dung phyur phrag dgu dang bye ba phrag gnyis/ rgya mtsho'i rdul gyi sras brgyad cu/ slob ma stong phrag gcig
bram ze bye ba phrag gsum rnams lung bstan pas/ rnam par gzigs dang / gtsug tor can dang / thams cad skyob kyi bar du gyur to/ /de nas bram ze rig byed klog pa stong gi
dang po lung bstan/ de nas rig byed klog pa stong gi gnyis pa karma skyong ni/ bskal pa bzang po'i sangs rgyas dang po 'khor ba 'jig gsum pa ti bu ru ni bskal bzang gi sangs
rgyas gser thub/ bzhi pa kun gyis bsrung ni sangs rgyas 'od srung / lnga pa dri med 'od ni byams pa/ de bzhin du lhag ma rnams kyang lung bstan nas/ de nas bram ze rgya
mtsho'i rdul gyis rig byed klog pa stong gi tha ma de la/ zhing bzung sems skyed cig gsungs pas/ cung zad bsam long yod do zer nas/ de nas bram ze rgya mtsho'i rdul gyi
bsnyen bkur ba lngas/ zhing bzung sems bskyed pas bskal pa bzang po'i sangs rgyas su lung bstan to/ /de nas rig byed klog pa stong gi tha ma des sangs rgyas rin chen snying
po la/ bskal pa bzang po de

la thub pa nyi ma du mchi bar 'gyur zhus pas/ thub pa stong dang bzhi 'byung bar 'gyur ro gsungs pa dang / de yis gsol pa/ thub pa stong dang bzhi po de dag gi sku tshe'i tshad
gdul bya la sogs pa ji tsam pa de tsam du bdag gyur cig ces smon lam btab pas/ legs so gnang ste sangs rgyas gsal mdzad ces par lung bstan to/ /de nas bram ze rgya mtsho'i
rdul gyi dgongs pas/ rgyal po chen po la sogs pa srog chags mang po sems bskyed cing / sangs rgyas kyi zhing dag pa yang bzung zin gyi da ni bdag gis sems bskyed par
bya yis snyam du dgongs te/ zhing ma dag pa mi mjed kyi zhing / sems can ma rungs pa mi dge ba bcu tshang bar spyod pa/ mtshams med lnga byed pa shin tu 'dul dka' ba rnams
la thugs rjes lhag par gzigs nas smon lam lnga brgya btab ste bden pa'i stobs brjod pas/ sangs rgyas rin chen snying pos legs so gnang ste/ byang chub sems dpa' rnams
kyi brtson 'grus brtsams pa ni bzhi ste/ sangs rgyas kyi zhing ma dag par smon pa dang zhes sogs dang / khyod ni padma dkar po lta bu'i byang chub sems dpa'o/ /gzhan ni
me tog lta bu'i byang chub sems dpa' 'o/ /zhes bya ba la sogs bsngags pa bsam gyis mi khyab pa brjod nas/ bskal pa bzang po'i sangs rgyas shAkya thub pa lung bstan/ phyogs
bcu'i sangs rgyas thams cad kyi skyes bskur/ lha dang mi'i skye dgu thams cad kyis mchod do/ /de nas sangs rgyas rin chen snying po yang mya ngan las 'da' ba'i tshul bstan/
bram

ze rgya mtsho'i rdul yang rab tu byung / lo nyis khri'i bar du tshangs par spyod pa byas so/ /de ltar snying rje padma dkar po nas 'byung ba'i rjes su 'brangs na bskal pa bzang
po 'di la sangs rgyas stong dang lnga 'byung ba yin no/ /gnyis pa gsang ba bsam gyis mi khyab pa'i mdo'i rjes su 'brangs te stong 'byon pa'i tshul ni sngon byung ba
'das pa'i dus na bskal pa mdzes par snang ba la/ 'jig rten gyi khams rnam par rgyal ba zhes bya bar sangs rgyas ston mtha' yas rin chen sna tshogs bkod pa'i rgyal po zhes
pa byung / de'i tshe pho brang rnam par dag pa can du 'khor los bsgyur ba'i rgyal po yul 'khor bsrung zhes bya ba btsun mo bdun 'bum dang / sras stong yod pa zhig byung
ba des sangs rgyas dge slong gi dge 'dun dang bcas pa la lo bye bar bsnyen bkur te/ dge slong re re la yang g.yog gsum gsum phul zhing / rgyal bu de dag sangs rgyas 'byung
ba brgya lam rnyed par 'gyur/ /mir skye ba yang shin tu dka' bas rnyed/ /grogs po gang dag dad dang chos nyan pa/ /'di 'dra bskal pa brgyar yang rnyed par dka'/ /zhes pa
la sogs pa'i tshigs bcad 'don du bcug ste/ tsandan sbrul gyi snying po'i khang pa brtsegs pa'i nang du rgyal po sras dang btsun mor bcas pa bzhugs pa'i ring nas nam mkha'
la byon te sangs rgyas kyi spyan sngar 'khod pa dang / bcom ldan 'das kyis/ rgyal po chen po dad pa 'di yongs su ma nyams na khyad par du 'gro bar 'gyur ba'o/ /zhes pa
la sogs pa'i chos bstan pa nyan nas rang gi khyim du phyin pa dang /

zla ba nya ba la babs pa'i tshe/ btsun mo ma smad pa'i pang par khye'u chos sems dang / dpe med ma'i pang bar chos kyi blo gros gnyis brdzus te byung ngo / /de gnyis dang bcas
te sangs rgyas la chos nyan pa'i tshe/ rgyal po'i thugs la rgyal bu 'di dag thams cad byang chub tu zhugs pa sha stag yin na gang thog mar sangs rgyas brtag pa bya snyam
du sems te/ gzhon nu thams cad kyi ming bris nas bum par bcug zhag bdun mchod pa byas te btsun mo'i 'khor dang sras stong dang gzhon nu gnyis dang bcas pa'i mdun du/
nang mi'i bum pa'i nang nas ming rnams phyung bas/ thog mar gzhon nu rnam par dga' ba'i blo gros kyi ming byung ba na/ sa g.yos shing rol mo'i sgra byung ste/ de ni 'khor
ba 'jig go /de nas rnam par rgyal ba'i sde gser thub bo/ /dbang po zhi ba 'od srung / don thams cad grub pa shAkya thub pa/ ska rags can byams pa/ de bzhin du rim bzhin
byung ste stong gi nang nas tha ma blo mtha' yas kyi ming byung ba dang / blo mtha' yas la gzhan rnams kyis bdag cag gis sems can thams cad smin par byas/ sangs rgyas kyis
mdzad pa byas pa'i 'og tu khyod kyis ci byar yod ces smras pa dang / des/ sangs rgyas chos rnams 'di dag nam mkha' mtshungs shing 'dra/ /bdag gi yid la sems can zad pa
med snyam bgyid/ /tshul khrims kyis ni bdag gi smon lam 'di dag 'gyur/ /bdag gi smon lam ci 'dra thams cad 'dir gson cig /khyod kyi tshe chad ci tsam pa dag sdom pa dang
/ /tshogs kyi rgya mtsho'i ji snyed de dag kun

sdom pa/ /thams cad sdom pa de snyed bdag gi tsher 'gyur te/ /bdag gi dge slong tshogs kyang de kun ma lus snyed/ /ces sogs smras so/ /de ni sangs rgyas stong gi tha ma mos
pa zhes pa ste/ de yang sangs rgyas dgu brgya dgu bcu go dgu po de dag gi tshe tshad dang / nyan thos kyi dge 'dun sogs ji snyed pa de snyed du bdag nyid la 'gyur bar smon
cing mos pas na de skad du brjod do/ /de nas rgyal bu stong gis sngar gyi brdzus skyes kyi khye'u chos sems dang / chos kyi blo gros gnyis la/ khyed gnyis smon lam ji
ltar 'debs dris pas/ chos sems kyis nga khyed thams cad kyi lag na rdo rjer gyur te/ nang na spyod cing de bzhin gshegs pa'i gsang ba thams cad las phyi rol tu ma gyur la/
phyi nang gi chos thams cad nyan mos rtogs par smon lam btab ste/ de ni phyag na rdo rje ste sangs rgyas thams cad kyi bka' sdud pa po de yin zhing / ma 'ongs pa na bskal
pa rnam par sbyong ba la/ 'jig rten gyi khams kun nas yongs su dag par sangs rgyas rdo rje rnal 'byor rnon po zhes par 'gyur bar lung bstan to/ /chos kyi blo gros kyis/
sangs rgyas de thams cad la chos kyi 'khor lo bskor bar bskul bar gsol ba 'debs pa por smon lam btab ste/ de ni tshangs pa gtsug phud can no/ /yab rgyal po yul 'khor bsrung
ni sangs rgyas mar me mdzad yin no/ /des na gsang ba bsam gyis mi khyab pa'i mdo'i rjes su 'brangs na bskal pa bzang po 'di la sangs rgyas stong 'byung ba yin la/ 'o
na ci'i phyir bskal pa bzang po zhes brjod ce

na/ 'jig rten 'di chags pa'i tshe chu'i dkyil 'khor gyi nang nas gser gyi padmo stong byung ba la lha rnams kyis brtags pas sangs rgyas stong 'byung ba'i ltas su shes te/ kye
ma bskal pa 'di ni bzang po'o zhes brjod pas bskal pa bzang po zhes grags par bshad do/ /bzhi pa khyad par du mi mjed 'jig rten gyi khams 'dir ston pa nyid ji ltar byon
pa'i tshul la theg pa thun mong ba'i ston pa ji ltar byon pa'i tshul dang / thun mong ma yin pa'i ston pa he ru ka ji ltar byon pa'i tshul gnyis las/ dang po ni/ ston pa
'di gang du byon pa'i zhing ni mi mjed kyi khams yin la mi mjed ces pa yang bzod pa dang don gcig ste/ nyon mongs pa dug gsum gyis mi 'phrog cing bzod pa ste sems bsran
thub pas na mi mjed ces bya ste/ snying rje pad dkar las/ ci'i phyir 'jig rten gyi khams de ni mi mjed ces bya zhe na/ sems can de dag 'dod chags la mi mjed pa dang / zhe
sdang la mi mjed pa dang / gti mug la mi mjed pa dang / nyon mongs pa'i 'ching ba rnams la mi mjed pas de'i phyir 'jig rten gyi khams de ni mi mjed ces bya'o/ /zhes gsungs
pas so/ /de lta bu'i zhing khams 'dir ston pa thub pa'i dbang po ji ltar byon pa'i tshul la/ klu sgrub kyi mchod rten brgyad kyi bstod par/ dang po byang chub mchog tu
thugs bskyed de/ /bskal pa grangs med gsum du tshogs bsags shing / /bar du gcod pa'i bar chad bzhi 'joms mdzad pa/ /bcom ldan seng ge de la phyag 'tshal lo/ /zhes gsungs
pa

ltar/ dang po byang chub kyi mchog tu thugs bskyed tshul/ bar du tshogs gnyis ji ltar bsags pa'i tshul/ mthar mngon par sangs rgyas pa'i tshul dang gsum las/ dang po ni/ 'di
dag la theg pa che chung gi bshad tshul mi 'dra ba mang na yang / 'dir theg pa chen po'i lugs ltar bshad na/ mdo sde drin lan bsab pa las/ ston pa 'di rigs la gnas kyang
las kyi nus pas/ lcags bsregs kyi sa gzhi la me'i shing rta 'dren pa'i gyad du 'khrungs pa'i tshe/ zla bo stobs chung bas/ dmyal ba'i srung ma a bang bya bas yang yang
bsnun pas shin tu brtse ba skyes te/ de'i rkyen gyis byang chub tu sems bskyed cing / 'di la snying rje'i sems cung zad skyed cig ces smras pas/ de nyid rab tu khros nas
mdung rtse gsum pa bsnun pas tshe'i dus byas/ me'i shing rta'i dmyal ba las thar te/ bskal pa brgyad kyi sdig pa byang bar gyur to zhes 'byung la/ phung po gsum pa las/ ston
pa 'di tshong dpon gyi bu mngon dgar gyur pa na/ de bzhin gshegs pa mdzes phyin gyi drung du dang por thugs bskyed par bshad cing / bskal bzang du/ nga ni sngon tshe
dman par gyur pa'i tshe/ /de bzhin gshegs pa shAkya thub de la/ /'jam gang zhig gi dbul ba byas nas kyang / /dang por byang chub tu ni thugs bskyed do/ /zhes gsungs/ yang
snying rje padma dkar po las/ gong du bshad pa ltar bskal pa chen po 'dzin pa zhes pa la/ 'khor los bsgyur ba'i rgyal po rtsibs kyi mu khyud kyi mdun na 'don gyi gtso bo
bram ze rgya mtsho'i rdul du

gyur pa'i tshe/ zhing khams 'dir 'gro ba'i don mdzad par smon lam btab te thugs kyang bskyed par bshad do/ /yang ston pa 'di rdza mkhan gyi khye'u snang byed du gyur pa na/
de bzhin gshegs pa shAkya thub pa chen po la/ kham sa'i bum pa gcig mgron bu lnga/ mchil lham zung gcig gdugs gcig rnams phul te/ de bzhin gshegs pa khyod sku ci 'dra dang
/ /'khor dang sku tshe'i tshad dang zhing khams dang / /de bzhin mtshan mchog bzang po ci 'dra ba/ /de 'dra kho nar bdag kyang 'gyur bar shog /ces smon lam btab ste sems
bskyed cing shAkya thub pa zhes pa'i mtshan can du gyur pa yang smon lam de'i stobs las byung ba yin par bshad do/ /gnyis pa bar du tshogs gnyis ji ltar bsags pa'i tshul
la/ bsag bya'i tshogs ngos bzung ba/ ji tsam bsog pa'i dus/ ji ltar bsog pa'i tshul dang gsum las/ dang po ni/ mdo sde rgyan las/ byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi tshogs/
/bsod nams ye shes mtshungs pa med/ /gcig gis 'khor bar mngon mtho byed/ /gzhan gyis nyon mongs med par 'khor/ /zhes gsungs pas/ mngon mtho dang nges legs kyi rgyur gyur
pa'i zag bcas kyi dge ba dang zag med kyi dge bas bsdus pa'i las rnams la tshogs zhes bya la/ tshogs zhes pa'i nges tshig kyang / rgyun du bsgom pa thob nas ni/ /dge ba
yang dang yang du bsgrub/ /ces gsungs pa ltar/ saM skr-i ta'i skad du sam bha ra zhes 'byung / de bod skad du tshogs yin zhing / de yang sa ta na

rgyun du/ bha na bsgom pa/ ra ti ni yang yang ste/ rgyun mi 'chad par yang yang bsgoms pas thob pas na tshogs zhes bya'o/ /de la phye na/ mtshan 'dzin gcod pas shes rab dang
/ dge rtsa sdud pas thabs te thabs shes gnyis su dbye ba dang / theg chen gyi lam thams cad phyin drug gis bsdus pas pha rol tu phyin pa drug tu dbye ba dang / sa bcu po
re re rgyu'i pha rol tu phyin pa bcu la rim pa bzhin gtso bor spyod pas phar phyin bcu'am sa mtshan nyid pa bcu dang / dad pa'i sa dang / mos pas spyod pa'i sa ste sa btags
pa tshogs sbyor gnyis rnams su dbye ba dang / mdo sde rgyan las/ sbyin mtshungs de ston legs 'jug dang / /bdag nyid rjes su 'jug rnams kyis/ /snyan par smras dang don
spyod dang / /don mthun nyid du 'dod pa yin/ /zhes pa ltar sbyin pa'i phar phyin dang mtshungs pa'i sbyin pa dang / gzhan la phar phyin drug ston pa'i snyan par smra ba
dang / gzhan dag phyin drug nyams su len du 'jug pas don spyod pa dang / rang nyid kyang phyin drug la 'jug pa don mthun pa ste bsdu ba'i dngos po bzhir dbye ba dang / byang
sa las/ byang chub sems dpa'i spyod pa 'di bzhis ni byang chub sems dpa'i spyod pa thams cad bsdus par rig par bya'o/ /zhes gsungs pa'i spyod pa bzhi ni/ mdo sde rgyan
las/ lus can theg pa chen po dang / /theg pa dman la mos pa dang / /gnyis ka 'dun par bya ba dang / /gdul bya'i phyir na bstan rnams kyi/ /spyod pa bzhi po mdo bzhin du/
/rjes su 'brangs nas bshad pa yin/ /

zhes pa ltar te/ theg chen la mos pa rnams kyi phyir pha rol tu phyin pa'i spyod pa/ theg dman la mos pa rnams kyi phyir byang chub phyogs mthun gyi spyod pa/ gnyis ka 'dun
par bya ba'i phyir mngon shes kyi spyod pa/ theg pa gsum ka'i gdul bya smin pa'i phyir sems can yongs su smin pa'i spyod pa dang spyod pa bzhir dbye ba dang / slob dpon
shanti pas mdzad pa'i nyi khri'i 'grel pa dag ldan las/ sems bskyed bsam sbyor lhag bsam dang / /pha rol phyin drug tshad med dag /mngon par shes dang bsdu dngos bzhi/ /byang
chub phyogs mthun zhi gnas sogs/ /gzungs sogs chos kyi mdo bshad dang / /bgrod cig thabs la mkhas pa'o/ /zhes gsungs pa ltar/ sems bskyed dang / bsam pa/ sbyor ba/ lhag
pa'i bsam pa/ phar phyin drug tshad med bzhi/ mngon shes lnga/ bsdu dngos bzhi/ so so yang dag rig pa bzhi/ chos la ston gyi gang zag la mi ston/ don la ston gyi tshig
la mi ston/ nges don la ston gyi drang don la mi ston/ ye shes la ston gyi rnam shes la mi ston pa ste ston pa bzhi dang / tshogs gnyis dang / byang phyogs so bdun dang
/ zhi lhag gnyis dang / gzungs spobs gnyis dang / chos kyi sdom bzhi dang / bgrod pa gcig pa dang / thabs la mkhas pa ste brgyad cu pos theg chen gyi lam thams cad bsdus
pas mi zad pa brgyad cur dbye ba dang / mngon rtogs rgyan las/ de yang sa gser zla ba me/ /gter dang rin chen 'byung gnas mtsho/ /rdo rje ri sman bshes gnyen

dang / /yid bzhin nor bu nyi ma glu/ /rgyal po mdzod dang lam po che/ /bzhon pa bkod ma'i chu dang ni/ /sgra snyan chu bo sprin rnams kyi/ /rnam pa nyi shu rtsa gnyis so/ /zhes
pa ltar dpe de dag gi mtshon pa'i don nyer gnyis kyis theg chen gyi lam thams cad bsdus pas sems bskyed nyer gnyis su dbye ba dang / yul ni rnam pa gsum po ru/ /sbyor
ba bzhi yi bdag nyid dang / /zhes pa ltar rnam rdzogs sbyor ba/ rtse sbyor/ mthar gyis pa'i sbyor ba/ skad cig ma'i sbyor ba ste sbyor ba bzhi'am/ go sgrub/ 'jug sgrub/
tshogs sgrub/ nges 'byung sgrub pa ste sgrub pa bzhir dbye ba dang / theg pa thun mong ba dang sgo bstun nas tshogs lam/ sbyor lam/ mthong lam/ sgom lam ste slob pa'i lam
bzhir dbye ba dang / mdo sde rgyan las/ bslab gsum dbang du mdzad nas ni/ /rgyal bas pha rol phyin pa drug /yang dag bshad de dang po gsum/ /tha ma gnyis kyi rnam pa gnyis/
/gcig ni gsum char la yang gtogs/ /zhes gsungs pa ltar/ lhag pa tshul khrims kyi bslab pa/ lhag pa ting nge 'dzin gyi bslab pa/ lhag pa shes rab kyi bslab pa ste bslab
pa gsum du dbye ba dang / sbyin pa'i pha rol tu phyin pa lta bu sbyin pa las byung ba'i bsod nams bya ba'i

dngos po dang / tshul khrims kyi phar phyin lta bu tshul khrims las byung ba'i bsod nams bya ba'i dngos po dang / bzod pa brtson 'grus bsam gtan shes rab phar phyin lta bu
bsgom pa las byung ba'i bsod nams bya ba'i dngos po ste bsod nams bya ba'i dngos po gsum du dbye ba dang / byang phyogs so bdun du dbye ba la sogs pa dbye sgo bcu gcig tsam
gsungs shing / 'di dag kyang rnam grangs dang gtso che ba sogs kyi sgo nas dbye ba yin gyi/ grangs nges kyi dbye ba ni ma yin te/ mi zad pa brgyad cur dbye ba lta bu mang
po'i dbye sgo ni mi dgos shing / bsdu dngos bzhir dbye ba lta bu la mi 'du ba'i skyon yang yod pas so/ /de ltar bsag bya'i tshogs la rnam grangs shin tu mang ba zhig
gsungs mod kyang / slob pa lam gyi gnas skabs kyi tshogs thams cad bsdu na pha rol tu phyin pa bcur 'dus/ de dag phar phyin drug tu 'dus/ de dag bslab pa gsum mam/ bsod nams
bya ba'i dngos po gsum du 'dus/ de dag bsod nams kyi tshogs dang / ye shes kyi tshogs gnyis sam/ thabs dang shes rab gnyis su 'dus/ de yang stong nyid snying po can/
rnam kun mchog ldan gyi stong pa nyid kyi ting nge 'dzin du 'dus pa yin la/ des na nyams su len pa'i tshe thabs shes zung 'jug gam tshogs gnyis zung 'jug tu nyams su len
dgos shing de ltar blangs pas 'thob bya sku gnyis zung 'jug thob par 'gyur ba yin te/ rin chen phreng bar/ sangs rgyas rnams kyi gzugs sku ni/ /bsod nams tshogs las 'khrungs
pa ste/ /chos kyi sku ni mdor bsdu na/ /rgyal po ye shes tshogs las 'khrungs/ /zhes dang / rigs pa drug cu par/ bsod nams ye shes las byung ba'i/ /dam pa gnyis po 'thob
par shog /ces gsungs pas so/ /gnyis pa ji tsam gsog pa'i dus ni/ /

seng ge bzang pos brgyad stong 'grel chen dang / dbyig gnyen gyi mdzod rang 'grel gnyis mthun par/ grangs med gsum zhes pa drang don yin gyi/ nges don du grangs med sum cu
rtsa gsum gyi bar du tshogs bsog dgos par gsungs shing / de yang tshogs lam la gcig sbyor lam la gcig sa dang po nas bcu pa'i bar la gsum gsum ste/ byang chub sems dpa'i
sa rnams rdzogs nas kun tu 'od sangs rgyas kyi sa bsgrub par bzhed/ slob dpon dul ba'i lhas/ sde pa tha dad bklags par grangs med bcur bshad/ 'phags pa rgya che rol par/
bskal pa grangs med pa bdun du dge ba'i rtsa ba thams cad yang dag par bsgrub pa zhes grangs med bdun du bshad la/ dbu ma pa chos kyi bshes gnyen gyis byang chub sems dpa'i
smon lam dang / brtson 'grus la sogs pa'i dbang gis grangs med gsum gyi nges pa med/ ces grangs med gsum las nyung bas chog pa dang / grangs med mtha' yas pa dgos pa yang
yod par bzhed pa sogs lugs srol shin tu mang na yang / mkhas pa mang pos bzhed cing thams cad la grags che ba dang / byams pa mgon pos/ sa ni dang po yin par 'dod/ /'di
de bskal pa dpag med kyis/ /zhes pa dang / grangs med gsum ni rdzogs pa yis/ /bsgom pa'i lam ni mthar phyin to/ /zhes mthong lam la gcig sgom lam ma dag sa bdun la gcig
dag pa sa gsum la gcig ste grangs med gsum gyi bar du tshogs bsags pa 'di nyid gtso bor gzung bar bya'o/ /

de ltar grangs med gsum du tshogs bsags pa las 'bras bu rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas 'thob par gsungs pa'i grangs med ni/ mdzod rang 'grel dang / thub pa dgongs rgyan sogs las/
grangs kyis bgrang du med pa'i grangs med ma yin par/ grangs kyi gnas gzhan drug cur phyin pa'i grangs med la bshad pa ltar 'thad pa yin zhing / de dag gang zhe na/ mdzod
rang 'grel las/ gcig bcu brgya stong khri 'bum dang / /sa ya bye ba dung phyur rnams/ /rkyang pa yin par shes par bya/ /ther 'bum phrag khrig rab bkram dang / /gtam dkrigs
mi 'khrug khyad phyin dang / /spangs rten ded 'dren mtha' snang dang / /rgyu rigs 'od mdzes dbang po dang / /legs phyin rtogs 'gro 'bying rdul dang / /brgya rtags stobs
'khor brda shes dang / /rnam 'byung stobs mig nyal nyul dang / /wal wol khyad khyud phyan phyin rnams/ /chen por byas te bgrang bar bya/ /grangs med pa ni tha ma yin/ /gnas
gzhan drug cu par ni grags/ /zhes pa ltar/ gcig nas dung phyur gyi bar rkyang par bgrangs/ de nas ther 'bum ther 'bum chen po nas/ phyan phyin/ phyan phyin chen mo'i
bar bgrangs pas lnga bcu nga dgu de nas grangs med pa bsnan pas drug cur bgrangs pa'i grangs med ces pa de yin la/ drangs ma thag pa'i grangs kyi sdom de mdzod 'grel las
'byung yang / grangs med kyi gong gi nyal nyul/ nyal nyul chen po sogs brgyad ni mdzod 'grel nyid du mi gsal ba/ paN chen shAkya shrIs sil bu'i mdo nas kha bskangs pa yin
par bshad do/ /'o na de lta

bu'i grangs med kyi mgo gang nas 'dzin pa yin snyam na/ dang po byang chub tu sems bskyed ma thag nas mgo brtsams pa ma yin te/ dkon mchog sprin las/ nam byang chub sems dpa'
chos mnyam pa nyid du zhugs par gyur pa de'i tshe nas brtsams te bskal pa rnams bgrang bar bya yi/ thog ma'i sems nas brtsams te de ni ma yin no/ /zhes gsungs pas so/
/des na theg bsdus las/ bzang dang smon pa'i stobs can dang / /sems gtan khyad par 'gro ba yi/ /byang chub sems dpa' grangs med gsum/ /kun tu rtsom par mdzad pa yin/ /zhes
pa'i 'grel par gsungs pa ltar/ bzang ni dge ba dang / smon pa ni smon lam de gnyis kyi stobs can te/ dge ba'i stobs dang ldan pas dge ba'i mi mthun phyogs zil gyis gnon
nus pa/ smon lam gyi stobs can yin pas rtag tu dge ba'i bshes gnyen dang 'phrad pa/ mi dge ba'i grogs po mos pa ldog kyang byang chub kyi sems mi gtong bas sems brtan pa/
khyad par 'gro ba ste/ mthong chos tshe 'di nas/ ma mthong ba tshe rab phyi ma la dge ba'i chos 'phel zhing mi nyams par yon tan cung zad tsam gyis chog par mi 'dzin pa
ste/ mdor na tshogs legs par dge ba'i stobs can dang / smon lam gyi stobs can dang / rkyen dbang gis byang sems mi gtong ba'i sems brtan pa dang / yon tan cung zad tsam
gyis chog par mi 'dzin pa ste/ yon tan bzhi po de dag dang nam ldan pa nas grangs med gsum du tshogs bsag pa'i 'go rtsom pa yin no/ /gsum

pa ji ltar bsog pa'i tshul ni/ grangs med dang po ni/ ston pa 'di rgyal po'i pho brang rnam par rgyal ba'i rgyal mtshan du rgyal po tshe rnam par rgyal ba'i sras gzhon nu brtson
'grus spyod ces bya bar gyur pa'i tshe/ de bzhin gshegs pa 'od 'phro'i phung po chen po 'jig rten du byon pa la bsnyen bkur cing dge ba'i rtsa ba bskrun pa nas brtsams
te bskal pa grangs med gcig tu tshogs bsags pas sa dang po thob par gyur to/ /grangs med gnyis pa ni/ de nas grong khyer 'dzam bu chu bo'i gser du ston pa 'di rgyal po
mdzes par snang ba'i gnas chen por tshong dpon shes rab bzang por gyur pa'i tshe/ de bzhin gshegs pa dkon mchog yan lag 'jig rten du byon pa la bsnyen bkur cing rjes su
bstan pa nas bzung ste grangs med gcig tu tshogs bsags pas sa bdun pa non par gyur to/ /de nas grangs med gsum pa ni/ ston pa 'di bram ze'i khye'u gzhon nu sprin du gyur
pa na/ bram ze rin po che la rig byed bslabs nas/ de la bsnyen bkur gyi rgyu btsal ba'i phyir yul dbus kyi grong khyer dag tu ljongs rgyur song ste mthar gyis rgyal po dgra
thul gyi pho brang padmo can zhes bya ba'i tshong 'dus kyi dbus su phyin te/ de'i tshe bram ze mar me'i bdag po'i sras de bzhin gshegs pa mar me mdzad 'jig rten du byon
pa la lha rnams kyis me tog dang sil snyan glu dbyangs dang bcas pas mchod pa mthong nas/ khyod ci zhig byed dris pas/ khyod kyis mi shes sam 'di na sangs rgyas mar me
mdzad

bzhugs so zer ba na/ bram ze de kyi phung byed cing / sangs rgyas 'byung ba ni rnyed par dka' bas/ bdag gis slob dpon gyi yon phyis btsal bar byas la/ karsha pa ni lnga brgya
po 'dis sangs rgyas la mchod pa'i rgyu bya'o snyam du dgongs nas byon pa/ bram ze'i bu mo bzang ldan mas me tog utpal la bdun khyer nas 'ongs pa dang 'phrad/ bram ze'i
khye'u des bu mo me tog 'di dag nga la tshongs shig sangs rgyas la mchod pa bya'o gsungs pas/ des/ gal te khyod skye ba thams cad du bdag gi khyim thabs su dam bca' na sbyin
no zer ba la/ khye'us bu mo khyod de skad ma zer/ khyod ni g.yeng zhing rgod la/ kho bo sangs rgyas kyi chos dka' ba dpag tu med pa bsgrub pa'i bar chad ma byed cig
gsungs pas/ des/ gal te khyed lus kyi sha yungs 'bru tsam du bcad de ster yang sbyin pa'i bar chad mi byed do zer bas/ 'o na de ltar bya'o gsungs te bram ze'i bu mo bzang
len ldan mas me tog btsongs pa'i drin lan du skye ba thams cad du khyim thabs su khas blangs shing / utpal lnga nyos nas sangs rgyas la gtor te/ kr-iShNa sa ri'i pags pa
btings nas/ de bzhin gshegs pa bdag gi lhag pa'i bsam pa mkhyen par mdzod/ ri dwags kyi pags pa 'di la zhabs 'jog par mdzod cig ces bskul bas na/ sangs rgyas kyis der byon
pas dges par byas te ral pa gser gyi mdog can gdan du btings nas/ mar me mdzad kun mkhyen ye shes spyan ldan 'di la zhabs mi 'jog gi lung mi ston na 'di nyid du lus

bskam par bya'o/ /zhes yid dam brtan por bcas pa dang / ston pas zhabs bzhag ste/ dge slong dag khyed kyis khye'u 'di'i skra la rdog pa ma 'jog cig de ci'i phyir zhe na/ 'di
ni lha dang bcas pa'i 'jig rten thams cad kyi mchod gnas yin te/ ma 'ongs pa'i dus su shAkya thub pa zhes bya bar 'gyur ro zhes lung bstan pa dang / bram ze'i khye'u de
dga' ches te/ shing rta la bdun srid du nam mkha' la 'phags te/ ting nge 'dzin brgya stong yang mngon du byas/ sa brgyad pa thob pa de yin te/ ji skad du/ sangs rgyas mar
me mdzad la utpal lngas/ /gtor te ral pa gdan du btings byas pas/ /mi skye'i chos la bzod pa thob gyur nas/ /shAkya'i rgyal por 'gyur zhes nga lung bstan/ /ces dang / lung
las kyang / gang tshe mar me mdzad kyis nga / /lung bstan gyur pa de yi tshe/ /sa brgyad pa ni thob gyur te/ /dbang bcu dag kyang thob par gyur/ /ces gsungs pas so/ /de
nas bzung ste brgya byin mig bzang la sogs pa'i skye ba mang du bzhes nas sems can gyi don mdzad pa'i mthar/ bskal pa 'di'i tshe lo nyi khri pa la grong khyer nyer ldan
du sangs rgyas 'od srung byon pa'i tshe/ bram ze'i khye'u bla mar gyur pa'i bar la bskal pa grangs med gcig tu tshogs bsags pas sa bcu rdzogs/ de ltar grangs med gsum du
tshogs bsags pas gnas skabs dag tu sangs rgyas bye ba du mar bsnyen bkur cing chos gsan pa yin te/ zla ba sgron mar/ sangs rgyas dag ni bye ba phrag khrig dang / /de las
lhag pa'i gangga'i bye ma snyed/ /kun kyang bya rgod phung po

'dir bzhugs te/ /mi dbang de kun nga yis bkur sti byas/ /zhes gsungs pas so/ /gsum pa mthar sangs rgyas pa'i tshul la/ sangs rgyas kyi rang bzhin bshad pa/ nges don du sangs
rgyas pa'i tshul/ drang don du mdzad pa rnams mdzad pa'i tshul dang gsum las/ dang po ni/ spyir sangs rgyas kyi rang bzhin la rten sku/ brten pa ye shes/ mdzad pa 'phrin
las dang gsum du 'chad pa dang / sku gsung thugs yon tan 'phrin las lngar 'chad pa dang / spangs rtogs 'phrin las gsum du 'chad pa dang / phun sum tshogs pa gnyis sam gsum
du 'chad pa la sogs pa bshad tshul ches mang ba zhig yod na yang / sku gsum mam bzhi dang / ye shes lnga po rnams kyis sangs rgyas kyi sa'i yon tan nam rang bzhin thams
cad bsdus par bshad pa yin cing / de'i dang po sku la yang / chos sku/ longs spyod rdzogs pa'i sku/ sprul pa'i sku mdzad pa 'phrin las dang bzhir yod de/ mngon rtogs rgyan
las/ ngo bo nyid longs rdzogs bcas dang / /de bzhin gzhan pa sprul pa ni/ /chos sku mdzad pa dang bcas pa/ /rnam pa bzhir ni yang dag brjod/ /ces gsungs pas so/ /yang
bsdu na sku dang po gsum po der nges pa yin te/ sku gsum dag gis sangs rgyas kyi/ /sku bsdus par ni shes par bya/ /sku gsum dag gis rang gzhan gyi/ /don 'di rten dang bcas
par bstan/ /ces longs sku rang don dang / sprul sku gzhan don/ de gnyis ka'i rten chos sku dang gsum du nges pas so/ /

'o na ci'i phyir chos sku dang / longs sku dang / sprul sku zhes bya zhe na/ zag med kyi chos bsags pas chos sku'am/ yang na bden gnyis las/ chos rnams kun gyi lus yin phyir/
/yon tan bsam yas kun rten phyir/ /rigs pa'i rjes 'brangs ngo bo'i phyir/ /skyob pa rnams ni chos sku yin/ /zhes pa ltar/ chos thams cad la gdod ma nas khyab pa dang /
yon tan bsam yas kyi rten byed pa dang / ngo bo nyid du grub pas chos sku zhes bya la/ theg pa chen po'i chos la yongs su rdzogs par longs spyod rdzogs pa'i sku zhes bya
ste/ sna tshogs chos la rdzogs longs spyod/ /ces pa dang / 'di de chos rdzogs longs spyod pas/ /zhes dang / chos la rdzogs longs spyod ston phyir/ /zhes gsungs pas so/ /nges
par 'gyur ba'am/ rgyun mi brtan pa'am/ nges par gzhan du sprul zhing bsgyur bas sprul sku ste/ dpag med bsam yas sprul pa ste/ /sems can don kun bsgrub pa'o/ /zhes gsungs
pa ltar ro/ /brten pa ye shes ni lnga ste/ sangs rgyas pa'i mdo las/ chos lngas sangs rgyas kyi chos thams cad bsdus te/ lnga gang zhe na/ chos kyi dbyings rnam par
dag pa dang / me long lta bu'i ye shes dang / mnyam pa nyid kyi ye shes dang / so sor rtog pa'i ye shes dang / bya ba grub pa'i ye shes dang / zhes pa ltar ro/ /des na sangs
rgyas kyi rang bzhin ni dbyings rang bzhin gyis rnam par dag pa glo bur gyi dri ma dang bral zhing / rnam par mi rtog bzhin du mkhyen brtse nus pa'i sgo nas sems can
gyi don 'bad med 'byung

ba'i ye shes kyi sku ste sku gsum grub pa las/ dri med de bzhin nyid dang ni/ /mi rtog ye shes ma gtogs pa/ /sangs rgyas rnams kyi chos gzhan ni/ /'ga' yang yod pa ma yin no/
/zhes gsungs so/ /de nyid zag med kyi yon tan dang dbyer mi phyed pa'i dbyings dag pa gnyis ldan mngon du gyur pa'i cha nas ngo bo nyid sku ste/ mngon rtogs rgyan las/
thub pa'i ngo bo nyid sku ni/ /zag pa med pa'i chos gang dag /thob gyur rnam kun rnam dag pa/ /de dag rang bzhin mtshan nyid can/ /zhes so/ /de nyid 'og min chen por rgyal
sras 'phags pa rnams la mtshan dang dpe byad kyis brgyan pa'i skur bstan nas theg pa chen po'i chos la rgyun mi chad par longs spyod pa ni longs spyod rdzogs pa'i sku
ste/ mtshan ni sum cu rtsa gnyis dang / /dpe byad brgyad cu'i bdag nyid 'di/ /theg chen nye bar longs spyod phyir/ /thub pa'i longs spyod rdzogs skur bzhed/ /ces gsungs pas
so/ /de nyid gdul bya mtha' yas pa'i bsam pa dang mthun par rnam 'phrul sna tshogs pas sems can gyi don rgyun mi chad par mdzad pa'i sprul pa'i sku ste/ gang gi srid pa
ji srid par/ /'gro la phan pa sna tshogs dag /mnyam du mdzad pa'i sku de ni/ /thub pa'i sprul sku rgyun mi 'chad/ /ces gsungs pas so/ /de lta bu'i chos sku de la dbye na
chos can dang chos nyid kyi chos sku'am/ 'dus byas dang / 'dus ma byas kyi chos sku gnyis sam/ ngo bo nyid sku dang / rtogs pa ye shes chos sku gnyis su yod de/

gser 'od dam pa las/ de kho na nyid dang yang dag pa'i ye shes nyid tsam du gnas pa de ni chos kyi sku zhes bya'o/ /zhes gsungs pas so/ /longs sku la sa bcu pa yan chad thob
pa kho na'i yul gyi longs sku dang / sa thob pa thams cad kyi yul du gyur pa'i longs sku gnyis su yod mod kyang / dang po mtshan nyid pa dang / phyi ma btags pa bar dbu
ma pa chos kyi bshes gnyen gyis bshad pa ltar don la gnas so/ /sprul sku la ni/ bzo dang skye dang byang chub che/ /mya ngan 'das pa rtag ston pa/ /sangs rgyas sprul pa'i
sku 'di ni/ /rnam par grol ba'i thabs chen po/ /zhes pa ltar bzhi las/ mchog gi sprul sku ni/ theg pa chen po'i sbyor lam drod yan chad nas nam 'dod du mthong zhing / tshogs
lam chen po nas kyang pha rol mthong ste zhes bu ston gyis bshad la skye ba sprul sku sogs ni gang la gang 'dul la snang ste/ gang dang gang la gang dang ni/ /gang
tshe bya ba phan gyur pa/ /de dang de la de snang ngo / /zhes gsungs pas so/ /gnyis pa nges don du sangs rgyas pa'i tshul ni/ de lta bu'i sku gsum mnga' ba'i sangs rgyas
rnams thog mar nges pa lnga ldan gyi longs spyod rdzogs pa'i skur sangs rgyas pa yin zhing / sangs rgyas pa'i rgyu ni dka' ba dpag tu med pa'i bsod nams dang ye shes kyi
tshogs gnyis yongs su rdzogs pa ste/ yan lag bdun ldan las/ tshogs gnyis dag ni rdzogs pa las/ /byang chub rgyu gzhan yod ma yin/ /zhes pa ltar ro/ /sangs rgyas pa'i dus
ni bskal pa dpag tu med pa'i sngon rol tu sangs rgyas

nas/ gdul bya 'dul ba'i phyir du sangs rgyas kyi mdzad pa bsam gyis mi khyab pa bstan cing / slar yang ston par 'gyur ba ste/ yab sras mjal ba'i mdo las/ sems can rnams la
thugs brtse zhing / /sems can yongs su smin mdzad phyir/ /dpa' bo chen po rnam par 'phrul/ /bye ba brgyad bcur rgyal ba nyid/ /sangs rgyas nyid du bstan gyur kyang / /da
dung chog pa'i 'du shes gsal/ /zhes dang / da dung dang por thugs bskyed par/ /de dang der ni yongs bstan te/ /da dung yang ni 'dren pa khyod/ /sangs rgyas mang po ston par
mdzad/ /ces so/ /sangs rgyas pa'i gnas ni/ 'og min stug po bkod pa'i zhing du longs spyod rdzogs pa'i sku rten la don dam chos sku mngon du mdzad cing / 'jig rten gyi
khams grangs med pa rnams su sprul pa'i skus gcig car byang chub pa la sogs pa'i tshul ston par mdzad pa ste/ ngag dbang grangs pas/ dpal ldan stug po bkod pa nyid du don
dam thugs chud cing / /dga' ldan skye bo'i phyir ni dam pa tog dkar gyur/ /de nas 'dir ni 'gro ba'i don du shAkya'i tog gyur gang / /'chi bdag las rgyal sgyu ma kun ston
de ni rgyal gyur cig /ces so/ /tshul ji ltar du sangs rgyas pa yin zhe na/ sa bcu rgyun gyi tha mar rdo rje lta bu'i ting nge 'dzin gyis bag chags dang bcas pa'i dri ma
shin tu phra ba rnams kyang slar mi ldog pa'i tshul du sbyangs pas spangs pa mthar phyin pa dang / shes bya ji lta ba dang ji snyed pa'i don ma lus pa mngon sum du mkhyen
pa'i ye shes brnyes pas rtogs pa mthar phyin pa'i

byang chub chen po thob pa ste/ dper na rin po che'i rang bzhin gyi dag pa snod kyi sgrib byed bsal nas mngon sum du gyur pa lta bu ste/ mdo sde rgyan las/ dka' spyad dpag
med brgya phrag dang / /dpag med dge ba bsags pa dang / /dpag tu med pa'i dus dang ni/ /dpag med sgrib pa zad pa'i phyir/ /sgrib pa kun gyi dri med pa/ /rnam pa thams cad
mkhyen nyid thob/ /rin chen snod ni phye ba ltar/ /sangs rgyas nyid ni yang dag bstan/ /ces gsungs pa ltar ro/ /de ltar nges don du sangs rgyas thams cad chos kyi skur ro
gcig cing / drang don du gzugs kyi sku sngon gyi smon lam gyi rjes su 'brangs pa'i phyir/ sangs rgyas rnams gcig kyang ma yin la/ mang po'ang ma yin zhing / gcig dang tha
dad gang du'ang ma grub ste/ mdo sde rgyan las/ zag med dbyings las sangs rgyas rnams/ /mkha' ltar lus ni med phyir dang / /sngon gyi lus rjes 'brangs pa'i phyir/ /gcig
min mang po nyid ma yin/ /zhes pa dang / tha dad rigs don med phyir dang / /rdzogs dang thog ma med pa'i phyir/ /sangs rgyas gcig min dri med gnas/ /tha dad min phyir mang
po'ang min/ /zhes gsungs pas sa/ /de ltar sangs rgyas rnams thog mar 'og min stug po bkod pa'i zhing khams su sangs rgyas par bshad pa'i 'og min de la kha cig lang kar
gshegs pa las/ 'dod pa'i khams dang gzugs med du/ /sangs rgyas rnam par 'tshang mi rgya/ /gzugs kyi khams kyi 'og min tu/ /'dod chags bral khyod 'tshang rgya 'o/ /zhes
dang / slob

dpon ka rma pa la shI las kyang / 'og min zhes bya ba ni lha dag ste/ de dag gi phyogs gcig na gnas gtsang ma'i rigs kyi lha rnams yod de/ der 'phags pa nyid 'ba' zhig gnas
so/ /de dag gi steng na dbang phyug chen po'i gnas zhes bya ba yod de/ der sa bcu la bzhugs pa'i byang chub sems dpa' srid pa tha ma kho na skye ba bzhes pa yin la/ 'dir
ni de lta bu'i sprul pa dmigs pa yin no/ /zhes gsungs pas ston pa 'di longs spyod rdzogs pa'i skur sangs rgyas pa'i gnas kyi 'og min ni/ gzugs khams kyi 'og min 'di'i steng
na dbang phyug chen po'i gnas zhes bya ba'i gnas shig yod pa de yin no zhes 'dod/ de la slob dpon rin po che bsod nams rtse mo'i rgyud sde spyi rnam las/ de ni ma yin
te/ de ltar bshad pa'i gzhung yang ma mthong la/ de'i steng na gnas gzhan yod kyang / sa bcu pa rnams kyi gnas su bshad kyis/ longs spyod rdzogs pa'i sku'i bzhugs gnas su
ma bshad do/ /des na de dag 'jig rten gyi khams chung ngu yin no/ /yang de dag 'jig pa la brten pas 'jig rten gyi khams zhes pa mi rtag pa yin la/ stug po bkod pa ni mi
'jig ste/ rdo rje rtse mo las/ 'og min stug po nyams dga' 'dir/ /stug po'i zhing khams 'jig med pa/ /des na sangs rgyas rnams kyi chos/ /rdzogs par longs spyod tshul 'di
'byung / /zhes gsungs pas so/ /zhes bshad cing / rang gi bzhed pa 'god pa na/ 'o na gang yin zhe na/ 'phags pa sangs rgyas phal po che'i mdo las 'byung ba

ste/ de'ang 'jig rten gyi khams mi mjed la sogs pa bsam gyis mi khyab pa nang du chud pa ni gzhi dang snying po me tog gis brgyan pa zhes bya ba yin no/ /de lta bu du ma nang
du chud pa ni 'jig rten gyi khams rgya mtsho zhes bya ba yin la/ 'jig rten gyi khams rgya mtsho de ni de bzhin gshegs pa rnam par snang mdzad ye shes gangs chen mtsho'i
phyag gi mthil na gnas so/ /bcom ldan 'das de byang chub sems dpa' chen po rnams kyi 'khor dang bcas te gang na bzhugs pa'i gnas de ni yang dag par rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas
longs spyod rdzogs pa'i sku'i gnas yin la/ de'i nang na gnas pa'i dum bu thams cad ni sprul pa'i sku'i sangs rgyas kyi gnas yin te/ de yang blo gros kyi rim pas kha cig
la ni 'dzam bu'i gling du sangs rgyas par snang la/ kha cig la gnas gtsang ma'i 'og min tu sangs rgyas nas mdzad pa mdzad par snang la/ byang chub sems dpa' kha cig la
ni stong gsum gyi stong chen po'i 'jig rten gyi khams gling bzhi bye ba phrag brgyar sangs rgyas par mngon no/ /kha cig la ni gzhi dang snying po me tog gi rgyan gyis brgyan
pa mtha' dag gis sangs rgyas gcig tu bstan te/ phyag na rdo rje dbang bskur ba'i rgyud dang / 'phags pa mi g.yo ba'i rtog pa chen po las/ de nas bcom ldan 'das kyis
'jig rten gyi khams gzhi dang snying po me tog gi rgyan gyis brgyan pa 'di thams cad 'od kyis khyab par mdzad de zhes bya ba la sogs pa lta bu ste/ de bas na blo gros rgya
che chung gi dbye bas sna tshogs su snang ba ni sprul pa'i sangs rgyas kyi

gnas so zhes gsungs pas/ gnas gtsang ma'i gzugs khams ni longs sku'i zhing 'og min tu mdo sngags gang gi lugs la yang mi 'thad de/ lang gshegs las/ gtsang ma'i rigs dag spangs
pa yis/ /'og min zhes bya nyams dga' 'di/ /yang dag sangs rgyas der sangs rgyas/ /sprul pa po gcig 'dir 'tshang rgya/ /zhes dang / slob dpon kun snying gis de nyid 'dus
pa'i gleng gzhir bcom ldan 'das 'og min gyi lha'i rgyal po'i gnas na bzhugs te/ zhes pa'i 'grel par/ 'og min gyi lha zhes bya ba ni thog ma'i lha ste/ bcom ldan 'das rnam
par snang mdzad kyi sras kyi thu bo ste sa bcu pa'i byang chub sems dpa' 'o/ /de'i gnas ni thog mar sangs rgyas pa'i gnas so/ /zhes gsungs pa dang / gzhan yang stug po
bkod pa'i zhing ni mi 'jig par rdo rje rtse mo'i lung gong du drangs pa des legs par 'grub cing / gzugs khams kyi 'og min ni 'jig par bshad de/ slob dpon dbyig gnyen gyis/
bzhi pa na med mi g.yo'i phyir/ /zhes bsam gtan bzhi pa'i gnas brgyad po de mi g.yo bar bshad pa'i dogs spong du/ mi rtag de yi gzhal yas khang / /sems can bcas pa 'byung
'jig phyir/ /zhes bsam gtan gsum pa man chad ltar me chu rlung gsum gyis mi 'jig kyang mthar 'jig par bshad pa'i phyir/ 'o na/ gzugs kyi khams kyi 'og min tu/ /'dod
chags bral khyod 'tshang rgya 'o/ /zhes pa dang / gong gi kA ma la shI la'i lung de'i don gang zhe na/ rgyud sde spyi rnam las gsungs pa ltar/ de dag ni sprul

sku'i gnas la dgongs pa yin te/ spyir sprul sku'i gnas de la gdul bya rnams kyi blo gros kyi rim pas 'dzam bu'i gling du sangs rgyas par snang ba dang / gnas gtsang ma'i 'og
min tu sangs rgyas par snang ba dang / stong gsum gyi stong chen po'i 'jig rten gyi khams su sangs rgyas par snang ba dang / gzhi dang snying po me tog gi rgyan gyis brgyan
pa'i 'jig rten gyi khams kyi sangs rgyas gcig tu gyur par bstan pa sogs gdul bya la snang tshul mang du yod pa las/ byang sems kha cig la gzugs khams kyi 'og min tu
sprul pa'i sku de nyid sangs rgyas par snang ba la dgongs nas/ gzugs kyi khams kyi 'og min tu/ /zhes sogs gsungs pa yin par bshad do/ /gsum pa drang don du mdzad pa rnams
mdzad pa'i tshul ni/ stug po bkod pa'i mdo las/ sangs rgyas thams cad 'og min du/ /sangs rgyas ma gyur 'dod khams su/ /sangs rgyas mdzad pa mi mdzad do/ /zhes gsungs pas/
thog mar 'og min tu sangs rgyas nas/ gzod 'dod pa'i khams su mdzad pa rnams ston par bshad pa yin zhing / de lta bu'i sangs rgyas kyi mdzad pa la spyir bsam gyis mi khyab
kyang / grangs la dga' ba'i gdul bya rnams rjes su bzung ba dang / gtso bo'i mdzad pa nye bar bzung nas/ dus kyi 'khor lo las/ 'di rnams sgrol ba'i slad du sras dang rgyal
ba'i bdag po las kyi sar ni rab bzhugs te/ /mngal ni rab tu bzung bar mdzad cing mchog gi thugs rje dag gi byang chub bskyed par mdzad nas ni/ /nyon mongs dang ni bdud
rnams bcom

nas sa yi steng du chos kyi 'khor lo rab bskor te/ /sprul pa sgyu ma mdzad nas slar yang bcom ldan 'das ni dag pa'i sku can de nyid kho na'o/ /zhes mdzad pa drug tsam gsungs
shing / rdo rje gur las/ chos kyi 'khor lo bskor ba dang / /rigs dang byang chub byed pa dang / /de bzhin du ni lhar gshegs dang / /khyim nas 'byung bar byed pa dang /
/rab tu 'byung ba 'dzin pa dang / /skye ba yongs su len pa dang / /yongs su mya ngan 'das pa ston/ /zhes mdzad pa brgyad du gsungs la/ theg pa chen po rgyud bla mar/ skye
ba mngon par skye ba dang / /dga' ldan gnas nas 'pho ba dang / /lhums su zhugs dang bltams pa dang / /bzo yi gnas la mkhas pa dang / /btsun mo'i 'khor dgyes rol pa dang
/ /nges 'byung dka' ba spyad pa dang / /byang chub snying por gshegs pa dang / /bdud sde gzhom dang rdzogs par ni/ /byang chub chos kyi 'khor lo dang / /mya ngan 'da' bar
gshegs mdzad rnams/ /yongs su ma dag zhing rnams su/ /srid pa ji srid gnas par ston/ /zhes pa dang / padma'i ngang tshul gyis/ sangs rgyas kyi sku'i mdzad pa bcu gnyis la
sogs pa bsam la bying ba gsal bar bya'o/ /zhes pa dang / gzhan yang 'phags pa klu sgrub/ chos kyi bshes gnyen la sogs pa mang po dgongs pa mthun par mdzad pa bcu gnyis
su gsungs pa yin no /'o na mdzad pa bcu gnyis po sangs rgyas dang byang sems gang gi mdzad pa yin snyam na/ nyan thos pa rnams ni rgyal bu don grub yan chad du so so skye
bo rang rgyud pa

zhig gis bskal pa grangs med gsum du thar pa cha mthun gyi dge ba bsags nas mthar rdo rje'i gdan du srod la bdud btul/ gung la bsam gtan bzhi pa'i dngos gzhi la brten nas sbyor
lam yan chad rgyud la bskyed de/ tho rangs skya rengs 'char kha'i skad cig gcig yan chad la phar phyin drug po rdzogs nas mngon par byang chub 'dod do/ /mdzod las/ ston
dang bse ru byang chub par/ /bsam gtan mthar rten gcig la kun/ /de yi sngon du thar cha mthun/ /zhes dang / de grangs med gsum la sangs rgyas zhes gsungs pas so/ /de
ltar sangs rgyas nas chos dang gzugs kyi sku'i bdag nyid can du gyur nas/ kun shes nas rab bzang gi bar la chos kyi 'khor lo bskor te lhag med du mya ngan las 'da' bar 'dod
pas byang chub sems dpa' dang sangs rgyas kyi mdzad pa gnyis su mdzad kyang / 'dir ni theg chen thun mong ma yin pa'i lugs ltar/ bcu gnyis po thams cad sangs rgyas kho
na'i mdzad pa yin te/ thub pa'i dbang po 'di bskal pa dpag tu med pa'i sngon rol tu sangs rgyas dbang po'i tog ces bya bar sangs rgyas zin kyang / da dung yang sangs rgyas
dang byang chub sems dpa'i tshul bzung nas/ de dag gi mdzad pa rnams mdzad par yab sras mjal ba'i mdo las bshad pa'i phyir/ de ltar mdo de nyid las/ bye ba brgyad cur
sangs rgyas nyid/ /sangs rgyas nyid du bstan gyur kyang / /da dung chog pa'i 'du shes gsal/ /zhes sogs gsungs shing / dam pa'i chos padma dkar po las kyang / bskal pa bye
stong bsam

bgyis mi khyab par/ /de yi tshad ni nam yang med pa nas/ /byang chub mchog rab 'di ni ngas thob ste/ /nga ni rtag tu chos kyang rab mchod do/ /zhes gsungs pas so/ /de lta bu'i
mdzad pa de dag theg pa chen po rgyud bla ma nas ji skad gsungs pa dang mthun par bshad na/ gong du bstan pa ltar bram ze khye'u bla ma de tshe 'phos nas lha'i bu dam
pa tog dkar po zhes bya bar gyur te lha rnams la chos bstan pas lha'i tshogs mang po smin grol la bkod do/ /de'i tshe 'dzam bu gling pa rnams gdul ba'i dus la babs pa na/
nyid kyi bsod nams kyi mthu dang / sangs rgyas rnams kyi byin rlabs kyi rol mo'i sgra las/ bsod nams rgya chen tshogs mang dran rtogs dang / /blo gros mtha' yas shes rab
'od mdzad pa/ /mtshungs med stobs mnga' sgyu rtsal rgya che ba/ /mar me mdzad kyi lung bstan dgongs par mdzod/ /skyes mchog khyod kyi bsod nams dpal gyis ni/ /dga' ldan
pho brang shin tu mdzes mod kyi/ /'on kyang thugs rje'i thugs dang ldan pas na/ /'dzam bu'i rgyal mtshan du ni char pa phobs/ /zhes sogs kyi tshigs bcad byung bas yang nas
yang du bskul lo/ /de'i tshe lha'i bu rnams bram ze'i cha byad du sprul nas 'dzam bu'i gling gi mi rnams rig byed slob tu bcug ste/ 'di ltar mtshan dpe dang ldan na 'khor
los bsgyur rgyal lam sangs rgyas su 'gyur zhes 'don du bcug cing / yang da ste lo bcu gnyis na byang chub sems dpa' lhums su 'jug go zhes bsgrags pas/ de rang rgyal rnams
kyis thos pas rgyal po'i khab kyi mjug ma bsgyur ba'i

ri la gnas pa'i rang rgyal glang po zhes pas rdo la zhabs rjes bzhag ste 'das so/ /gzhan yang wa ra na ser rang rgyal lnga brgyas me'i khams la zhugs te 'das nas ring bsrel
rnams sa la lhung bas yul de la drang srong lhung bar grags/ de nas byang chub sems dpa' 'dzam bu gling du gshegs par dgongs nas gzigs pa lnga la gzigs te/ dus tshe lo brgya
pa/ gling 'dzam bu gling / yul dbus/ rigs rgyal rigs/ bud med yon tan dang ldan pa ste de lta bu 'dzoms pa'i dus su lha rnams la 'chi 'pho sbyong bar byed pa'i chos
bstan cing / gang gi tshe na dga' ldan gnas mchog nas/ /'dren pa skyes bu seng ge 'chi 'pho'i tshe/ /lha rnams dag la tshig tu smras pa ni/ /grogs dag bag med spyod pa spang
bar gyis/ /zhes sogs gsungs te/ rin po che'i cod pan mi pham pa'i dbu la bcings nas/ grogs po dag khyed rnams la mi pham pas chos ston gyis/ kho bo ni sems can gyi don
du 'dzam bu gling du 'gro 'o zhes gsungs pas/ lha rnams yid ma dga' nas/ skyes bu dam pa khyed ni mi bzhugs na/ /dga' ldan gnas ni mdzes par mi 'gyur ro/ /zhes pa dang
/ byang chub sems dpa' 'dzam bu'i gling de ni deng sang 'od srung rdzogs byed la sogs pa rtog ge pa drug dang / bram ze rgyus rgyal la sogs pa rjes su sgrog pa drug dang
/ rengs byed kyi bu lhag spyod la sogs pa snyoms par 'jug pa drug ste ston pa drug gsum bco brgyad kyis ma rungs par byas pas gshegs pa'i skabs ma lags so zhes gsol pas/
de dag nyid kyis zil gyis /

gnon par 'gyur te/ seng ge gcig gis gcan gzan tshogs rnams du ma rnam par skrag /rdo rje gcig gis brag gi rtse mo du ma rnam par 'jig /brgya byin gcig gis lha ma yin rnams
du ma rnam par 'joms/ /nyi ma gcig gis mun pa'i tshogs rnams du ma rnam par sel/ /zhes gsungs shing / kho bo ji lta bu'i gzugs kyis 'gro bar rigs gsungs pas/ la la tshangs
pa'i gzugs kyis rigs zer/ 'ga' zhig brgya byin la sogs pa'i rnam pas rigs zer yang / lha'i bu gzi brjid dam pa na re/ rig byed nas 'byung ba bzhin glang po che'i gzugs
kyis rigs zer ba ltar/ byang chub sems dpa' 'byon par chas pa na/ rgyal po zas gtsang ma'i khab tu/ khang pa dga' dang bya mang byung / /shing phung me tog kha bye dang /
/longs spyod 'phel zhing sgra rang khrol/ /gter mang kha bye 'od gsal ba'o/ /zhes pa ltar gyi ltas bzang po brgyad byung / de nas dpyid zla tha chung skar ma sa ga la babs
pa tshes bco lnga'i rgyal nam gyi gung la dar ba'i dus su/ yum gso sbyong la gnas pa'i tshe glo g.yas pa nas glang po che'i rnam pas lhums su zhugs te/ de'i tshe yum gyi
rmi ltas su/ gser gyi dra bas legs g.yogs spyi gtsug dmar/ /thal dkar mche ba drug dang rab ldan zhing / /dung dang kha ba dngul mdog lta bu yis/ /glang po'i mchog cig
khong du song snyam byed/ /de zhugs nas ni bdag gi lus dang sems/ /sngon chad mthong thos gyur pa ma gyur pa'i/ /gya nom bde bas shin tu bder gyur te/ /bsam gtan mnyam par

nabazhag pa nyid du gyur/ /ces pa ltar byung ste/ rmi lam de rgyal po la smras pas/ rgyal pos kyang bram ze rnams la dris pa na/ sras khyad par can zhig 'byung ste/ khab tu
bzhugs na 'khor los bsgyur ba dang / rab tu byung na sangs rgyas su 'gyur bar lung bstan to/ /de nas yum gyi lhums su rgyal sras kyi nye bar dpyad pa rin po che'i bkod pa
zhes bya bar byin gyis brlabs nas/ phyi nang thams cad phan tshun gsal ba la bzhugs te/ der yang sum cu rtsa gsum la sogs pa'i lha dang mi'i skye dgu bye ba phrag khrig
sum cu rtsa drug smin par mdzad nas/ zla ba bcu zag med kyi bde ba la longs spyod cing bzhugs/ de nas zla ba bcu rdzogs pa na me tog kha 'bus pa la sogs pa ltas sum cu rtsa
gnyis byung ba dang yum lum bi ni'i tshal du byon nas shing pa la sha'i sdong po la phyag gis 'jus te glo g.yas pa nas mngal gyi dri mas ma gos shing yum la gnod pa med
par rgyan dang na bza' dang bcas te sku bltams pa na lhas me tog gtor/ tshangs pa dang brgya byin gyis ka shi ka'i ras kyis blangs/ dga' gdong nyer dga' gnyis kyis sku
khrus gsol/ kau shi ka nga thongs gsungs/ shar phyogs su gom pa bdun gshegs te/ dge ba'i chos thams cad kyi sngon du 'gro bar bya'o gsungs/ de bzhin du lhor lha dang mi'i
sbyin gnas su 'gyur bar bya'o/ /nub tu 'di ni nga'i skye ba tha ma ste/ skye rga na 'chi med par bya'o/ /byang du sems can gyi nang na bla na med par bya'o/ /'og tu sems
can dmyal ba'i me bsad pa dang bdud gzhom par bya'o/ /steng du gshegs

te/ sems can thams cad gyen du blta bar bya'o/ /zhes gsungs te/ phyogs drug pa der gom pa bdun bdun gshegs pa'i shul thams cad du padma re re byung zhing / de'i tshe bkra shis
pa'i ltas phyogs thams cad 'od kyis khyab pa dang / yul chen po bzhi'i rgyal po bzhi la sras bzhi yang btsas/ ya rabs kyi rigs lnga brgya/ grags 'dzin ma la sogs pa'i
brgyad brgya/ 'dun pa sogs bran lnga brgya/ lnga ldan la sogs pa'i rte'u khri dang / rte'u mo khri/ ba glang khri yang btsas/ gling gi dbus su byang chub kyi shing skyes/
skyed tshal lnga brgya dang / gter kha lnga brgya yang byung bas rgyal bu'i ming don thams cad grub par btags/ 'od de byung bas rgyal po bzhi'i bu'i ming kyang 'od la dras
nas btags te/ rgyal po'i khams kyi rgyal po padma chen po'i bu gzugs can snying po/ mnyan yod kyi rgyal po tshangs sbyin gyi bu gsal rgyal/ kau shambi'i rgyal po dmag
brgya pa'i bu shar ba pa/ 'phags rgyal gyi rgyal po mu khyud mtha' yas kyi bu rab snang zhes btags so/ /gzhan yang 'od de ri bo kun 'dzin na drang srong nyon mongs med bya
ba tsha bo mes byin dang bcas yod pas mthong ste/ tsha bos/ mkhan po/ 'dir ni nyi ma thams cad dag /gcig car byung bar gyur tam ci/ /'di ltar ri dang phug bcas pa/ /'od
gcig gis ni gsal bar gyur/ /ces smras pa dang / drang srong gis/ nyi ma'i 'od tsha 'od ni bsil/ /kun tu 'jug pas thub chen 'od/ /byang chub sems dpa' 'od po che/ /lhums
nas byung bar gdon mi za/ /zhes smras pa na/ tsha bos/ 'o na de blta

ba'i phyir 'gro 'o zer ba la/ drang srong gis de da lta lha mthu bo che dag gis bskor bas blta dka'/ phyis grong khyer du gshegs te ming 'dogs pa'i tshe blta'o smras so/ /de
nas bram ze mtshan mkhan la bstan pas/ khyim du bzhugs na 'khor los bsgyur rgyal dang / rab tu byung na sangs rgyas su 'gyur ro/ /zhes lung bstan/ rigs kyi lha mchod pa'i
sar byon pas/ shAkya rnams kyis lha gnod sbyin shAkya 'phel bya ba gzhon nu'i zhabs la phyag byas pas lha'i lha zhes dang shAkya mu cor smra ba rnams thub pa bzhin du
'dug pas shAkya thub pa zhes kyang btags so/ /byang chub sems dpa' 'khrungs nas zhag bdun 'das pa na yum 'das te sum cu rtsa gsum gyi gnas su skyes so/ /de'i rgyu mtshan
yang byang chub sems dpa' dga' ldan na bzhugs pa'i dus su yum gyi tshe tshad brtags nas gshegs pas/ sras mngon par 'byung ba gzigs na yum snying gas bar 'gyur bas yum gyi
tshe tshad mthar phyin par bya ba'i ched du yin no/ /de nas gzhon nu skye dgu'i bdag mo la gtad de/ pang na 'tsho ba'i ma ma brgyad la sogs pas skyed bsrings so/ /de nas
sngar gyi drang srong de tsha bo dang bcas pas byang chub sems dpa' blta bar sems te rdzu 'phrul gyis chas pa na/ byang chub sems dpa'i mthus rdzu 'phrul nyams nas rkang
pas phyin te/ grong khyer ser skya'i sgor song ste 'phrin springs pa na/ rgyal pos don ci la 'ongs gsungs pa dang / drang srong de na re/ rgyal chen bdag ni 'dir 'ongs pa/
/khyod kyi sras ni blta phyir te/ /'jig rten 'dul ba'i

gtso bo yi/ /thub pa de ni blta bar 'dod/ /zer ba la/ rgyal pos/ de lta na gzhon nu nyal gyis ma sad kyi bar du sdod cig gsungs pas/ mnal ba nyid blta'o zer/ bltar bcug pas/
mig mi 'dzum par mnal ba mthong nas/ rigs dang ldan pa'i rta rnams ni/ /mtshan mo'i bzhi cha nyal ba ltar/ /dgos pa don gnyer rnams kyi gnyid/ /mig la yun ring mi gnas
so/ /zer zhing / lha bram ze la bstan nam zer/ bstan gsungs pas/ ji skad lung bstan zer/ 'di ni gnyis su 'gyur gyi gzhan du min/ /khyim du gnas na 'khor los bsgyur rgyal
lam/ /khyim nas khyim med rab tu byung gyur na/ /'dren pa gzhan gyi rting la mi 'jog par/ /'jig rten 'dir ni mngon rdzogs rgyal bar 'gyur/ /zhes lung bstan gsungs pas drang
srong des legs par brtags nas/ sa bdag rtog pa po rnams blo 'khrul te/ /rtsod pa'i dus na 'khor los bsgyur mi 'byung / /bsod nams mchog gi chos kyi mdzod 'di ni/ /nyes
las rnam par rgyal nas sangs rgyas 'gyur/ /mi gsal mtshan dang ldan na mi'i dbang po/ /gling bzhi rnams kyi bdag po'i dbang phyug 'gyur/ /shin tu mtshan gsal thub dbang
rdzogs sangs rgyas/ /'di ni mi mchog chos kyi 'khor los bsgyur/ /zhes smras so/ /de nas yar skyes te shAkya'i khye'u stong phrag bcu dang lhan cig tu byis pa kun gyi bshes
gnyen gyi drung du yi ge slob pa'i grwar byon te/ kyai slob dpon/ tshangs pa'i yi ge drug cu rtsa bzhi las/ bdag gang la bslab ces gsungs pas/

slob dpon ngo mtshar skyes te/ sems can dag pa ngo mtshar skyes/ /bstan bcos kun la bslabs gyur kyang / /'jig rten 'jig rten rjes bsnyeg phyir/ /yi ge'i grwar ni byon par gyur/
/yi ge gang gi ming dag kyang / /bdag gis shes par ma gyur pa/ /de la 'di ni byang gyur kyang / /yi ge slob pa'i grwar byon to/ /zhes smras so/ /de nas yi ge'i ma mo
la slob pa ltar mdzad pas/ a zhes brjod pa na 'dus byas thams cad mi rtag pa'o zhes pa dang / A ring po brjod pa'i tshe chos thams cad bdag med pa'o zhes pa'i sgra byung
zhing / lha klu dri za la sogs pa'i yig rigs thams cad mngon du gyur pa'i tshul mdzad/ rtsis pa shAkya srid sgrub kyi drung du/ rtsis dang / 'phong dang / gyad kyi 'dzings
stangs la sogs pa 'jig rten pa'i bslab par bya ba thams cad kyang slob pa ltar mdzad do/ /de nas shAkya rgan rab dag 'dus te/ 'khor los bsgyur ba'i gdung mi gcad pa'i
phyir khab mdzad par zhus pas/ byang chub sems dpas/ 'dod pa'i skyon ni bdag gis mtha' yas rig /'thab mo 'khon bcas mya ngan sdug bsngal rtsa/ /'dzin byed dug gi lo ma 'dra
ba ste/ /me dang 'dra zhing ral gri'i so dang 'dra/ /'dod pa'i yon tan bdag 'dod ma yin te/ /bdag ni bud med tshogs dang mdzes ma yin/ /bsam gtan ting 'dzin bde bas zhi
sems su/ /bdag ni mi smra nags tshal gnas par bya/ /zhes gsungs te ma gnang / phyis brtags nas/ 'dam dang ljan ljin khrod na padmo rnam par 'phel/ /mi rnams gang gi nang
na rgyal pos

mchod pa thob/ /gang tshe byang chub sems dpa' 'khor mchog thob gyur pa/ /de tshe sems can bye ba phrag khrig 'chi med 'dul/ /sngon gyi byang chub sems dpa' mkhas par gang
gyur pa/ /de dag kun gyis btsun mo sras dang slas kyang bsten/ /'on kyang 'dod pas chags med bsam gtan bde ba nyams/ /bdag kyang de dag yon tan rjes su bslab par bya/ /zhes
gsungs te gnang ba na/ rgyal pos bud med ci lta bu zhig blang gsungs pas/ gzhon nus bud med kyi yon tan yi ger bris te/ yon tan sum cu rtsa gnyis po 'di dag dang ldan
pa bsngags so/ /rgyal pos mdun na 'don la khyod song la gang na yon tan 'di dang ldan pa'i bud med tshol cig gsungs/ rgyal rigs bram ze'i bu mo dang / /rje rigs dmangs rigs
de bzhin te/ /su la yon tan 'di yod pa'i/ /bu mo de ni 'dir 'on cig /nga yi bu 'di rigs dag dang / /rus la ngo mtshar 'dzin ma yin/ /yon tan bden pa chos kyi rnams/ /de
la 'di ni yid dga' 'o/ /zhes smras pa dang / mdun na 'don des yul kun tu song bas/ shAkya lag na be con gyi bu mo sa mtsho ma mthong nas yi ge de byin pas/ bu mo de bzhin
'dzum ste/ bram ze/ yon tan 'di dag bdag la kun tshang gis/ /des pa'i gzugs can de ni bdag gi khyim thabs so/ /gal te gzhon nu bzhed na phyi bshol ma mdzad gsungs/ /rgya
la skye bo phal dang bzhugs par gyur kyang gda'/ /zhes zer ba de bram zes rgyal po la gsol pas/ bud med 'di brdzun che bas rgyal po yid ma ches par/ zhag bdun na bu mo
thams cad 'dun

khang du shog cig gzhon nus yid du 'ong ba'i yo byad dag sbyin no zhes smras pas/ bu mo dag byung ba na ji ltar 'ongs pa bzhin yo byad dag byin pas/ de dag gis kyang gzhon
nu'i gzi brjid ma bzod par myur du song / de nas sa mtsho ma yong ba na yo byad zad de/ de 'dzum dmul te/ bdag gi nongs pa ci bgyis nas/ /bdag la thugs ngan sdang ba mdzad/
/byas pas/ gzhon nus sngon sdang min gyi khyed 'phyis pas lan no gsungs nas sor gdub srang brgya stong ri ba de sbyin no/ /de song ba na bya ra ba dag gis gzhon nu sa
mtsho ma la spyan chags te/ bka' mchid kyang cung zad bgyis so zhes smra 'o/ /de nas rgyal pos shAkya lag na be con la khyod kyi bu mo gzhon nu la byin cig gsungs pas/ des/
bdag gi rigs chos la bu mo sgyu rtsal shes pa la gtong ba lags na/ mi shes pa la ji ltar sbyin zer ba thos pas/ rgyal po yid ma dga' bar sems shing 'dug la/ gzhon nus
mthong nas/ yab ci nongs bka' stsol rigs so smras pas/ yab kyis tshul de bsnyad pa na/ gzhon nus sgyu rtsal 'gran par khas blangs pas rgyal po mnyes te sgyu rtsal 'gran par
dril bsgrags so/ /de nas shAkya gzhon nu lnga brgya tsam 'tshogs te/ ral gri'i thabs dang / 'phongs dang / gyad kyi 'dzings stangs sogs su rgyal ba de la sa mtsho ma ster
ba dam bcas pa na/ thog mar lhas sbyin byung ste/ glang po che khrid pa dang 'phrad nas phrag dog dang nga rgyal gyis kun nas bslangs te thal mo lan gcig bsnun nas bsad/
mdzes dga' bos ro de grong khyer gyi phyi rol tu bskyur

ba na/ gzhon nus zhabs kyi mthe bong gis blangs te ra ba bdun/ 'obs bdun gyi phyi rgyang grags gcig tsam gyi sar 'phangs te gshongs chen por gyur pas glang po'i gshongs zhes
grags so/ /de nas yi ge dang rtsis 'gran pas kyang gzhon nu rgyal lo/ /de nas dga' bo dang kun dga' bo gnyis kyi stobs brgal ba'i phyir drung du phyin pas/ des lag pa reg
ma thag 'gyel/ de nas lhas sbyin byung ba na/ byang chub sems dpas phyag g.yas kyis btegs te nam mkha' la bskor nas sa la bor yang lus la mi gnod par byas so/ /de nas
'phongs 'gran pa na kun dga' bos rgyang grags gnyis/ lhas sbyin gyis rgyang grags bzhi/ dga' bos rgyang grags drug be con gyis dpag tshad gnyis kyi pha rol rnams su lcags
rnga re 'ben du btsugs pas rang rang gi 'ben la phog de las pha rol tu ma son/ gzhon nus rgyang grags bcu'i pha rol tu lcags rnga gcig shing ta la bdun/ de'i pha rol tu
lcags kyi phag rgod cig rnams btsugs te/ lha khang nas mes seng ge'i za 'gram gyi gnam ru blangs nas/ phyed krung du 'dug nas bdungs nas mda' 'phangs pas/ sngar gyi 'ben
de dag thams cad phug ste sa la zug nas mi snang bar gyur te khron pa lta bu byung bas mda'i khron pa zhes grags/ gzhan yang bang dang / mchongs la sogs pa sgyu rtsal thams
cad la gzhon nu lhag nas/ shAkya lag na be con gyis sa mtsho ma phul te/ byang chub sems dpas kyang 'jig rten dang mthun par bya ba'i

phyir/ sa mtsho ma dang / grags 'dzin ma dang / ri dwags 'dzin ma rnams 'khor mang po dang bcas khab tu bzhes pa'i tshul mdzad de/ dgung lo nyer dgu'i bar du de dag dang rtse
dga' la yongs su spyad do/ /de nas byang chub sems dpa' dam bca' dus las mi 'da' yang sangs rgyas kyis bskul ba chos nyid yin pas/ sangs rgyas kyis byin gyis brlabs pa'i
sil snyan gyi sgra las/ sdug bsngal brgyas gang sems can mthong nas ni/ /'gro ba'i mgon dang skyabs dang gnas gyur cing / /phan byed mgon dang dpung gnyen gyur cig ces/
/khyod kyis sngon gyi smon lam de skad btab/ /dge ba dpa' bo sngon gyi spyod pa dang / /'gro phan bya zhes smon lam dran par byos/ /'di ni khyod kyi tshad dang dus yin
gyi/ /drang srong mchog rab khyim nas 'byung bar byos/ /zhes sogs kyis bskul cing / btsun mo dag gi rol mo'i sgra las kyang / /srid gsum dga' dang nad kyi sdug bsngal 'bar/
/'chi med rab 'bar 'di ni mgon med pa/ /srid las 'byung la 'gro ba rtag tu rmongs/ /bum par chud pa'i bung ba 'khor ba bzhin/ /srid gsum mi rtag ston ka'i sprin dang 'dra/
/'gro ba'i skye 'chi gar la blta dang mtshungs/ /skyes bu'i tshe srog nam mkha'i glog 'dra ste/ /ri gzar 'bab chu lta bu myur 'gyogs 'gro/ /zhes sogs nas/ sngon gyi
spyod de rjes su dran gyis la/ /gti mug rab rib mun pas bsgribs pa yi/ /'gro la shes rab dam pa 'od bzang ba/ /chos mig dri med nyon mongs med pa byin/ /zhes pa'i sgra byung
bas/ byang chub sems dpa' yang rgyags pa'i

sems spangs te/ byang chub tu sems btang / de bzhin du lha'i bu 'bum phrag sum cu rtsa gnyis kyis kyang tshigs su bcad pas bskul cing / de'i tshe rgyal po'i rmi lam du byang
chub sems dpa' rab tu byung ba rmis pas/ de yid chags pa'i phyir/ dpyid bsil/ dbyar ran/ dgun dro ba'i khang bzang gsum byas pa'i tshe/ gzhon nu sus kyang ma tshor bar
mngon par 'byung du 'ong ngo zhes pa'i sgra dpag tshad gsum gyi bar du byung zhing / ltas mkhan rnams kyis kyang gzhon nu bkra shis kyi sgo nas mngon par 'byung bar 'gyur
ro zhes lung bstan pas/ rgyal pos sgo 'phar chen po sgra dpag tshad du grags pa'i mi lnga brgyas 'byed cing gcod pa byas so/ /de nas byang chub sems dpa' skyed mos tshal
du 'byon par dgongs te/ 'dun pa la shing rta sbyor cig gsungs pas/ 'dun pas kyang rgyal po la gsol pas/ rgyal pos gzhon nus yid du mi 'ong ba mi mthong bar bya ba'i phyir
phyogs thams cad nyams dga' bar byas so/ /de nas byang chub sems dpa' shar sgo nas thon pa dang / nyid kyi mthus lha'i sprul pas rgas pa'i sdug bsngal gyis nyen pa'i mi
zhig 'dug pa gzigs te/ 'dun pa la/ kha lo bsgyur ba mi rid nyam chung ba/ /sha khrag skam la rus lpags nyi tshe'i dkris/ /mgo dkar so rnal lus ni rab skem la/ /'khar ba
brten zhing mi bde 'khyor 'gro su/ /zhes gsungs pas/ 'dun pas/ lha/ mi 'di rgas pas zil gyis non pa ste/ /dbang po nyams shing sdug bsngal brtson stobs nyams/ /gnyen gyi
skye bos brnyas shing

mgon med gyur/ /don bgyid mi nus nags khrod shing ltar bor/ /zhes gsol pas/ yang byang chub sems dpas/ 'di ni 'di yi rigs kyi chos yin no/ /'on te 'gro ba 'di kun la yang 'byung
/ /tshig 'di yang dag ji bzhin myur du smros/ /thos nas de don 'dir ni tshul bzhin bsam/ /gsungs pas/ des/ lha/ 'di ni rigs chos yul 'khor chos ma lags/ /dar la babs
pa'i skye bo rgas pas 'joms/ /khyod kyi yab yum nye du gnyen tshogs kyang / /rgas las ma thar gzhan du 'gro thabs med/ /ces smras pa na/ byang chub sems dpas/ kha lo bsgyur
ba byis pa mi mkhas 'gro/ /gzhon pas rgyags spyos blo ngan rgas ma mthong / /nga ni slar 'gro shing rta myur du sgyur/ /nga ni rgas 'gyur rtse dgas ci zhig bya/ /zhes
gsungs nas nang du log go /yang lho sgor byon pas na ba'i sdug bsngal gzigs te/ kha lo bsgyur ba nyam chung lus mdog ngan/ /dbang po kun nyams dbugs dbyung rab tu dka'/
/yan lag kun skam lto dkrugs nyam thag gyur/ /rang gi gcin stug smad pa'i nang 'dug su/ /gsungs pas/ des/ lha/ mi 'di shin tu nad kyis btab pa ste/ /nad kyi nyer 'tshe 'chi
bas 'gum la thug /gzi brjid ma mchis stobs kyang rnam par nyams/ /mgon skyabs gling dang dpung gnyen ma mchis lags/ /zhes smras so/ /byang chub sems dpas/ nad med pa
yang rmi lam rtsed dang mtshungs/ /nad kyi 'jigs pa 'di ltar mi zad pa'i/ /gnas 'di mthong nas skyes bu mkhas pa rnams/ /rtse dga' sdug pa'i 'du shes ji ltar

skyed/ /zhes gsungs/ nub tu shi ba gzigs nas/ kha lo bsgyur ba mi 'di khyor btegs nas/ /mi dag skra bshig mgo la sas 'thor zhing / /sna tshogs gang dag brjod cing brang brdungs
pas/ /mdun nas bskor te khyer ba 'di su zhig /gsungs pa dang / yang des/ lha/ mi 'di 'dzam bu'i gling du gum pa ste/ /pha ma 'chi 'brangs bu rnams slar mi mthong / /longs
spyod khyim dang mdza' bshes gnyen tshogs rnams/ /spangs nas 'jig rten pha rol dag tu 'gro/ /zhes zer ba la/ byang chub sems dpas/ rga bas gnod 'gyur gzhon yang ci
mi rung / /nad kyis gnod 'gyur nad med ci mi rung / /ring du mi gnas gson yang ci mi rung / /dga' ba la chags mkhas kyang ci mi rung / /da lta na rga 'chi ba med gyur kyang
/ /sdug bsngal chen po phung po lnga 'dzin na/ /na rga 'chi ba rtag 'brangs smos ci dgos/ /slar log rab tu thar bar bya ba bsam/ /zhes gsungs shing / yang byang sgor dge
slong gzigs te/ kha lo bsgyur ba sems zhi rab zhi zhing / /mig phab 'gro la gnya' shing gang tsam lta/ /ngur smrig gos gyon spyod ni lhung bzed thogs/ /mi rgod ma khengs
skyes bu 'di su zhig /gsungs pa na/ des smras pa/ lha/ mi 'di dge slong zhes ni bgyid pa lags/ /'dod pa'i dga' ba spangs shing dul bar spyod/ /bdag nyid rab tu byung zhing
