zhi ba 'tshol/ /chags sdang bral ba bsod snyoms spyod cing rgyu/ /zer ba dang / byang chub sems dpas/ dge ba legs smras 'di ni nga 'dod de/ /rab byung mkhas pa rnams
kyis rtag tu bsngags/ /de ni bdag

dang sems can gzhan la'ang phan/ /'tsho bde nyams mthun 'chi med 'bras bur 'gyur/ /gsungs shing / de nas byang chub sems dpas nang du log ste bzhugs so/ /rgyal pos de dag mthong
thos pas/ bsrung ba'i phyir ra ba dang / 'obs dang / sgo brtan po bcu drug grong khyer gyi bzhi mdor srung ba'i mi bzhag btsun mo rnams glu dbyangs dang rtse dga' byed
du bcug de'i tshe byang chub sems dpa' khab nas gshegs pa'i ltas su bya skad mi 'byin/ padma rnyid/ shing la me tog mi 'char/ gling bu dang pi waM sogs rgyud chad/ rdza
rnga brdungs kyang skad med par gyur te/ de dag mthong bas rgyal po sems khong du chud cing / sa mtsho ma la sa g.yo ba sogs rmis/ byang chub sems dpa'i rmi lam du/ rkang
lag gis rgya mtsho dkrugs/ sa mal char byas/ ri rab sngas su bcug 'od kyis mun pa gsal/ gdugs gcig gis 'jig rten gsum khyab pa la sogs pa rmis so/ /de nas byang chub
sems dpas yab kyis ma gnang bar rab tu 'byung bar mi rigs dgongs nas yab kyi drung du song ste/ bdag mngon par 'byung ba'i dus la babs kyi bgegs dang mi dges par ma mdzod
cig gsungs pas/ yab kyis/ khyod kyis 'dod pa'i mchog sbyin gyi khab tu bzhugs shig gsungs pa dang / byang chub sems dpa'i rga nad 'chi rgud bzhi med pa 'tshal lo gsungs
pas/ yab kyis de sbyin pa'i thabs med/ gzhan gang 'dod pa slongs shig zer ba la/ yang byang chub sems dpas/ rga nad 'chi ba'i 'jigs dang rgud par mi 'gyur ba/ /lha gcig gal
te mchog

[A: 31b ]bzhi 'di dag mi stsol na/ /gzhan yang mchog gcig gsol gyi rgyal po gsan du gsol/ /'di nas shi 'phos nying mtshams sbyor bar mi 'gyur mdzod/ /ces gsungs pas/ rgyal
po'i dgongs pa la de ni bdag gis sbyin par mi nus/ 'di btsas pa'i tshe yang srid pa tha ma bar bya'o zhes smra la/ bram ze rnams kyis kyang mngon par 'byung ba lung bstan
pas/ 'di nges par 'gro snyam nas skad chung ngus khyed kyi bsam pa rdzogs par gyur cig ces smras so/ /rgyal pos don de shAkya rnams la bsnyad pas/ bsrung bar rigs zhes thams
cad bgros te bsgo bzhir shAkya gzhon nu lnga brgyar re/ shing rta lnga brgya re/ dpung bu chung lnga brgya re dang bcas bkod/ shAkya rgan rabs rnams lam gyi bzhi mdo
dang / sum mdor 'khod/ rgyal po'ang mel tshe byed do/ /de'i tshe gnod sbyin rnams dang / 'phrog ma'i bu rnams dang / sum cu rtsa gsum pa rnams mchod pa'i las byed do/ /lha'i
bu chos spyod la sogs pas btsun mo'i 'khor mi sdug par bsgyur ba de la gzigs pas dur khrod kyi 'du shes skyes te/ e ma skye dgu rnams ni sdug bsngal gyur/ /srin mo'i
tshogs la dga' ba ji ltar rnyed/ /'dod pa yon tan med la yon tan 'dzin/ /gti mug mun pas rab bsgribs blo gros ngan/ /dper na bya ni bya rgyar chud pa bzhin/ /nam yang 'byung
ba rnyed par 'gyur yin/ /zhes gsungs te mi sdug par sgom mo/ /de nas byang chub sems dpas smon lam 'di skad btab ste/ sems can thams cad la chos kyi sgra bsgrag par
bya'o/ /ma rig pa'i mun pa gsal bar bya'o/ /nga rgyal gyi ri bo bsnyil bar bya'o/ /srid pa'i mdud pa dgrol bar bya'o/ /zhes dgongs te nam phyed kyi dus khang bzang gi steng
du song ste/ sangs rgyas thams cad la phyag btsal nas bltas pas/ brgya byin dang rgyal po chen po bzhi dang / nyi zla gnyis kyang phyag 'tshal zhing 'dug pa dang / skar
ma rgyal shar ba yang mthong ste/ 'dun pa la/ nga yi bkra shis 'di ni don kun 'grub/ /do nub gdon mi za ba don 'grub kyi/ /'dun pa phyi bshol ma byed la gor du/ /rta rgyal
rgyan gyis brgyan pa nga la byin/ /gsungs pa na/ 'dun pas gang du bzhud zhus pas/ mngon par 'byung ngo gsungs/ 'dun pas yang yang ldog kyang ma gnang bar/ dus ma lags
so zhus pas/ sems can rnams kyi don ni 'tshol ba na/ /byang chub rga shi med pa'i gnas thob nas/ /'gro ba sgrol zhes nga yis yun ring nas/ /smon lam btab pa de yi dus la
bab/ /ces gsungs shing / lha'i bu yang dag bskul ba pos kyang / da ni mngon par 'byung ba'i dus la bab bo zhes bskul/ lha'i bu kha cig gis srung ma rnams myos par byas/
de nas brgya byin gyis bkra shis kyi sgo phyes/ rta lnga ldan la chibs la rgyal chen bzhis btegs te nam mkha' la byon pas/ tshangs pa dang brgya byin gyis lam bstan/ 'od
kyis mun pa gsal/ mchod pa dang / rol mo dang bcas te gyad kyi yul 'das nas mchod rten rnam dag gi drung du phyin te/ rta dang rgyan 'dun pa la byin la/ 'di dag khyer la
ser skyar songs shig gsungs/ 'dun pas bdag la chad pas gcod du mchi'o byas pas/ nga la byams

pa bzhin khyod la byams par 'gyur gyi ma 'jigs shig gsungs pa bzhin des kyang log ste/ bkod pa'i gtam rnams rgyal po sogs la smras pas thams cad ngo mtshar skyes/ byang chub
sems dpa'i mthus mya ngan yang med par gyur to/ /der mchod rten zhig brtsigs pas 'dun pa slar log gi mchod rten zhes grags/ de nas mchod rten rnam dag gi drung du nyid
kyi dbu skra nyid kyis bzhar ba lha rnams kyis gdan drangs te mchod rten brtsigs pas gtsug phud kyi mchod rten du grags/ der rab byung gi tshul dang mthun pa'i gos shig rnyed
na rung snyam pa dang / gnas gtsang ma'i lha rngon pa'i gzugs su sprul pas na bza' ngur smrig phul ba bzhes te/ sa der mchod rten brtsigs pas ngur smrig blangs pa'i
mchod rten zhes kyang grags/ de ltar gtsug phud bcad/ ngur smrig bgos te rang byung gi rab tu byung bar mdzad pas don grub rab tu byung ngo zhes pa'i sgra 'og min gyi bar
du grags so/ /de nas bram ze rigs ldan gyi gnas su bsod snyoms la byon nas yangs pa can na sgyu rtsal shes kyi bu ring 'phur slob ma mang po la ci yang med kyi skye mched
ston pa nyan pas tshegs med du mkhyen nas de bas lhag pa'i chos shig 'tshol snyam du dgongs te/ ma ga dha dang / rgyal po'i khab kyi grong khyer sogs su byon/ rgyal po
gzugs can snying po grong khyer ba dang bcas pa dad par byas/ rgyal po'i khab de nyid na rengs byed kyi bu lhag spyod slob ma mang po la srid rtse'i sems ston pa'i sar phyin
te bslabs pas khong du chud de/ 'dis ni myang 'das su 'gyur ba ma yin no zhes sun

phyungs te song ngo / /de'i lnga sde yang byang chub sems dpa'i rjes su 'brangs so/ /de nas brtul zhugs ngan pas dag pa sun phyung ba'i ri chu bo ne ranydza na'i 'gram du til
'bru gcig dang 'bras 'bru gcig rgya shug 'bru gcig la brten nas lo drug tu dka' ba spyad de mkha' khyab kyi ting nge 'dzin la zhugs pas/ lha'i bu khag cig gis lha mo sgyu
'phrul ma la gzhon nu shi'o zhes smras pas lha mos bltar 'ongs te/ byang chub sems dpa'i lus skam pa shi ba dang 'dra ba mthong bas/ nga'i skye ba'i tha ma 'di'o zhes
pa'i dam bca' yang ma rdzogs/ bram ze dag gis lung bstan kyang mi bden no zer zhing smre sngags 'don pa na/ byang chub sems dpas/ nyi zla skar tshogs sa la lhung 'gyur srid/
/so so skye bo yin yang nga mi 'chi/ /de phyir 'di la mya ngan khyod ma byed/ /ring por mi thogs byang chub sangs rgyas mthong / /zhes gsungs pas dga' ste rang gnas
su song ngo / /de'i tshe ba glang rdzi rnams kyis rna bar shing bal bcug nas snar 'byin pa la sogs pa byed cing / bdud kyis glags btsal kyang ma rnyed do/ /de nas dka' thub
kyis grol bar 'dzin pa dgag pa'i phyir kha zas rags pa gsol bas/ lnga sdes 'di ni lhod pa/ mang du bza' ba/ dka' thub las nyams pa'o zhes brjod cing ma dad par gzhan du
song ngo / /der lha rnams kyis gos ngur smrig phul ba bzhes te/ de'i tshe byang chub sems dpa' lus mdzes pas dge sbyong mdzes pa zhes grags/ de nas zhing pa'i bu mo legs
skyes mas ba stong gi zho'i nying khu phul ba de dag gsol bas mtshan dpe mchog tu gsal zhing 'od

'dom gang gis brgyan par gyur to/ /de nas byang chub sems dpas bdud las rgyal bar bya ba'i phyir byang chub kyi shing drung du gshegs pas/ lha'i mthus rlung dang char gyi lam
chags shing chag chag btab/ ri dang shing dang byis pa btsas ma thag pa thams cad kyang mgo de phyogs su ston cing / stong gsum gyi bdag po tshangs pas rang gi 'khor rnams
la do nub byang chub sems dpa' byang chub kyi snying por gshegs kyi mchod pa'i las gyis shig ces bsgos nas mchod pa'i bkod pa bsam gyis mi khyab pa sprul lo/ /byang
chub sems dpas 'od bkye ba de phog pa'i sems can thams cad kyi nyon mongs pa dang sdug bsngal thams cad zhi zhing snod kyi skyon thams cad sbyangs so/ /de nas rtswa 'tshong
bkra shis la/ bkra shis rtswa 'di nga la myur du byin/ /de ring nga la rtswa yis don chen 'gyur/ /dpung dang bcas pa'i bdud rnams bcom nas su/ /byang chub dam pa zhi ba
'thob par 'gyur/ /zhes gsungs pa dang / des kyang rtswa ku sha sngo 'jam yid du 'ong ba phul ba bzhes te/ byang chub kyi shing la lan gsum bskor te/ rtswa'i rtse mo nang
du bstan/ rtsa ba phyir bstan pa la zhal shar du phyogs par bzhugs te/ sku drang por bsrangs nas dgongs pa mngon du bzhag ste/ stan 'dir bdag gi lus 'di skam gyur tam/
/sha rus lpags pa'i tshogs rnams zhig kyang rung / /bskal mang rnyed dka'i byang chub ma thob bar/ /stan 'di la ni lus bskyod mi bya'o/ /zhes yid dam brtan po mdzad pas/
lha rnams kyang byang chub sems dpa' bsrung ba'i phyir phyogs bcur 'khod do/ /de nas

byang chub sems dpas smin mtshams nas 'od bkyes pas/ zhing khams dpag med snang bar byas nas byang chub sems dpa' mang po 'dus nas mchod pa byed cing / slar yang bdud 'joms
pa zhes bya ba'i 'od zer bkyes pas bdud gnas thams cad snang zhing g.yos/ slar mog mog por byas te/ sems can shin tu dag pa bskal mang spyod spyad pa/ /zas gtsang sras pos
rgyal srid dag ni rab spangs te/ /phan byed de ni bdud rtsi mngon par 'dod pas byung / /byang chub shing drung 'ongs kyi de ring bsgrin par gyis/ /zhes pa la sogs pa'i
sgra yang byung zhing / bdud sdig can la rang gnas su mun pas khyab pa sogs rmis te/ rang gi 'khor rnams la sbran/ bu ded dpon gyis ldog kyang ma ldog par/ gnod sbyin grul
bum lto 'phye chen po'i gzugs/ /srin po yid dang sha za'i gzugs dang bcas/ /'jig rten mi sdug drag gzugs ji snyed pa/ /thams cad sgyu yis der ni sprul pa bya/ /zhes pa
ltar sgyu ma lta bu'i blo can ma yin pa rnams mthong ba tsam gyis snying 'gas par 'gyur ba/ kha bzhin dmar la lus po ser ba dang / /lus po dmar la kha bzhin ser ba dang
/ /mgo gcig mgo gnyis mgo gsum ldan pa dang / /mgo stong bye ba'i bar ldan rab tu mang / /zhes pa ltar gyi lus can mtshon cha sna tshogs 'dzin pa'i dmag sa ya sum cu lhags
te/ g.yas phyogs nas byang chub sems dpa' la dga' ba rnams kyis bzlog g.yon nas mi dga' rnams kyis bskul te/ phyogs rnams kun nas ri yi phreng ba dang / /mkha'

las brag dang mtshon gyi char pa dang / /rdo rje 'bar ba'i tshogs char 'bab pa yis/ /shAkya'i bu de thal bar brlag par bya/ /zhes zer zhing mtshon cha sogs char bzhin du bar
mtshams med par babs kyang / shAkya'i sras pos chos rnams rten 'byung ba/ /dngos po med pa'i ngo bo nyid du rtogs/ /nam mkha' lta bu'i sems dang rab tu ldan/ /dpung bcas
g.yo sgyu mthong yang nyes pa med/ /ces pa ltar byang chub sems dpa'i ting nge 'dzin gyi mthus gnod pa med cing mtshon cha rnams me tog gi char du gyur pa dang / bdud na
re/ khyod kyi bsod nams de tsam gyis thar pa ga la thob zer ba la/ byang chub sems dpas/ khyod kyis gtan pa med pa'i mchod sbyin gcig byas pas 'dod pa'i dbang phyug tu
gyur pa yin/ ngas gtan pa med pa'i mchod sbyin du ma byas so zhes gsungs pas/ bdud kyis/ sngon chad kho bo'i mchod sbyin kha na ma tho med/ /gtan pa med pa byas pa'i dpang
du khyod 'dir yod/ /'dir ni khyod la dpang po gang yang yod min pas/ /smras kyang phan pa ci yod khyod ni pham par gyur/ /zer ba na/ byang chub sems dpas phyag g.yas pa
sa la brdabs te/ sa 'di 'gro ba kun gyi gnas yin te/ /rgyu dang mi rgyu snyoms shing nye 'khon med/ /'di ni bdag gi dpang ste bdag brdzun med/ /'di la khyod kyi dpang byos
shig ces gsungs pas/ sa rnam pa drug tu g.yos pa'i gseb nas sa'i lha mo lus phyed phyung nas thal mo sbyar te/ skyes bu chen po de bzhin no/ /khyod kyis ji skad smras
pa de bzhin te/ 'di ni bdag la mngon sum mo/ /'on kyang bcom

ldan 'das nyid lha dang bcas pa'i 'jig rten thams cad kyi dpang du gyur pa lags so/ /zhes smras te mi snang bar gyur to/ /de nas/ g.yon can dpung bcas sa sgra de thos pas/
/nags su seng ge'i sgra bsgrags was thos dang / /bya rog rdo 'phangs mdo la byer ba bzhin/ /dngangs skrag snying gas thams cad rab tu byer/ /zhes pa ltar phyogs su byer ro/
/de nas sdig chen yid ma dga' nas bdud kyi bu mo rnams nyams sad du btang bas/ de dag gis kyang byang chub sems dpa'i mdun du phyin te g.yo sgyu sna tshogs bstan kyang
bslu ma nus pas sdig can shin tu yid ma dga' ba na/ shing gi lha dpal ldan sogs kyis/ khyod ni dgung zla yar gyi ngo ltar mdzes pa'o/ /zhes sogs kyis byang chub sems dpa'
la bstod pa dang / gnas gtsang ma'i rigs kyi lha dag gis/ sdig can khyod ni glang rgan 'dam du bying ba ltar nyam chung ba'o/ /zhes sogs kyis smad cing bzlogs kyang bdud
kyi dmag grangs ji snyed pa yod do cog sbran te song nas mtshon char sna tshogs 'phangs shing cho 'phrul sna tshogs bstan kyang glags ma rnyed pa thams cad 'thor nas zhag
bdun du ma 'phrad/ de'i tshe bdud mang pos byang chub tu sems bskyed do/ /de nas byang chub sems dpas nam gyi stod la bsam gtan bzhi mngon du mdzad/ gung la mngon shes
rnams bskyed nas/ nam gyi cha smad skya rengs 'char kha'i tshe zag med kyi ye shes mngon du byas te mngon par rdzogs par sangs rgyas nas shing ta la bdun tsam du nam mkha'
la 'phags te/ lam gyi rgyud ni chad do zhes sogs ched du brjod/ lha rnams kyis me tog pus nub tsam du

gtor te mchod/ lha'i bu mo rnams kyis bstod/ 'od kyis 'jig rten snang bar byas/ sa rnam pa drug tu g.yos/ phyogs bcu'i sangs rgyas rnams kyis kyang / bdag cag ji ltar sangs
rgyas pa/ /de lta kho nar khyod sangs rgyas/ /dper na mar dang mar nyid kyi/ /nying khu mtshungs pa bzhin du gyur/ /ces gsungs shing / nyid kyi gsung gis kyang / bsod nams
rnam smin bde zhing sdug bsngal sel/ /bsod nams ldan pa'i mi yi bsam pa 'grub/ /bdud bcom nas ni byang chub mngon sangs rgyas/ /mya ngan 'das shing bsil ba'i dngos po
thob/ /ces ched du brjod do/ /zhag bdun phrag dang po la skyil krung ma bshig par byang chub kyi zhing la gzigs/ gnyis pa la stong gsum ring du 'chag gsum pa la byang chub
kyi snying po la spyan mi 'dzum par gzigs/ bzhi pa la shar nub kyi bar du rgyang mi ring bar 'chag bdud kyis mya ngan las 'da' bar zhus kyang gdul bya'i don ma zin gyi
bar du mya ngan las mi 'da' bar zhal gyis bzhes/ bdud kyi bu mo dga' ma sogs bslur byung ba na rgan mor mdzad/ bdun phrag lnga pa la klu btang bzung ba'i gnas su bzhugs so/
/drug pa la shing nya gro dha skyong du bzhud de/ kun tu rgyu rnams la/ chos thos pa dang mthong ba dang / /dben par dga' ba bde ba yin/ /srog chags 'byung po rnams la
gdams/ /gnod pa mi byed 'jig rten bde/ /zhes sogs gsungs/ bdun pa la shing sgrol rgyu'i drung du bzhugs te/ tshong pa ga gon dang bzang pos/ sbrang rtsi

dang / skyo ma dang / bu ram shing bshus pa dag phul ba na/ sngon gyi sangs rgyas rnams kyis snod ji lta bur bzhes dgongs pa dang / rgyal chen bzhis gser la sogs pa'i lhung
bzed phul ba ma bzhes/ rnam sras la rdo'i lhung bzed bzhi yod pa rgyal chen bzhis re re bzung rin po ches bkang nas phul bas/ bde bar gshegs la lhung bzed phul cig dang
/ /khyod ni theg pa mchog gi snod du 'gyur/ /nga 'dra dag la lhung bzed phul ba yis/ /dran dang blo gros nam yang nyams mi 'gyur/ /zhes gsungs te bzhes nas bzhi cha gcig
tu byin gyis brlabs pa blangs so/ /de nas ga gon dang bzang pos ba stong gi spris ma bzhos nas rin po che'i gzhong par blugs te phul ba gsol nas gzhong pa bor ba tshangs
pas khyer/ de nas ston pas/ lha yi bkra shis don grub cing / /phyogs rnams bkra shis byed pa des/ /khyod kyi don rnams 'grub gyur cig /thams cad myur du mthun par shog /ces
sogs kyis shis pa brjod de/ sbrang rtsi 'byung ba zhes bya ba'i rgyal bar lung bstan/ de nas ston pa thugs las chung ngur bzhugs te/ zab zhi spros bral 'od gsal 'dus ma
byas/ /bdud rtsi lta bu'i chos shig kho bos rnyed/ /su la bstan kyang go bar mi nus pas/ /mi smra nags 'dabs gnas par bya ba snyam/ /zhes dgongs shing / 'jig rten kun la
snying brtse mtha' yas nga / /gzhan gyis gsol ba btab la nga mi ston/ /skye bo 'di dag tshangs la dad pa ste/ /de yis gsol ba btab na 'khor lo bskor/ /snyam du dgongs te
'od zer bkye bas/ stong

gsum gyi bdag po tshangs pa gtsug phud can gyis grogs sbran te tshangs pa 'bum phrag drug cu rtsa brgyad dang bcas pas thal mo sbyar te/ ye shes chen mo mchog gi dkyil 'khor
bsgrubs nas ni/ /phyogs bcu dag tu 'od zer rnam par bkye mdzad de/ /ye shes zer gyis mi yi padma kha 'byed pa/ smra ba'i nyi ma de ring ci slad btang snyoms bzhugs/ /zhes
sogs kyis bskul nas/ cang mi gsungs bar gnang ngo / /slar yang chos la gus pa bskyed pa'i phyir yang yang gsol ba btab pa'i slad du/ thugs las chung ngu la gzhol bar mdzad
do/ /de tshangs pas shes nas brgya byin sbran nas/ brgya byin gyis/ zla ba nya ba gza' las thar ba ltar/ /khyod kyi thugs ni shin tu rnam par grol/ /g.yul las rnam par
rgyal ba bzhengs su gsol/ /'jig rten mun par shes rab 'od dbyung gsol/ /zhes pa dang / tshangs pas kyang kun tu 'tshal bar gyur pa mchis lags kyi/ thub pa khyod kyis chos
ni bstan du gsol/ /zhes gsol ba btab pa na/ ston pas/ skye dgu 'dod pa rnams kyis bcings/ /rgyun gyis rab tu bdas pa yin/ /ngas ni tshegs chen po yis rnyed/ /de lta bas
na bstan mi phan/ /zhes gsungs pa na/ slar yang tshangs pas gser gyi 'khor lo rtsibs stong dang ldan pa phul te/ ma ga dha yi yul 'dir sngon chad chos/ /ma dag dri mas
rjes su 'brel ba byung / /bdud rtsi'i sgo mo dbye bar mdzod cig chos/ /rdul bral dri ma med pa bstan du gsol/ /zhes gsol ba btab pas/ bcom ldan 'das kyis 'jig

rten la gzigs nas ma nges pa dang / log par nges pa dang / yang dag par nges pa ste gsum du gnas pa las/ ma nges pa la gzigs te/ tshangs pa ma ga dha yi sems can gang su dag
/skal bar ldan zhing rigs dang ldan gyur pa/ /mi tshe 'du shes rtag tu chos nyan pa/ /de dag la ni bdud rtsi'i sgo dbye 'o/ /zhes zhal gyis bzhes so/ /de nas byang chub
kyi shing gi lha bzhis/ chos kyi 'khor lo gang du bskor zhus pas/ wa ra na sir bskor gsungs pa na/ de dag gis/ de ni skye bo nyung zhing grib ma chung bas gzhan du rigs
so zer ba la/ ston pas/ bzhin bzang dag de skad ma zer cig wa ra na si de ni sngon gyi drang srong rnams kyi gnas sa ste/ lha dang klu yis mngon bstod rtag tu chos ni rnam
par gzhol/ /ngas ni sngon chad sangs rgyas bye ba dgu bcu rtsa gcig bsten/ /de dag drang srong zhes bya nags mchog dam pa der ni 'khor lo bskor/ /zhes gsungs shing de nas
su la chos bstan dgongs pa dang / lhag spyod 'das nas zhag bdun dang / ring 'phur 'das nas zhag gsum lon par dgongs nas lnga sde la gzigs pas/ de dag skal ba dang ldan
par mkhyen nas gsal ldan du byon pas/ 'tsho ba pa nyer 'gro dang 'phrad de/ khyod dbang po ni gsal/ pags pa ni dag na/ su las tshangs par spyad zhus pa na/ ston pas/ nga
la slob dpon gang yang med/ /nga dang 'dra ba yod ma yin/ /nga ni gcig pu rdzogs sangs rgyas/ /bsil 'gyur zag pa med pa yin/ /gsungs pas/ de na re/ dgra bcom par zhal gyis
'che 'am zer ba dang /

ston pas/ nga ni 'jig rten dgra bcom pa/ /nga ni ston pa bla na med/ /lha dang lha min dri zar bcas/ /nga yi do zla'i gang zag med/ /gsungs pas/ des rgyal bar zhal gyis bzhes
sam zer ba la/ ston pas/ gang dag zag pa zad brnyes pa/ /nga 'dra rgyal bar shes par bya/ /nga ni sdig pa'i chos las rgyal/ /de bas nyer 'gro nga rgyal yin/ /gsungs pas/
des/ 'o na gar bzhud zer/ nga ni wa ra na sir 'gro/ /grong khyer gsal ldan song nas ni/ /long ba lta bu'i 'jig rten la/ /mtshungs pa med pa'i 'od bya'o/ /zhes gsungs pas
de bzhin du 'gyur ro zer te lho phyogs su song / ston pas byang phyogs su steng rgyas sogs nas rim gyis gshegs/ ganggA'i 'gram du byon te gru la sgrol gsungs pas mnyan
pas gru tshas dgos zer ba la/ nga la gru tshas med gsungs nas nam mkha' la 'phur nas gshegs pas/ mnyan pa dag 'gyod pa skyes shing ngo mtshar nas rgyal po la zhus pas/ rgyal
po gzugs can snying pos de phyin chad rab byung la gru tshas mi len par byas so/ /de nas 'khor mo 'jig tu gshegs pa lnga sdes rgyang ring po nas mthong nas/ dge sbyong
go'u ta ma lhod pa mang du bza' ba/ spong ba las nyams pa de 'ong gi 'di la sngon du ldang ba dang / phyag kyang mi bya/ stan lhag ma 'di la 'dug na 'dug tu chug zer ba'i
'og khrims bcas te/ kun shes kyi sems kyis khas ma blangs/ de nas ston pas byon pas lnga sde'i 'og khrims de rang zhig tu song ste/ stan las langs te/ la las bsu/ la
las gdan btings/ la las zhabs bkru ba'i chu

bshams nas khyed legs par byon nam/ stan 'di la bzhugs su gsol zhes zhus pa na/ ston pas stan la bzhugs nas lnga sde dga' mgu bar bya ba'i gtam mang po mdzad pa na/ lnga sdes
tshe dang ldan pa gau ta ma/ dbang po ni gsal/ pags pa ni yongs su dag na/ ye shes mthong ba'i khyad par mngon du mdzad dam zhes zer ba la/ ston pas/ dge slong dag de
bzhin gshegs pa la tshe dang ldan pa zhes ma zer zhig khyed rang dag yun ring por mi bde bar 'gyur ro/ /ngas ni bdud rtsi thob bo/ /sangs rgyas so/ /thams cad mkhyen pa'o/
/sngar khyod rnams kyis 'og khrims 'di ltar ma bcas sam/ dge slong dag ngas khyod rnams la chos bshad kyi tshur shog nyon cig nan tan gyis shig rna ba lhogs shig dang ngas
gdams shing rjes su bstan no/ /zhes gsungs pas de'i mod la/ de dag gi mu stegs kyi rtags rnams med par gyur te/ dge slong bsnyen par rdzogs nas lo brgya lon pa lta bur
gyur te/ de dag gis kyang nyes pa bshags te gus pa yang bskyed do/ /de nas ston pas/ sngon gyi sangs rgyas rnams gang du bzhugs nas chos kyi 'khor lo bskor snyams pa dang
/ sa phyogs der rin po che'i khri stong byung bar gyur to/ /der khri snga ma gsum la bskor ba mdzad de/ bzhi pa la skyil mo krung bcas te bzhugs so/ /lnga sdes kyang ston
pa'i zhabs la phyag btsal te spyan sngar 'khod do/ /de'i tshe bcom ldan 'das kyi sku las 'od zer bkyes nas 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad khyab par byas te/ 'od de las/
de ni thugs dam bstan pa ste/ /wa ra

na si ri dwags nags/ /gshegs te 'khor lo bla med pa/ /shin tu rmad byung dpal ldan bskor/ /rgyal las bskal pa phrag khrig bsgrubs/ /chos de nyan par gang 'dod pa/ /de ni rings
par la gor du/ /chos nyan pa yi phyir shog cig /ces bya ba la sogs pa'i sgra grags pas/ byang chub sems dpa' dang / lha'i 'khor dpag tu med pa 'dus so/ /de nas ston pa
'dis 'khor gyi thog ma kun shes kau dri nya/ rta thul/ rlangs pa/ ming chen/ bzang ldan ste/ lnga sde bzang po la/ dge slong dag mtha' gnyis po 'di dag ni rab tu byung
bas 'jug par bya ba ma yin te/ 'dod pa bsod nyams kyi mtha' dang / ngal zhing dub pa'i mtha' 'o/ /de bas na mtha' gnyis spangs nas dbu ma'i lam gyis de bzhin gshegs pa chos
ston to/ /de ni 'di lta ste 'phags pa'i lam yan lag brgyad do/ /dge slong dag bzhi po 'di dag ni 'phags pa'i bden pa bzhi ste/ gang zhe na/ sdug bsngal dang / kun 'byung
dang / 'gog pa dang / lam mo zhes sogs lan dang pos bden pa bzhi'i ngo bo dang / yang dge slong dag sdug bsngal yongs su shes par bya'o/ /kun 'byung spang bar bya'o zhes
sogs lan gnyis pas bden pa bzhi'i bya ba dang / yang dge slong dag sdug bsngal shes so kun 'byung spangs so zhes sogs lan gsum pas bden pa bzhi mthar phyin par bzlas pa
ste/ de ltar rnam pa bcu gnyis dang ldan pa'i chos kyi 'khor lo bskor bas lan gnyis pa la kun shes kyis dgra bcom pa thob/ gzhan bzhi la mthong lam skyes/ gsum pa'i tshe
bzhi pos kyang dgra bcom pa thob bo/ /'o na lnga sde 'di dag ston

pa 'di'i 'khor gyi thog mar 'byung ba'i rgyu mtshan ci zhe na/ ston pa 'di sngon rgyal po byams pa'i stobs su gyur pa na/ de'i tshe gnod sbyin mig dmar zhes pa lngas nyin re
la sems can du ma srog gcod cing bza' bar byed pa las/ rgyal po 'di 'khrungs pa'i stobs kyis gnod sbyin de dag la sems can gyi srog gcod pa'i skal ba med par gyur nas lus
shin tu rid par gyur nas nags gseb cig tu gnas pa las/ rgyal po des nags su byon pa dang / de dag mthong nas lus 'di lta bur gyur pa ci yin gsungs pas/ gnod sbyin rnams
kyis gong gi rgyu mtshan zhus pa na/ rgyal po snying rje dpag tu med pa skyes te rang gi mgrin pa'i rtsa bcad de khrag dang / lus kyi sha bcad nas de rnams la byin pas/
de dag na re/ 'di ltar byas nas khyed ci 'dod zer ba na/ rgyal pos/ bsod nams 'di yis thams cad gzigs pa nyid/ /thob nas nyes pa'i dgra rnams pham byas te/ /skye rga na
'chi'i rba klong 'khrugs pa yi/ /srid pa'i mtsho las 'gro ba 'don par shog /ces gsungs pas/ de dag gis/ de'i tshe nged rnams kyang khyed kyi 'khor gyi thog mar skye bar gyur
cig ces smon lam btab pa la brten nas gnod sbyin de dag rgyal po de sangs rgyas nas ston pa 'dir gyur pa'i tshe 'khor 'dus pa dang por byung ba yin par bshad pa yin no/
/de ltar chos 'khor bskor nas/ mya ngan las 'das pa'i mdzad pa ni/ de nas mya ngan las 'da' bar nye ba na/ ston pas kun dga' bo la mya ngan las mi 'da' ba gsol bar bskul
ba'i phyir du/ kun dga' bo gang su yang rung rdzu 'phrul gyi

rkang pa bzhi la brten sgom mang du byas pa de 'dod na bskal pa'i bskal pa las lhag gi bar du 'dug go /de bzhin gshegs pas rdzu 'phrul gyi rkang pa bzhi la brten sgom mang
du byas pas/ de bzhin gshegs pa bzhed na bskal pa'i bskal pa las lhag pa'i bar du yang bzhugs so/ /zhes lan du mar bskul kyang kun dga' bo bdud kyis khebs pas cang mi zer
ro/ /de'i tshe bdud sdig can gyis mya ngan las 'da' bar gsol ba btab pas zla ba gsum na 'da' bar zhal gyis bzhes so/ /de nas ston pas 'tsho ba'i 'du byed ni byin gyis brlabs/
tshe'i 'du byed ni spangs so/ /de'i tshe sa g.yos/ skar mda' lhung / phyogs tshig bar snang gi lha rnams kyis rnga brdungs par gyur pa na/ de'i rgyu zhus pas/ sa g.yos
pa'i rgyu brgyad gsungs pas/ kun dga' bos bcom ldan 'das kyis tshe'i 'du byed btang bar rig nas gsol ba btab pas ma gnang ngo / /de nas kyang yul yangs pa can la sogs
pa du mar gdul bya mang po'i don mdzad de/ rim gyis grong khyer rtswa can gyad kyi yul dang nye ba shing sA la zung gi tshal ga la ba der gshegs pas/ der grong khyer pa
rnams kyis lam thams cad mdzes par byas/ sA la zung gi dbus su khri bcas 'phong byang du bstan pa la glo g.yas pa phab/ zhabs kyi steng du zhabs bzhag ste mya ngan las 'da'
ba'i 'du shes mdzad nas gzims so/ /der kun dga' bo ni khri la 'jus nas ngu zhing smre sngags 'don pa la/ ston pas/ kun dga' bo khyod mya ngan dang smre sngags 'don par
ma byed cig de ci'i phyir na/

kun dga' bo khyod kyis de bzhin gshegs pa'i nye gnas byas pa ni/ byams pa'i lus dang / ngag dang / yid kyi las kyi phan pa dang / bde ba dang / gnyis su med pa dang / tshad
med par byas so zhes gsungs shing / ngo mtshar ba'i chos bzhi gsungs nas mya ngan bsal lo/ /de nas ston pa'i sku dngos kyi gdul bya rab dga' dang / rab bzang / 'dun pa rnams
la chos bstan pas de rnams kyis kyang bden pa mthong / de nas bcom ldan 'das kyis mu stegs can shAkya dang mos pa ral pa can ma gtogs rab tu mi dbyung / 'khor rnam bzhir
phan bder 'gyur ba'i gsung rab bcu gnyis bklag ston pa so thar la gyis/ rgan pas gzhon pa rnams yo byad kyis bsdu/ gzhon pas rgan pa la ming 'bod mi bya/ dad pa can
la ston pa 'khrungs pa/ sangs rgyas pa/ chos gsungs pa/ mya ngan las 'das pa'i phyogs bzhi bstan par bya'o/ /dge slong dag dkon mchog gsum dang bden pa bzhi la the tshom
yod na zhus shig zhes sogs gsungs nas mya ngan las 'da' ba'i tshul bstan to/ /de'i tshe sa g.yos/ skar mda' lhung / phyogs tshig lhas rol mo'i sgra ches cher bsgrags so/
/dge slong kha cig sa la 'gre ldog la las ku co 'don/ kha cig sdug bsngal gyis gzir/ 'ga' zhig chos nyid la rtog cing gnas/ dge slong kha cig gis/ sA la zung ni rab mdzes
pa'i/ /ljon shing mchog gi tshal du 'dir/ /ston pa mya ngan 'das pa la/ /me tog dag gis rab tu gtor/ /zhes zer/ brgya byin gyis/ kye ma 'dus byas rnams mi rtag /skye

zhing 'jig pa'i chos can yin/ /skyes nas 'jig par 'gyur ba ste/ /de dag nye bar zhi ba bde/ /zhes dang / tshangs pas/ 'byung po kun gyi 'jig rten 'dir ni bsags pa'i mtha'/
/'dod 'gyur 'jig rten 'di na gang zag bla med gcig /de bzhin gshegs pa stobs rnams brnyes pa spyan ldan pa/ /ston pa 'di lta bu yang yongs su mya ngan 'das/ /zhes pa dang
/ ma 'gags pas/ brtan pa'i thugs kyis skyob mdzad pa/ /mi g.yo zhi ba brnyes gyur pa/ /dbugs dbyung ba dang rngub 'gags nas/ /spyan ldan yongs su mya ngan 'das/ /zhes gsungs
so/ /de nas nyan thos chen po ni kun shes/ skul byed/ stobs bcu 'od srung / 'od srung chen po ste bzhi la sogs pas sku gdung shing bal gyi lwa ba dang / ras zung lnga
brgyas dkris/ lcags kyi sgrom du bcug 'bru mar gyis bkang / lcags khab gnyis kyis bkab ste/ dri zhim po'i shing mang po spungs pas me rang 'bar du gyur te zhag bdun du
ma shi ba na/ gyad rnams kyis bsad de/ 'o ma las me tog ser can/ ser skya/ rta don/ u dum wa ra ste bzhi skyes/ sku gdung rnams gser gyi bum par bcug mchod pa byas so/ /de
nas yul sdig pa can gyi gyad rnams dang / yul rtog pa g.yo ba'i rgyal rigs bu lu ka sgra sgrogs kyi kro dha ba/ khyab 'jug gling gi bram ze/ ser skya'i shAkya/ yangs pa
can gyi li tsa byi/ ma ga dha'i ma skyes dgra rnams kyis rtswa can gyi gyad rnams la/ ston pa ni nged rnams la yun ring po nas phan zhing bla mar gyur pa yin pas/ khyed
kyi yul gyi nye 'khor du 'das pa zhig na/

gdung gi skal ba byin cig so so'i yul du mchod rten byas te dus ston byed do/ /mi ster na dmag gis don 'phrog zer ba la/ gyad gis kyang de bzhin nged kyang byed do zer nas
gdung gi phyir 'thab par brtsams pa na/ bram ze'i rigs bre bo dang mnyam pas/ rtswa can gyi gyad rnams dang / sku gdung slong ba po rnams la/ ston pa ni yun ring po nas bzod
pa dang ldan pa/ bzod pa'i bsngags pa brjod pa yin pa la/ sku gdung gi phyir gcig gis gcig gsod par mi rigs kyi kho bos sku gdung cha brgyad du bgos la so so la sbyin/
bum pa la kho bos mchod pa bya'o/ /zhes smras pas/ de la kun mthun te/ de bzhin byas pas rang rang gi skal ba yul du khyer te mchod rten brtsigs pa dang dus ston byed cing
/ sgra sgrog pa'i skal ba klus 'phrogs te klus mchod do/ /de bzhin du gdung bcug pa'i bum pa bram ze'i rigs bre bo dang mnyam pa la byung ba de/ gdung gi sol ba nya gro
dha la byung ba gnyis la yang mchod rten brtsigs pas mchod rten bcu/ tshems mche ba bzhi la mchod rten re re ste bcu gnyis byon pa yin no/ /de ltar mya ngan las 'das pa'i
tshul 'di la nyan thos pa dag bud shing zad pa'i me bzhin du bem rig rgyun chad par 'dod/ theg chen ltar na/ sprul pa'i sku ni mya ngan las 'da' bar brjod kyi cig shos
min/ gtan du gnas pa'i rgyu ldan pa/ /mya ngan 'da' bar yang mi rigs/ /zhes gsungs pa ltar longs sku ni mya ngan las 'da' ba'i tshul yang mi ston la/ sprul sku gdul bya'i
dbang gis mya ngan las 'da' ba'i tshul ston yang / rgyun

chad pa ni mi 'dod de/ dper na sman pa mkhas pas bu sman mi 'thung ba la/ phas 'di 'thungs shig ma 'thungs na/ nga ni 'chi 'o zhes smras pa dang / bu des pha ni 'chi gzhan
sman ster ba ni med snyam sman 'thung nad gsos pa na pha shi ba min par shes kyang rdzun gyi nyes par mi 'gyur ba bzhin/ gdul bya rtag 'dzin can rnams chos la bskul ba'i
phyir yin gyi/ brgya byin sogs su sprul nas 'gro ba'i don mdzad pa yang yod pa dang / da lta shar phyogs kyi zhing khams rnam par spud pa zhes pa na sangs rgyas rnam par
snang mdzad 'od zer gyis brgyan pa rnam par 'phrul ba'i rgyal po zhes bya ba sku tshe bskal pa grangs med bdun brgya thub pa zhig bzhugs te de bdag cag gi ston pa 'di yin
par bshad do/ /de ltar yang / mdo sde rgyan las/ ji ltar me ni gzhan du 'bar/ /de bzhin sangs rgyas sems can la/ /snang dang mi snang shes par bya/ /zhes gsungs pas so/
/gnyis pa thun mong ma yin pa ston pa he ru ka'i byon tshul la/ gdul bya dbang phyug gi byung tshul/ 'dul byed he ru ka'i byon tshul/ des de ji ltar btul pa'i tshul dang
gsum las/ dang po ni/ nam byung ba'i dus la mkhas pa rnams mi mthun pa mang yang / thog mar na ro pa'i man ngag gi lugs ltar bshad na/ dus bzhi las rtsod dus kyi mgo rtsom
pa'i tshe mi rnams phan tshun

mig ser la brten nas sems can rnams gcig gis gcig gsod pa'i las byung zhing / bsad pa'i ro rnams phyogs mtshams brgyad du bskyal bas dur khrod brgyad chags/ der ro la khrag
byung ba'i rlangs pa nam mkha' la song bas sprin brgyad chags/ de las char babs pas chu chen brgyad byung / chu'i rlan la brten nas shing chen brgyad skyes/ shing brgyad
la phyogs skyong brgyad gnas/ chu chen po brgyad la klu chen brgyad gnas la/ de nas gnas nyi shu rtsa bzhi dang / yul sum cu so gnyis kyang rim gyis chags so/ /de'i tshe
ri rab kyi steng na drag po dbang phyug chen po sku mdog nag po zhal gcig pa/ phyag bcu gnyis pa/ gcer bu lus la thal bas byugs pa/ ral pa'i cod pan can/ yum lha mo u ma
sku mdog dmar mo zhal gcig phyag gnyis mas 'khyud pa zhig byung ngo / 'di la thugs gsung sku yon tan 'phrin las kyi sprul pa bzhi las/ thugs kyi sprul pa nam mkha' la lha'i
gtso bo bzhi chung ma dang bcas pa byung nas/ shar phyogs pu la ri ma la ya/ byang dza landha ra/ nub o Di ya na/ lho arbu ta dang bzhi bzung zhing / gnas sam yul de
bzhi la lha'i skad du gnas zhes bya'o/ /yang lha'i g.yog po dri za bzhi chung ma dang bcas pa byung ste/ shar lho go ta wa ri/ lho nub ra mi shwa ra/ nub byang de wi ko Ta/
byang shar ma la ba ste mtshams bzhi bzung ngo / /de bzhi la dri za'i skad du nye ba'i gnas zhes bya'o/ /de brgyad ni dbang phyug gi thugs kyi sprul pa ste nam mkha' la
spyod pas mkha'

spyod kyi 'jigs byed brgyad ces bya bar grags so/ /yang ri rab kyi khong seng nas gnod sbyin gyi gtso bo gnyis chung ma dang bcas pa byung nas shar phyogs ka ma ru pa dang
/ byang phyogs o Ti gnyis bzung ste/ gnas de gnyis la gnod sbyin gyi skad du zhing zhes bya'o/ /gnod sbyin gyi g.yog po gnyis chung ma dang bcas pa byung nas nu tr-i sha
ku ne dang / lho ko sa la gnyis bzung zhing / gnas de gnyis la gnod sbyin gyi skad du nye ba'i zhing zhes bya'o/ /yang srin po'i gtso bo gnyis chung ma dang bcas pa byung
ste/ shar lho ka ling ka dang / lho nub lam pa ka gnyis bzung zhing / gnas de gnyis la srin po'i skad du tshandho zhes bya'o/ /srin po'i 'khor gnyis chung ma dang bcas pa
byung ste nub byang kan dzi dang / byang shar hi ma la ya gnyis bzung ste/ de gnyis la srin po'i skad du nye ba'i tshandho zhes bya'o/ /de rnams ni drag po dbang phyug
gi gsung gi sprul pa ste sa bla na spyod pas sa spyod kyi 'jigs byed brgyad ces bya'o/ /yang rgya mtsho'i nang nas klu gtso bo gnyis chung ma dang bcas pa byung ste shar
phyogs pre ta pu ri dang / byang phyogs kyi gr-i ha de wa gnyis bzung ste/ gnas de gnyis la klu'i skad du 'du ba zhes bya zhing / klu'i 'khor g.yog gnyis chung ma dang bcas
pa byung nas nub sau raShTa dang / lho phyogs su warna de wi gnyis bzung ste de gnyis la klu'i skad du nye ba'i 'du ba zhes bya la/ yang ri rab kyi 'og nas lha ma yin
gyi gtso bo gnyis chung ma dang bcas pa byung nas/ shar lho na ga ra dang / lho nub sindhu ra gnyis bzung

ste/ gnas de gnyis la lha ma yin gyi skad du dur khrod ces bya'o/ /yang lha ma yin gyi bran g.yog gnyis chung ma dang bcas pa byung nas nub byang ma ro dang / byang shar ku
lu ta gnyis bzung ste/ de gnyis la lha ma yin gyi skad du nye ba'i dur khrod ces bya zhing / de rnams ni dbang phyug gi sku'i sprul pa ste sa 'og nas 'dzam bu'i gling du
spyod pas na sa 'og na spyod pa'i 'jigs byed brgyad ces bya'o/ /yang dbang phyug des yon tan las thun mtshams kyi yum bzhi sprul te/ de yang mdun du sgra gcan ma sngon mo/
g.yon du nye ba'i sgra gcan ma ljang khu/ rgyab tu mun pa ma dmar mo/ g.yas su nye ba'i mun pa ma ser mo rnams sprul/ yang des 'phrin las las thun mtshams kyi ma mo brgyad
sprul te/ shar du khwa gdong ma sngon mo/ byang du 'ug gdong ma ljang khu/ nub tu khyi gdong ma dmar mo/ lhor phag gdong ma ser mo/ mtshams bzhir mi'i gdong can phyed
gzugs ma bzhi sprul zhing / de rnams kyi nang nas thugs kyi sprul pa brgyad zhe sdang shas che bas kha dog kyang nag po/ gsung gi sprul pa brgyad 'dod chags shas che bas
kha dog kyang dmar po/ sku'i sprul pa brgyad gti mug shas che bas kha dog kyang dkar po/ yon tan gyi sprul pa brgyad nga rgyal dang / ser sna shas che bas rang rang gi
mdog la so mdangs che ba/ 'phrin las kyi sprul pa brgyad phrag dog shas che bas kha dog sna tshogs pa'o/ /de ltar sprul pa'i drag po dbang phyug nyi shu rtsa bzhi po de dag
mthu che ba/ rtsal drag pas phan tshun gcig 'og tu gcig ma 'du bar

thun mong du dpon gcig dgos so zhes gleng ba na/ ri rab kyi rtse na drag po dbang phyug chen po bzhugs te de la zhus pas/ de lha mo u ma dang rgyun du snyoms par 'jug cing
/ thun mtshams su yang ma mo bcu gnyis dang snyoms par 'jug pas mi khom ste/ de rnams la mchod pa'i rten du rdo'i rang byung gi ling ga nyi shu rtsa bzhi byin te/ de yang
pu li ra ma la yar mgo bo lta bu'i ling ga nas/ ku lu rar pus mo lta bu'i ling ga'i bar te/ de ltar na yul nyi shu rtsa bzhi na rang byung gi ling ga nyi shu rtsa bzhi gnas
so/ /de dag gis kyang de rnams la dus gsum du mchod pa byed do/ /de'i tshe dbang phyug rnams kyis 'dzam bu gling gi skye dgu thams cad ma rungs par byas te/ zhe sdang
shas che bas zas su mi sha bza'/ skom du mi khrag 'thung / gos stan mi lpags kyi g.yang gzhi la byas/ mi'i rus pas rgyan drug byas so/ 'dod chags shas che bas spyod lam
rnam pa bzhir 'dod chags kyis kun tu spyod pa byed cing / gti mug shas che bas 'dod yon lnga rang dgar spyod/ las dang de kho na nyid kyi don la rmongs pas/ rang log pa'i
lam la gnas nas/ gzhan dag kyang log pa'i lam la 'jug par byed do/ /nga rgyal shas che bas dregs pa'i rlom tshig smras shing / de ltar dug gsum la kun tu spyod cing 'dzam
bu gling gi skye dgu thams cad dbang du bsdus shing gnas so/ /gnyis pa 'dul byed he ru ka byon pa'i tshul ni/ de ltar drag po dbang phyug gtso 'khor dag gis 'jig rten gyi
khams ma rungs par byas pa de'i tshe/ 'og min stug po bkod pa'i zhing khams na bzhugs pa'i longs sku rgyu'i

he ru ka des/ dbang phyug 'khor bcas 'dul dgos shing dus la yang bab par mkhyen te/ 'dul thabs ji ltar rigs dgongs pa na/ gzhan gang gis kyang mi thul zhing / rang ming dang
cha lugs sogs mthun pas 'dul nus par dgongs te/ dgongs pa sna tshogs pa dam tshig chen po rnam par rol pa'i rdo rje zhes bya ba'i ting nge 'dzin la snyoms par zhugs te/
sku'i ba spu'i bu ga nas dkyil 'khor sna tshogs pa gling bzhi bye ba phrag brgyar spros shing / khyad par du ri rab kyi rtse mor sprul sku 'bras bu'i he ru ka gtso 'khor
drug cu rtsa gnyis sprul pa yin te/ de yang dbang phyug dang u ma'i gnyen por gtso bo yab yum gnyis/ thun mtshams kyi ma mo bzhi'i gnyen por snying po'i rnal 'byor ma bzhi/
drag po 'jigs byed nyer bzhi chung ma dang bcas pa'i gnyen por thugs gsung sku'i dpa' bo nyer bzhi yum dpa' mo nyer bzhi dang bcas pa/ ma mo brgyad kyi gnyen por sgo
mtshams ma brgyad rnams sku mdog dang zhal phyag sogs gdul bya dang mthun par sprul pa yin te/ rnal 'byor ma snying po'i rgyud las/ gdul bya'i ming ni 'dul byed la grags
'gyur/ /zhes gsungs pas so/ /gsum pa des de ji ltar btul ba'i tshul ni/ rgyud de nyid las/ drag po 'jigs byed 'khor dang bcas pa yang / /'jug cing dbang byas longs spyod
thim par spyad/ /ces gsungs pa ltar/ longs spyod pa dang / thim pa dang / dbang du byas pa gsum gyi sgo nas 'dul bar mdzad pa yin pas/ de'i dang po longs spyod pa ni/ drag
po 'jigs byed 'khor dang bcas pas kha zas dang btung ba sha dang khrag dron mo la byed pa

rnams he ru ka gtso 'khor rnams kyis tshogs kyi 'khor lor longs spyad de gsol bas dpal khrag 'thung gi lha tshogs zhes grags so/ /rus pa'i rgyan dang mi lpags kyi gos sogs
'phrogs te rgyan gos su mdzad pas he ru ka'i chas drug ces grags pa de yin no/ /gnyis pa thim pa ni/ drag po dbang phyug 'khor dang bcas pa tshar bcad de rnam par shes pa
'od gsal du bstims pas/ slar yang rjes su bzung bas ma 'ongs pa'i dus su de bzhin gshegs pa thal ba'i dbang po zhes bya bar lung ston par mdzad do/ /gsum pa dbang du bya
ba ni/ 'jig rten gyis thu bo che drag po 'khor dang bcas pa bcom pa'i brdar/ de thams cad kyi lus he ru ka 'khor dang bcas pa'i gdan du mdzad pa yin te/ thams cad kyang
yi dwags kyi gdan la bzhugs pa'o/ /zhes dang / rtsa rgyud las/ yi dwags chen po gdan du byas/ /zhes gsungs pas so/ /de yang he ru ka yab yum gyis 'jigs byed dus mtshan gdan
du mdzad/ snying po'i rnal 'byor ma bzhis sgra gcan ma sogs yab yum bzhi gdan du btings/ 'khor lo gsum gyi dpa' bo nyer bzhi'i 'jigs byed nyer bzhi chung ma dang bcas
pa gdan du mdzad/ sgo mtshams ma brgyad kyis thun mtshams kyi ma mo mi'am ci'i bu mo brgyad gdan mdzad pa yin no/ /de ltar gdul bya dang / 'dul byed 'dul tshul de dag drang
don du yin gyi/ nges pa'i don du sangs rgyas kyi ye shes gcig gis bsdus pa'i cho 'phrul yin pas tha dad pa ma yin te/ 'dus par/ sku yi rdo rje tshangs par 'gyur/ /gsung
gi ston pa dbang phyug che/ /thugs kyi ston pa khyab 'jug

yin/ /zhes bshad pa ltar/ 'jigs byed 'khor bcas ni dbang phyug gi sprul pa/ dbang phyug ni rdo rje 'chang gi sprul pa/ 'dul byed 'khor gyi lha tshogs rnams ni he ru ka'i sprul
pa/ he ru ka ni rdo rje 'chang gi sprul pa ste/ mdor na de thams cad nges don du rdo rje 'chang gi ngo bo'i rang bzhin yin no/ /yang 'khor lo bde mchog gi chos 'byung
'ga' zhig las/ sprul pa byung tshul gong dang 'dra ba la gtso bo dbang phyug chen po la zhi ba'i sku lag pa bzhi pa kha dog dkar po/ chung ma dkar mo dang snyoms par sbyor
ba ri rab kyi dbus na gnas/ rgyas pa'i sku ser po mgo bo brgyad pa chung ma ral gcig ma dang snyoms par 'jug pa ri rab kyi shar na gnas/ dbang gi sku dmar po chung ma
dmar mo dang snyoms par 'jug pa gzhan 'phrul dbang byed na gnas/ mngon spyod kyi sku drag po 'jigs byed nag po chung ma dang snyoms par 'jug pa 'dzam bu gling gi dbus ma
ga dha na gnas par bshad cing / 'dul byed he ru ka byon tshul la/ dus de'i tshe rdo rje 'chang chen chos kyi dbyings kyi pho brang du mngon byang lngas mngon par rdzogs par
sangs rgyas te/ chos sku dbyings dang ye shes dbyer med kyi ngang las gsang ba mchog gi gnas 'og min gyi pho brang du 'khor de bzhin gshegs pa dang / byang chub sems dpa'
tshad med pa 'dus pa la 'od gsal lhan cig skyes pa'i chos bstan to/ /de nas 'jigs byed 'khor bcas 'dul ba'i dus la bab par dgongs nas sprul sku 'bras bu'i he ru kar bzhengs
te ri rab kyi rtse mor byon pa la/ mi bskyod pas gzhal yas khang

gdan dang bcas pa phul/ rin 'byung gis 'jam dbyangs la sogs pa byang sems rnams/ dpa' bo nyer bzhi dang / rdo rje'i pho nya mo la sogs pa rnams dpa' mo nyer bzhir sprul te
phul/ snang ba mtha' yas kyis lha mo bcu gnyis sprul te/ don yod grub pas go cha'i lha bcu gnyis sprul te phul/ rnam snang gis phung khams skye mched byin gyis brlabs pa'i
lha rnams sprul te/ gzhan yang rigs bzhi'i mchod pa'i lha mo sprul te dkyil 'khor gyi lha rnams la mchod pa byas te/ sprul pa'i 'khor de rnams las kyang yang sprul dang
nying sprul gyi tshogs bsam gyis mi khyab pa sprul lo/ /de nas longs sku dgongs pa sna tshogs pa'i dam tshig chen po rnam par rol pa'i rdo rje zhes bya ba'i ting nge 'dzin
la zhugs nas gdul bya la gzigs te/ ba spu'i bu ga nas dkyil 'khor gyi 'khor lo sna tshogs pa sprul/ gling bzhi bye ba phrag brgyar spros/ 'dzam bu'i gling 'dir bcom ldan
'das 'khor lo bde mchog zhal bzhi phyag bcu gnyis par sprul nas drag po 'jigs byed dang / dus mtshan ma zhabs 'og tu mnan te btul bas/ 'jigs byed sa 'og tu sangs rgyas
so/ /byang chub sems dpa' kun tu bzang po la sogs pa nyi shu rtsa bzhi khro bor sprul nas/ rdo rje'i pho nya mo la sogs pa'i lha mo rnams khro mor sprul pa dang snyoms par
'jug pa'i sku can/ yul nyi shu rtsa bzhi na bzhugs pa'i thugs 'khor gyi dpa' mo brgyad kyis thod pa'i dum bu la sogs pa'i lha bzhi dang / dri za bzhi/ gsung 'khor gyi
dpa' bo brgyad kyis gnod sbyin bzhi dang srin po bzhi/ sku 'khor gyi dpa'

bo brgyad kyis klu bzhi dang lha ma yin bzhi btul cing / grong mtha' dang nye ba'i grong mtha'i/ 'thung spyod dang nye ba'i 'thung spyod na gnas pa'i mi'am ci bzhi/ sna tshogs
ma ste phra men ma bzhi'am/ yang na mi'am ci mo brgyad ni/ khro bo 'jig rten gsum rgyal dang / lha mo gau rI la sogs pa yab yum brgyad la/ sgo ba bzhi'i yab rnams gdong
brnyan gyi tshul du gnas/ mtshams ma bzhi'i yab rnams phyed gzugs kyi tshul du sbas nas ma mo'i skur bstan pas mi'am ci mo brgyad btul lo/ /ma mA ki la sogs pa'i yum bzhi
ni snying po'i rnal 'byor ma bzhir sprul te/ dbang phyug gi chung ma bzhi btul bar bshad la/ de dag gis de rnams btul tshul la yang / dbang du byed pa dang / longs spyod
pa dang / thim pa gsum du mdzad cing / dbang du byed pa la yang / lus dbang du byed pa/ ngag dbang du byed pa/ sems dbang du byed pa gsum du bshad nas/ lus dbang du byed
pa ni/ mnyam sbyor las/ sdig med stobs kyi ngo thon du/ /dbang phyug dam pa rab mnan pa/ /lha mo bhi mos 'phrogs nas ni/ /de tshe longs spyod rang gis spyod/ /ces pa
ltar/ 'dul byed de dag gdul bya de rnams dang ming dang cha lugs mthun par bsgyur nas/ dbang phyug la sogs pa'i 'jigs byed gtso 'khor rnams bsgyel te/ chung ma rnams 'phrogs
nas dga' ba bzhir longs spyod pa'o/ /ngag dbang du byed pa ni 'jig rten pa'i thod pa'i dum bu la sogs pa'i srog sngags ka ra ka ra la sogs pa rnams 'jig rten las 'das
pa'i sku gsung thugs kyi snying po oM dang / hU~M hU~M phaTa? kyi bar

du bcug nas lha so so'i sngags su byin gyis brlabs pa'o/ /sems dbang du byed pa ni/ gdul byed de rnams kyi sems rnam par mi rtog pa'i ngang du brgyal bar byas pa'o/ /longs
spyod pa ni/ btsun mo rnams la dga' ba bzhis longs spyad/ rus pa'i rgyan 'phrogs te sku la gsol/ longs spyod 'phrogs te tshogs kyi 'khor lor rol/ lag cha 'phrogs te phyag
mtshan du mdzad/ ro gdan sogs 'phrogs te gdan du btings/ 'dug pa'i yul 'phrogs te pho brang du byas pa'o/ /thim pa ni/ rnam par dag pa srog thim pa ste spangs pa phun sum
tshogs pa dang / sems 'od gsal du 'dres nas zung 'jug tu bzhengs pa sems thim pa ste rtogs pa phun sum tshogs par mdzad pa'o zhes 'byung ngo / /'o na gnas nyer bzhi po
de dag yul gang dang gang na yod snyam na/ rtsa rgyud las/ pu la sogs pa gang bstan pa/ /phyi nang bdag nyid can du gnas/ /zhes pa ltar/ spyir yul nyer bzhi la phyi'i yul
nyer bzhi/ nang gi yul nyer bzhi gnyis su yod pa las/ phyi ma ni nang rdo rje'i lus la tshangs pa'i spyi bo dang / spyi gtsug rna ba g.yas pa dang / ltag pa/ rna ba g.yon
pa dang / smin mtshams/ mig gnyis dang / phrag pa gnyis/ mchan khung gnyis dang / nu ma gnyis/ lte ba dang / sna rtse/ kha dang / mgrin pa/ snying kha dang / 'doms bar/
mtshan ma dang / bshang lam/ brla gnyis dang / byin pa gnyis/ mthe bong bzhi dang / pus mo gnyis/ ser mo bcu drug dang / bol gong gnyis te nyer bzhi po 'di dag go /phyi'i
yul nyer bzhi ni/ pu la

ra ma la ya sogs nyer bzhi ste/ yul dang po 'di ni/ rgya gar shar phyogs bhaM ga la'i lho mtsho ma la ya'i chu klung gi gnas Da khi ta 'dug pa'i sa na bsgrub gnas rdo'i ling
ga mgo bo lta bu'i mtshan pa yod pa de yin par bshad la/ dza landha ra ni/ gu ge'i nub byang na tho ling gi gtsang po sha ba ru/ gangs gtsang sha'i gtsang po pi pa sha
na/ sha la dza'i gtsang po me ra be dang gsum 'dus pa'i mdo na grong khyer chen po zhig yod par bshad cing / de'i nye logs na rdo'i ling ga thod pa kha sbubs pa lta bu phyogs
gcig na bu ga dang bcas pa yod pa'i gnas de yin par gsungs shing / de'i nye 'khor na zhing skyong lha mo dzwa la mu khi zhes bya ba rdo la rang 'khrungs su yod pa kha
bubs su nyal ba de la gtsug lag khang brtsigs pa yang yod par bshad la/ de nas rgyang grags gcig gi pha rol na sgrub pa'i gnas brag phug brgya/ chu mig brgya/ shing brgya
yod pa'i thad ka'i brag dkyil nas chu 'bab pa de la mu stegs byed rnams khrus byed pa zhig yod pa'i gnas de ni o Di ya na ste/ de zur chag pas u rgyan zhes grags pa rgyal
po indra bhu ti byon pa'i yul de yin par gsungs so/ /arbu ta ni/ rgya gar lho phyogs na ri dbus mtho zhing mtha' dma' ba 'brang rgyas 'dra ba/ nags tshal 'thug pos bskor
ba sgrub pa'i gnas nyams dga' ba zhig yod pa de yin par bshad do/ go ta wa ri ni/ ba'i mchog sbyin zhes bya ba ste/ bal yul du ba dkar mos 'o mas mchod sbyin byas pa'i
shul du brkos pas dbang phyug chen po'i ling ga zhig byung / de ri 'bigs byed dang nye ba rdo rje'i gdan

nas zla ba phyed phyin pa'i sar khyer te mchod pas sgrub chu byung ba'i gnas la grags so/ /ra me shwa ra ni/ dga' ba'i dbang phyug ste/ shar phyogs rgyal po dga' ba'i dbang
phyug gi grong khyer na sgrub gnas rdo'i ling ga rta'i rngog ma lta bu'i mtshan ma yod pa de'o/ /de wi ko Ta ni lha mo'i rdzong ste/ shar phyogs ba rentra'i sa phyogs gro
mo'i lho thad na grong khyer panytsa pa zhes bya ba'i pha rol rgyang grags bzhi'i sa na de wi ko Ta'i lha khang yod cing yul de na gnas chen po de yod par bshad pa yin
zhing / ma la wa ni nub phyogs na phreng ba can zhes bya ba'i yul na sgrub gnas ri g.yas g.yon gnyis mtho ba phrag pa lta bu'i gnas de nyid de/ de rnams ni mkha' spyod kyi
'jigs byed brgyad kyis bzung bas mkha' spyod kyi gnas zhes bya'o/ /ka ma ru pa ni/ 'dod pa'i gzugs te dmyal gyi lho thad na grong khyer chen po zhig yod cing / de'i phyogs
gcig na sgrub gnas rdo'i ling ga mchan khung lta bu'i mtshan pa'i chos 'byung mi gang tsam gyis mtho ba zhig yod pa de yin par bshad la/ o Te ni/ lho phyogs rgyal po
shing rta bcu pa'i gnas na rdo'i ling ga nu ma lta bu'i mtshan pa'i sgrub gnas yod par bshad pa de yin zhing / tri sha ku ne ni/ stag gzig gi yul na chu bo ganggA dang /
gan ti dang / sa ru pa gsum 'dus pa'i mod na ngang pa la sogs pa'i bya skad snyan pa sgrog pa'i sgrub gnas rdo'i ling ga lte ba lta bus mtshan pa yod pa de yin par gsungs
so/ ko sa la ni/ rgyal po gsal rgyal gyi yul te/ sngon dge ba zhes bya ba'i brtsigs pas dge ba can zhes bya ste/ de nas rgyang grags gcig gi pha rol na

rdo'i ling ga sna lta bus mtshan pa yod do/ /ka ling ka ni/ mang nang gi rgyab/ rdo rje gdan nas dpag tshad kyi tshu rol na glang po 'dzin pa zhes bya ba'i sgrub gnas yod pa
de'o/ yang 'ga' zhig las rdo rje gdan nas dpag tshad drug cu lho nub tu phyin pa'i sa thams cad sgrol gyi yul na yod ces pa yang 'byung ngo / /lamba ka ni/ gar log gi rgyab
brag dang chu 'thab pa'i 'gram na sgrub gnas shin tu dben pa zhig yod pa de'o/ /kan tsi ni/ rgya gar lho phyogs chos kyi grags pa'i yul dang nye ba na/ grong khyer gyi
mchog ces grags pa sngon dha ra ka pa'i grub pa brnyes pa'i sa phyogs te/ de na gser gyi ling ga lta bus mtshan pa'i sgrub gnas zhig yod pa de yin la/ hi ma la ya ni/
gangs can te/ kha cig ti sa na rdo'i ling ga khru gang tsam gcig las chu 'bab pa de la ngos 'dzin/ 'ga' zhig bod spyi la ngos 'dzin pa dag yod kyang / dpal ldan bla ma dam
pa bsod nams rgyal mtshan gyis brtag gnyis kyi rnam bshad du/ hi ma la ya/ gangs can la gsungs pa ltar ngos gzung bar bya'o/ /de dag ni sa spyod kyi 'jigs byed brgyad kyis
bzung bas sa spyod kyi gnas zhes bya'o/ /pre ta pu ri ni/ kha cig rgya gar na yod par 'dod kyang / pu hrang na lung pa zhig gi dbus na rdo'i pho mtshan mi gzugs che ba
tsam/ de'i dkyil na yar chu tshan 'phyur nas yong ba'i gnas de yin par bshad do/ /gr-i ha de wa ni/ li yul lcang ra smug po na rdo'i ling ga snying lta bus mtshan pa'i
sgrub gnas yod pa de nyid do/ /sau ra Ta ni/ yul 'khor bzang po can zhes bya ste/ rdo rje gdan nas nub phyogs su zla ba phyed dang gsum phyin pa na/ so ma thi'i rten yod
pa de yin no/ /

su warna de ba ni/ gser gling ste gser gling rgyal po'i gling chung zhig yin no/ /na ga ra ni/ nub phyogs na ga ra'i yi ge 'byung ba'i yul de na yod par bshad la/ sindhu ni
chu bo chen po sindhu ra 'bab pa'i sa'i cha rgya gar lho phyogs na yod par bshad/ ma ro ni/ dza landha ra dang nye ba'i byang phyogs na brag phug cig na rdo'i mtshan ma
rkang pa'i mthe bong lta bu 'phrul ba la/ ston pas mi 'thon pa shin tu 'jigs par grags pa'i gnas shig yod par bshad pa de'o/ /ku lu ra ni/ gar sha'i rgyab nyung ra'i phug
na rdo'i ling ga pus mo lta bus mtshan pa'i sgrub gnas phug pa thur du brkos pa'i ring po zhig yod pa de yin no/ /de rnams ni sa 'og na spyod pa'i 'jigs byed brgyad kyis
bzung bas sa 'og na spyod pa'i gnas zhes bya'o/ /de ltar 'jigs byed nyer bzhi'i gnas nyer bzhi po de dag la phyi'i yul chen nyer bzhi zhes bya bar yongs su grags pa yin
no/ /gnyis pa byon nas bstan pa dam chos ji ltar gsungs pa'i tshul la/ thun mong ba pha rol tu phyin pa'i chos 'khor bskor tshul dang / thun mong ma yin pa rdo rje theg pa'i
chos 'khor bskor tshul gnyis las/ dang po ni/ gong du bstan pa ltar bdag cag gi ston pa thugs rje chen po dang ldan pa des/ thog mar yul wa ra na sir/ dus lo bdun nam
drug tu/ 'khor lnga sde dang gzhan yang lha'i 'khor mang po la/ chos bden pa bzhi lan gsum du bzlas pa rnam pa bcu gnyis dang ldan pa'i chos kyi 'khor lo/ dngos kyi dgos
pa lnga sde

bden pa la 'god pa dang / brgyud pa'i dgos pa gdul bya gang zag tu 'dzin pa las ldog nas 'bras bu bzhi la 'god pa'i phyir du legs par bskor ba yin la/ de ni bka' bden pa bzhi'i
chos 'khor te drang don gtso che ba gdul bya nyan thos kyi rigs can la gtso bor gsungs pa yin te/ mdo sde dgongs pa nges 'grel las/ bcom ldan 'das kyis dang por yul
wa ra na si drang srong lhung ba ri dwags kyi nags su nyan thos kyi theg pa la yang dag par zhugs pa rnams la 'phags pa'i bden pa bzhi'i rnam pa bstan pas/ chos kyi 'khor
lo ngo mtshar rmad du byung ba/ sngon lhar gyur pa'am mir gyur pa sus kyang chos dang mthun par 'jig rten du ma bskor ba zhig rab tu bskor te/ bcom ldan 'das kyis chos kyi
'khor lo bskor ba de yang / bla na mchis pa/ skabs mchis pa/ drang ba'i don/ rtsod pa'i gzhi'i gnas su gyur pa lags la/ zhes gsungs pas so/ /de nas yang yul wa ra na si
dang nye ba'i gnas bya rgod phung po'i ri la/ 'khor stong nyis brgya lnga bcu 'am lnga stong gi dge slong dang / dge slong ma dang / dge bsnyen pha ma dang / byang chub
sems dpa'i 'khor bye ba phrag khrig brgya stong la sogs pa theg pa chen po'i rigs can rnams la/ chos bka' bar pa mtshan nyid med pa'i chos 'khor te/ chos thams cad ngo bo
nyid ma mchis pa las brtsams te/ sher phyin gyi mdo la sogs pa nges don gtso che ba'i mdo rnams so/ /dgos pa gdul bya rnams gang zag dang / chos su lta ba thams cad las
ldog nas bgrod pa gcig pa'i lam stong nyid du tshul

gcig pa la 'god pa'i phyir du gsungs pa yin te/ mdo sde dgongs pa nges 'grel las/ bcom ldan 'das kyis chos thams cad ngo bo nyid ma mchis pa las brtsams te/ skye ba ma mchis
pa dang / 'gag pa ma mchis pa dang / gzod ma nas zhi ba dang / rang bzhin gyis

yongs su mya ngan las 'das pa nyid las brtsams nas theg pa chen po la yang dag par zhugs pa rnams la stong pa nyid smos pa'i rnam pas ches ngo mtshar rmad du byung ba'i chos
kyi 'khor lo gnyis pa bskor te/ bcom ldan 'das kyis chos kyi 'khor lo bskor ba de yang / bla na mchis pa/ skabs mchis pa/ drang ba'i don rtsod pa'i gzhi'i gnas su gyur
pa lags la/ zhes gsungs/ 'di ni dbu ma pa rnams dgongs pa can du 'chad do/ /de'i rjes su slar yang bcom ldan 'das kyis/ gnas ri ma la ya dang / yangs pa can la sogs par/
'khor theg pa thams cad la yang dag par zhugs pa'i gang zag rnams la/ chos bka' tha ma legs par rnam par phye ba'i chos kyi 'khor lo/ dgos pa 'khor lo dang pos med par lta
ba ldog nas yod rtog shas che bar gyur pa na kun btags med cing / gzhan dbang kun rdzob tu yod pa dang / yongs grub gnyis don dam du yod par bstan pas mtha' gnyis su 'dzin
pa ldog pa'i ched du gsungs pa yin te/ mdo sde dgongs pa nges 'grel las/ bcom ldan 'das kyis chos rnams kyi ngo bo nyid ma mchis pa las brtsams te/ skye ba ma mchis pa
dang / 'gag pa ma mchis pa dang / gzod ma nas zhi ba dang / rang bzhin gyis yongs su mya ngan las 'das pa nyid las brtsams nas theg pa thams cad la yang dag par zhugs pa
rnams la legs par rnam par phye ba dang ldan pa/ ngo mtshar rmad du byung ba'i chos kyi 'khor lo gsum pa bskor to/ /bcom ldan 'das kyis chos kyi 'khor lo bskor ba 'di ni
bla na ma mchis pa/ skabs ma mchis pa/ nges pa'i don lags te/ rtsod pa'i gzhi'i gnas su gyur pa ma lags so zhes gsungs pas so/ /de ltar mdo sde dgongs pa nges 'grel las/
chos 'khor dang po gnyis drang don dang / tha ma nges don yin par bshad pa 'di ni/ rnam rig rtsal du pa ston sems tsam pa'i grub mtha' la dgongs pa yin gyi/ dbu ma pa dag
gi lugs dang mi mthun pas theg chen thun mong ma yin pa'i lugs la mdo de sgra ji bzhin pa'i don ni 'thad ldan du mi bzhed do/ /chos 'khor rim can du gsungs tshul de yang
/ rin chen phreng ba las/ brda sprod pa dag ji lta bur/ /yi ge'i phyi mo klog 'jug ltar/ /de bzhin sangs rgyas sems can la/ /ji tsam bzod pa'i chos bstan to/ /zhes gsungs
pa ltar gdul bya rim gyis drang dgos pa rnams kyi don du gsungs pa'i lugs yin la/ don dam par na bcom ldan 'das kyi gsung gcig nyid kyis/ dus gcig nyid la gdul bya tha
dad pa du ma la chos tha dad pa du ma gsungs pa'i snang ba cig char du bstan pa yin te/ dgongs pa lung ston las/ rtog pa med cing 'khrug med pa/ /yid 'ongs rdo rje'i tshig
gcig pu/ /gdul bya'i bsam pa'i dbang gi na/ /bye brag mang por 'gyur ba yin/ /zhes pa dang / gzhan yang / gsung

gcig nyid du gsungs mod kyi/ /du ma nyid du so sor go /zhes gsungs pas so/ /des na gdul bya rnams la dus gcig nyid du bcom ldan 'das kyi gsung gcig nyid kyis chos tha dad pa
du ma gsungs pa ni gsung gi bkod pa zhes bya ba yin la/ dus gcig la gnas tha dad par sku tha dad pa du ma ston pa ni sku'i bkod pa zhes bya ba yin no/ /gnyis pa thun mong
ma yin pa rdo rje theg pa'i chos 'khor bskor tshul la/ spyir gsang sngags gsungs tshul/ khyad par du 'khor lo bde mchog gsungs pa'i tshul dang gnyis las/ dang po ni/ spyir
gsang ba 'dus pa'i rgyud las/ gsang sngags rdo rje'i theg pa 'di da ltar gyi sangs rgyas shAkya thub pa kho nas gsungs kyi/ 'das pa'i sangs rgyas rnams kyis kyang ma
gsungs/ ma 'ongs pa'i sangs rgyas rnams kyis kyang gsung bar mi 'gyur zhes gsungs mod kyang / de ni gsang ba 'dus pa sogs kyi che ba brjod pa tsam yin gyi nges don du dus
gsum gyi sangs rgyas thams cad kyis gsang sngags rdo rje'i theg pa legs par gsungs pa yin te/ sgyu 'phrul dra ba las/ 'das pa'i sangs rgyas rnams kyis gsungs/ /ma 'ongs
rnams kyang gsung 'gyur la/ /da ltar byung ba'i rdzogs sangs rgyas/ /yang dang yang du gsungs pa gang / /zhes sogs gsungs shing / de ltar du slob dpon rtse mo'i rgyud sde
spyi rnam las gsungs pa'i don bsdus nas/ mkhas pa'i dbang po dkon mchog lhun grub kyi tshul gsum gsal rgyan las/ gal te thub pa'i sngon du sngags kyi lam/ /yod na 'dus
pa'i rgyud dang 'gal

snyam na/ /de ni chos de'i che ba brjod pa tsam/ /yin gyi gsang sngags theg pa dus gsum gyi/ /sangs rgyas kun gyis gsungs pa nges pa'i don/ /zhes gsungs pa yin no/ /de'i nang
nas kyang ston pa 'di thog ma med pa'i dus su 'og min stug po bkod pa'i zhing khams su mngon par rdzogs par sangs rgyas nas chos dang longs spyod rdzogs pa'i sku'i bdag
nyid can du gyur pa'i tshe/ 'khor de bzhin gshegs pa'i tshogs dang / byang chub sems dpa' brjod kyis mi lang ba la dus rtag tu rgyun mi chad par chos zab pa dang rgya che
ba'i gsang sngags rdo rje theg pa gsungs ba yin zhing / de yang sangs rgyas ma thag tu dang por de nyid 'dus pa'i rgyud gsungs pa yin te/ ji skad du de nyid 'dus pa las/
bcom ldan 'das rnam par snang mdzad mngon par rdzogs par sangs rgyas nas ring por ma lon par de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi thugs kun tu bzang po'o/ /zhes sogs dang
/ slob dpon sangs rgyas gsang bas de nyid snang chen las kyang / bcom ldan 'das rnam par snang mdzad kyis 'og min gyi gnas su mngon par byang chub pa sngon du mdzad pa'i
rjes thogs nyid la byang chub sems dpa' kun tu bzang po sogs la thog mar gsungs pa yin no/ /zhes gsungs pas so/ /de nas gzhan yang rgyud sde bsam gyis mi khyab pa zhig gsungs
nas/ de'i rjes su ri rab kyi rtse mo la sogs pa rnams su sprul pa mchog gi skur bstan nas kyang / gdul bya dbang phyug chen po sogs btul nas/ gsang sngags rdo rje theg
pa'i rgyud sde rin po che bsam gyis mi khyab pa zhig ston pa 'dis mi mjed 'jig rten gyi khams

'dir mdzad pa bcu gnyis la sogs pa'i tshul ma bstan gyi gong rol tu legs par gsungs pa yin par mkha' 'gro rgya mtsho sogs las bshad de rgyas par logs su 'chad do/ /khyad par
du ston pa 'di 'dzam bu'i gling du sangs rgyas pa'i tshul bstan nas/ thog mar theg pa gsum gyi chos kyi 'khor lo bskor ba'i rjes su gdul bya chags bral gyi lam gyis 'dul
bar mi nus pa rnams kyi don du gnas 'bras spungs kyi ri la sogs par gsang sngags rdo rje theg pa'i rgyud sde bsdus pa 'ga' zhig dang / gzhan yang dges rdor gyi rgyud sogs
bsam gyis mi khyab pa zhig shAkya thub pa de nyid kyis kyai rdo rje'i rnam pa la sogs par bsgyur nas gsungs pa yin te/ ji skad du/ 'dren pa'i theg pa gsum po dag /bcom
ldan nges par gsungs lags na/ /rgyu 'bras lhun grub tu spyod cing / /sangs rgyas gzhan nas mi 'tshol ba'i/ /nges pa'i theg pa cis ma gsungs/ /zhes zhus pa'i lan du/ rgyu
la mos pa rgyu chos kyi/ /'khor lo rab tu bskor byas nas/ /rdo rje theg pa'i nye lam zhig /ma 'ongs dus na 'byung bar 'gyur/ /zhes dang / de dang mthun par rgyud sde spyi
rnam las 'gal spongs dang bcas gsungs pa'i don bsdus nas/ thams cad mkhyen pa dkon mchog lhun grub kyis/ gsang rgyud mtha' dag grub pa'i gdul bya la/ /sprul sku mchog gis
sngon du gsungs zin kyang / /de nyid 'dus dang bde mchog ma gtogs pa/ /phal cher shAkya thub pa rang nyid dang / /de yi rnam 'phrul gzhan gyis bsdus te gsungs/ /zhes

gsungs pas so/ /gnyis pa khyad par du 'khor lo bde mchog gsungs pa'i tshul la/ rtsa bshad kyi rgyud ji ltar gsungs pa'i tshul/ rtsa bshad la brten pa'i bshad srol ji ltar byung
ba'i tshul/ de rnams kyi nang nas khyad par du 'phags pa'i lam srol ngos bzung / khyad par du 'phags pa de'i lam spyi'i rnam par gzhag pa/ lam de la yid ches shing khungs
btsun par bya ba'i phyir bla ma brgyud pa'i rnam thar bstan pa dang lnga yod pa las/ dang po la yang rtsa ba'i rgyud gsungs pa'i tshul/ bshad pa'i rgyud gsungs pa'i
tshul/ de dag bsdud pa pos bsdus tshul dang gsum las/ dang po ni/ spyir 'khor lo bde mchog gi rgyud rnams gsungs tshul la bshad tshul mang du yod de/ bha wa bha Ta dang
/ skal ldan grags pa sogs ston pa 'di thog ma med pa'i dus su sangs rgyas nas bde mchog gi rgyud rnams gsungs kyi/ phyis zas gtsang ma'i sras su gyur nas gsungs pa med par
bzhed/ de'i rgyu mtshan yang bde mchog yul nyi shu rtsa bzhi na bzhugs pa'i dpa' bo dang rnal 'byor ma rnams kyis rgyun du nyams su blangs pas/ bskal pa chags 'jig gi tshe
yang gzhig par mi nus pas ma nub par gnas/ chos gzhan rnams ni dang por gsungs kyang / bskal pa chags 'jig sogs kyis 'jig pas bar skabs su nub pa'i phyir slar shAkya
thub pas bskyar nas gsungs par bzhed do/ /yang rtsa rgyud kyi 'grel pa indra bhu tis mdzad par/ 'dzam gling gnas su 'gro rnams don gyi phyir/ /mngon par byang chub tshul
bstan bdud btul nas/ /bde bar

gshegs pa'i 'phrin las stobs gzigs pas/ /dha nya ka Ta partha ri zhes gling / /chags pa zad byed chos kyi 'byung gnas nyid/ /dkyil 'khor 'khor lo dpa' bo rnal 'byor ma/ /bye
ba phrag ni brgyad cu la sogs pa/ /dpag med 'dus la gsang chen legs gsungs so/ /zhes sogs kyi lung drangs nas/ dang por sangs rgyas pa'i gnas 'og min du bde mchog gi rgyud
rgyun mi chad par gsungs/ bar du ri rab kyi rtser sprul bshad mdzad nas/ phyis 'dzam bu'i gling du mdzad pa bcu gnyis kyi tshul bstan te/ theg pa gsum gyi chos kyi 'khor
lo bskor nas skal ba dang ldan pa'i gdul bya rnams la dpal 'bras spungs kyi ri la bcom ldan 'das bde mchog 'khor lo'i ting nge 'dzin la snyoms par zhugs nas/ dkyil 'khor
gyi 'khor lo sprul te/ rnal 'byor ma bye ba phrag brgyad cu la bde mchog gi rgyud rnams gsungs shing / drag po 'jigs byed 'khor bcas btul ba'i tshul yang bstan par gsungs
nas/ slar shAkya thub pa nyid kyis bzlas te gsungs par bzhed/ mkha' 'gro rgya mtsho las/ rtsod pa'i dus kyi sa nang du/ /bcom ldan mtha' yas pas 'di gsungs/ /shAkya
seng ges gsungs pa'i rgyud/ /rnal 'byor pha rol son pa'o/ /zhes dang / mkha' 'gro rgya mtsho'i 'grel par/ slar yang rtsod pa'i dus su rgyud chen po 'bum phrag sum cu rtsa
drug pa shAkya seng ges gsungs so zhes gsungs pas/ dang po longs sku rgyu'i he ru kas gsungs pa'i rjes su slar yang bzlas te gsungs

par bshad la/ slob dpon rdo rjes mdzad pa'i 'grel par/ gnyis ldan gyi dus drag po dbang phyug chen po btul zhing / de'i tshe gsungs pa yin par bshad kyang / 'dir ni gdul bya
dbang phyug kyang rtsod dus kyi mgo rtsom pa'i tshe byung ba yin zhing / de dag he ru ka 'khor bcas kyis btul ba'i rjes su rgyud gsungs pa yin pa ni mkha' 'gro rgya mtsho
las gsungs pa yin la/ rtsod dus su gsungs pa'i rgyu mtshan yang / rdo rje sa 'og gi rgyud las/ dus ni rnam bzhi'i dbye ba yis/ /rgyud sde rnam pa bzhir gsungs so/ /zhes
dus rnam pa bzhi'i gdul bya la dgongs nas rgyud sde bzhi gsungs par bshad cing / rtsod pa'i dus kyi gdul bya la bla med gsungs pa'i rgyu mtshan yang / de dus kyi gdul bya
rnams nyon mongs pa shas che bas dug gsum rags pa rnams byang chub kyi lam mam rtsa lag tu bsgyur ba la dgongs pa yin te/ he ru ka mngon 'byung las/ he ru ka dpal bzung
byas nas/ /snyigs ma'i dus su 'grub par 'gyur/ /zhes gsungs pas so/ /des na dus 'dzam bu'i gling gi drag po 'jigs byed 'khor dang bcas pa btul ba'i tshe ri rab kyi rtse
mor legs par sprul pa'i dkyil 'khor gyi nang du ston pa bcom ldan 'das 'khor bcas dkyil 'khor gyi 'khor lor 'khod pa la/ bshad pa'i rgyud ltar na/ dpal phyag na rdo rjes
tshogs mchod sngon du btang nas/ rtsa ba'i rgyud rnams gsung bar gsol ba btab pas/ gnas phun sum tshogs pa ri rab kyi rtser/ ston pa sku gsung thugs kyi bdag nyid

'khor lo bde mchog 'bras bu'i he ru kas/ 'khor gdul bya drag po 'jigs byed 'khor bcas dkyil 'khor la bkod de/ 'khor lo lnga'i lha tshogs rnams dang / gzhan yang ri rab kyi
rdul dang mnyam pa'i sangs rgyas dang byang chub sems dpa'/ skal ba dang ldan pa'i lha dang mi sogs dang / zhu ba po dang bsdud pa po'i 'khor phag mo'am/ phyag rdor la sogs
pa rnams la/ chos phun sum tshogs pa 'khor lo bde mchog rtsa ba'i rgyud rgyas 'bring bsdus pa gsum gsungs pa yin zhing / yang phyag rdor stod 'grel sogs las/ gong du bstan
pa'i 'khor de dag la/ zhu ba po rdo rje phag mos byas te/ bde mchog gi rgyud rnams gsungs pa yin par yang bshad de/ phyag rdor stod 'grel las/ snyigs ma lnga yi dus
'dir ni/ /bsod nams ye shes 'bras thob phyir/ /phag mos gsol btab rdo rje can/ /nyung ngu'i rgyud ni rab gsal mdzad/ /ces dang / he ru ka mngon 'byung las/ de nas dpa' bo
phyag rdor sogs/ /dpa' bo thams cad langs nas ni/ /dkyil 'khor bdag mo la ni zhus/ /zhes yum ngo chen du sbran te rgyud gsung bar gsol ba btab par bshad pas so/ /'ga' zhig
tu phag mo rgyud gsungs pa po dang / rdo rje 'chang zhu bar por bshad pa 'byung yang / gdul bya so so'i snang ngo yin pas 'gal ba med par bu ston rin po ches gsungs so/
/des na gong du bstan pa ltar/ skal ldan grags pa sogs kyis bde mchog gi rgyud rnams ston pa 'dis slar bzlas te ma gsungs par bshad pa dang / mkha' 'gro rgya

mtsho las/ rtsod pa'i dus kyi sa nang du/ /bcom ldan mtha' yas pas 'di gsungs/ /zhes rtsod dus su bzlas te gsungs pa gnyis 'gal ba ltar snang yang / don la de dag mi 'gal te/
snga ma ni ston pa 'dis 'dzam bu gling du mdzad pa bcu gnyis kyi tshul ston par mdzad pa'i rjes su bde mchog gi rgyud bzlas te ma gsungs pa la dgongs la/ phyi ma ni rtsod
dus su yin kyang 'dzam bu'i gling du mdzad pa bcu gnyis kyi tshul ma bstan pa'i snga rol tu gsungs pa la dgongs pa yin pas so/ /mdzad pa bcu gnyis kyi tshul bstan pa'i
rjes su gdul bya thun mong ma yin pa rnams la gsang sngags kyi rgyud shAkya thub pa rang nyid kyis gsungs pa yang mang du yod pa dang / gsang 'dus sogs 'ga' zhig thub dbang
gi rnam 'phrul gzhan gyis gsungs pa sogs yod kyang / de nyid 'dus pa'i rgyud dang / bde mchog gi rgyud rnams ni de dus su bzlas te ma gsungs par rje btsun rtse mos bshad
de/ des mdzad pa'i spyi rnam las/ phyi ma bzlas te ma gsungs pa'ang yod de/ de kho na nyid bsdus pa'i rgyud thog mar gsungs nas de'i rgyud rdzogs pa'i rjes la/ mi'i
nang du babs nas kyang zhes bya ba la sogs pa 'dzam bu'i gling du gshegs pa la sogs pa mdzad par bstan pa lta bu'o/ /dpal bde mchog gi rgyud kyang phyis bzlas te ma gsungs
pa'o/ /zhes slob dpon skal ldan grags pa bzhed de/ dpal bde mchog rtsa ba'i rgyud kyi 'grel pa las/ chos kyi rnam grangs 'di ni thog ma med pa'i rgyu can yin te/ bcom ldan
'das shAkya thub pa las snga ba nyid du gsungs so/ /zhes

'dren par mdzad nas/ de'i mjug tu zhes bshad pa lta bu'o/ /zhes skal ldan grags pa'i bzhed pa rang lugs su mdzad pa dang / de dag gi don bsdus nas tshul gsum gsal rgyan las
kyang / de nyid 'dus dang bde mchog ma gtogs pa/ /zhes gsungs pas so/ /gal te shAkya thub pas 'dzam gling du mdzad pa bcu gnyis sogs kyi tshul ston pa'i gong du rgyud gsungs
pa la dgongs pa yin na/ 'o na mkha' 'gro rgya mtsho las/ shAkya seng ges gsungs pa'i rgyud/ /ces pa dang / rgyud de'i 'grel par yang / slar yang rtsod pa'i dus su rgyud
chen po 'bum phrag sum cu rtsa drug pa shAkya seng ges gsungs so/ /zhes shAkya thub pa'i mtshan 'byung ba ci zhe na/ de ni ri rab kyi rtse mor rgyud gsungs pa po de dang
shAkya thub pa gnyis rgyud gcig pa la dgongs pa yin te/ de ltar du rgyud sde spyi rnam du gsungs shing / de'i don bsdus nas tshul gsum gsal rgyan las/ 'on kyang ston
pa'i ye shes gcig yin phyir/ /shAkya'i mtshan sogs 'byung ba 'gal ba med/ /ces gsungs pas so/ /de lta bu'i rtsa rgyud sogs de dag gi gzhung tshad kyang / rgyas pa le'u 'bum
pa/ 'bring shlau ka 'bum pa/ bsdus pa tshig 'bum pa zhes grub chen na ro ta pa'i man ngag gi lugs 'di la 'byung ba yin zhing / slob dpon rdo rje zhes bya ba'i 'grel par/
rtsa ba'i rgyud le'u 'bum pa/ rgyud phyi ma nam mkha' dang mnyam pa shlau ka 'bum pa/ phyi ma'i phyi ma le'u lnga bcu rtsa gcig shlau ka bdun brgya pa'o zhes gsungs pa
dang yang mthun pa yin no/ /de dag rgyas bsdus kyang rjod byed kyi tshig rgya che chung

gi sgo nas 'jog gi brjod bya rgyas bsdus kyi sgo nas ni ma yin te/ rgyud rgyas pa rnams kyi brjod bya yang bsdus pa'i nang du tshang bar bzhugs pas so/ /'o na de rnams la rtsa
rgyud ces gsungs pa'i rgyu mtshan gang yin snyam na/ rgyud sde spyi rnam gyi don bsdus tshul gsum gsal rgyan las/ rgyud gang sngon byung bshad gzhi rtsa rgyud de/ /phyis
byung 'chad byed rgyud rnams bshad rgyud yin/ /zhes gsungs pa ltar/ dang por byung zhing bshad pa'i gzhir gyur pa'i rgyud yin pas na rtsa rgyud ces bya la/ de la yang
rtsa rgyud du mi mthun kyang don gyi 'jog tshul mi 'dra ba bzhi'i sgo nas rnam pa bzhir gsungs te/ phyi ma las kyang phyi ma ste/ /zhes pa ltar/ rgyud phyi ma shlau ka 'bum
pa dang / phyi ma'i phyi ma tshig 'bum pa sogs 'byung ba'i gzhir gyur pa'i rtsa rgyud ni le'u 'bum pa lta bu ste/ rgyud phyi ma la ltos pa'i rtsa rgyud dang / yan lag
gi rgyud bsam gyis mi khyab pa yod pa rnams kyi rten nam gzhir gyur pa/ rtsa rgyud rgyas 'bring bsdus gsum lta bu yan lag gi rgyud la ltos pa'i rtsa rgyud dang / yang bde
mchog gi bshad rgyud du 'gro ba tsam sum cu rtsa gnyis la sogs pa yod par gsungs pa rnams kyis dgongs pa nges par 'grel pa'i gzhir gyur pa rtsa rgyud gsum ga lta bu ste/
bshad rgyud la ltos pa'i rtsa rgyud dang / thog mar gdul bya skal ba dang ldan pa rnams la don gsal zhing tshig rgyas pa/ bsdus rgyud bsdus pa'i gzhir gyur pa/ le'u 'bum
pa dang / shlau ka 'bum pa gnyis lta bu bsdus rgyud la ltos pa'i rtsa rgyud dang rnam pa bzhir gsungs pa yin no/ /de ltar gsungs pa'i rtsa rgyud dang po gnyis

ni de dus kyi 'khor rnams kyis thugs nyams su bzhes shing / snyigs ma'i gdul bya rnams kyi spyod yul du ma gyur pas sgra nam mkha' la dengs zhes kyang bshad cing / glegs bam
du bris te nub phyogs u rgyan gyi yul du mkha' 'gro ma rnams kyis spyan drangs zhes kyang 'byung bas/ da lta mi yul na dngos su mi bzhugs par bshad la/ de gnyis snyigs
ma'i gdul bya rnams kyi spyod yul du ma gyur pa'i rgyu mtshan yang snyigs dus kyi gdul bya rnams tshe thung ba sogs dang / rgyud de gnyis rjod byed tshig gi tshogs shin tu
rgya che bas tshe de la thos bsam mi rdzogs shing / bsgom pa'i nyams len mi nus pas na mi snang bar byin gyis brlabs pa yin te/ shanti pa chen po'i gsung las/ de bas na
bsam gtan gyi ro ma myang bar thos pa dang bsam pa'i shes rab tsam la chags bzhin du 'chi ba'i dus byed par ma gyur cig snyam du dgongs pa'i ched du gzhung rgyas pa mi snang
bar byin gyis brlabs pa'o/ /zhes gsungs pas so/ /gnyis pa bshad pa'i rgyud gsungs pa'i tshul ni/ sangs rgyas mnyam sbyor gyi 'grel par/ gsang sngags rgyud don shin tu
rtogs dka' bas/ /bshad rgyud cha mthun sogs kyis bsgrub par bya/ /zhes dang / padma lcags kyus/ rtsa rgyud shin tu zab cing rtogs dka' bas/ /bshad rgyud cha mthun rgyud
kyis gsal bar bya/ /zhes rtsa rgyud kyi dgongs pa bshad rgyud kyis bkral dgos par gsungs shing / rtsa rgyud 'di nyid las kyang / dpa' bo 'di yi skad du ni/ /nga yi rgyud
rnams sbas pa yin/ /zhes lam dang 'bras bu'i gsang ba zab mo

rnams dpa' bo dang / dpa' mo'i brdas bcings shing sbas nas yod pa/ gzhan gang gis kyang dpag par dka' ba rnams/ gsang don de nyid dngos po yang / /gcig nas gcig brgyud shes
par bya/ /zhes zhal nas zhal/ snyan nas snyan du brgyud pa'i gdams pa zab mo dang / bshad rgyud la brten pa'i yo ga sam bha ra'i dgongs pa rtogs dgos par gzigs nas/ dpal
phyag na rdo rjes/ tshogs mchod sngon du 'gro ba'i sgo nas bshad rgyud rnams gsung bar gsol ba btab bo/ /gnas dang / dus dang / 'khor sogs rtsa rgyud dang 'dra ba la/ de'i
tshe ston pa rdo rje 'chang chen pos bshad rgyud rnams gsungs pa yin te/ de ltar gsungs pa'i bshad rgyud la gsang mtha'i lugs la bshad rgyud rtsod med du bzhed pa a bhi
dha na/ rdo rje mkha' 'gro/ kun spyod/ he ru ka mngon 'byung / sambu Ti ste lnga dang / gzhan yang mkha' 'gro rgya mtsho/ sdom 'byung / rnal 'byor ma bzhi'i kha sbyor sogs
spyir gyi bshad rgyud mang du yod pa las/ bshad rgyud ces pa yang rtsa rgyud kyi phyis su byung zhing 'chad byed yin pas na bshad rgyud ces bya zhing / bshad rgyud du
'gro tshul yang / mi gsal ba gsal bar byed pa/ ma tshang ba kha skong ba/ tshul mi 'dra ba cha mthun pas nges shes bskyed pa/ don bsdu ba/ tshig rnam par 'byed pa/ don rnam
par 'byed pa dang / bshad rgyud du 'gro ba'i tshul bdun nam/ yang tshig don rnam par 'byed pa ste phyi ma gnyis gcig tu byas nas drug tu slob dpon rin po che'i rgyud
sde spyi rnam las gsungs pa'i 'jog byed de dag

re re tsam gyis bshad rgyud du mi 'gyur zhing / de dag phal cher tshang na bshad rgyud du 'gyur bar bshad pa ltar/ rtsa rgyud du/ zhal bzhi pa la phyag bzhi pa/ /ji srid phyag
ni 'bum gyi bar/ /zhes bcom ldan 'das gtso 'khor rnams kyi mtshan tsam ma gtogs zhal phyag sogs gsal bar ma gsungs pa la/ de dag gsal bar ston pa'i bshad rgyud mngon
brjod bla ma'am/ a bhi dha na dang por gsungs shing / 'di la gleng gzhi yang yod par bshad la/ rgyud 'di nas dkyil 'khor sum cu so brgyad gsungs shing / de yang gtso bo 'pho
ba/ yab sbas pa dang / yum sbas pa/ rigs bsdus pa sogs kyi tshe dkyil 'khor drug brgya dang bdun cu rtsa gcig gi bskyed rim mi gsal ba yang gsal bar byed/ sbyang gzhi
skye gnas bzhi sbyong ba'i bskyed chog mi 'dra ba rnams kyang gsal bar byed cing / gzhung tshad le'u brgyad cu rtsa dgu pa 'dis rtsa rgyud kyi don phal cher gtan la phab
par bshad/ gzhan yang / rtsa rgyud du/ las chen bcu gnyis 'di dag ni/ /rtag tu bsgrub pa pos yi bsgrub/ /ces las tshogs kyi rkang grangs tsam gsungs pa la/ rdo rje mkha'
'gro las/ rdzas dang / sngags dang / ting nge 'dzin dang / 'khrul 'khor gyi sgo nas las tshogs rgyas par bstan pas na rgyud 'di ni ma tshang ba kha skong ba'i bshad rgyud
do/ /yang rtsa rgyud du/ de ltar de nyid bcu bzhi ni/ /mdor bsdus nas ni bshad pa yin/ /zhes de nyid bcu bzhi'i nyams len bsdus nas ston pa rnal 'byor ma kun tu spyod pa'i
rgyud ni/ don bsdus pa'i sgo nas bshad rgyud du 'jog pa yin la/

'di yongs su rdzogs pa la rtog pa drug cu rtsa bzhi yod par bshad cing / rtog pa re re la yang le'u bcu bdun bcu bdun yod pa'i da lta'i 'di nyer lnga pa 'khor lo 'byung ba'i
rtog pa zhes bya ba yin no/ /he ru ka mngon 'byung ni/ rdo rje phag mo'i rtsa sngags btu ba dang / gzhan yang rtsa sngags dang / snying po sogs la brten pa'i las tshogs
rnams dang / sgyu ma lta bu'i ting nge 'dzin rgyas par bshad pas bshad rgyud du 'gro bar bshad cing / 'di la le'u zhe lnga/ dkyil 'khor gsum bstan par bshad la/ dpal sambu
Ti ni/ gleng gzhi'i yi ge re re'i don nang rdo rje'i lus la sbas don du bshad cing / brtag pa drug pa'i rab byed bzhi pa las gtum mo dpyid thig bstan/ de kho na nyid sdom
pa'i le'u las phyag rgya chen po gsal bar bstan pas na rtsa rgyud nyung ngu 'di'i bshad rgyud du 'jog pa yin par gsungs so/ /gzhan yang mkha' 'gro rgya mtsho dang / sdom
'byung dang / rnal 'byor ma kha sbyor gyi rgyud rnams kyang bde mchog rtsa ba'i rgyud 'di'i bshad rgyud yin zhing / phyi ma 'dir rnal 'byor ma nyi shu rtsa bdun du bsdus
nas/ de'i sgrub thabs dang / dkyil 'khor gcig kyang bstan to/ /bu ston rin po ches 'di rtsa rgyud kyi le'u bcu bdun pa'i sgos kyi bshad rgyud yin par yang gsungs/ ngor
chen rdo rje 'chang kun dga' bzang po'i gsung rgyun 'ga' zhig las/ rgyud 'di ma rgyud yin/ de'i nang nas bde kye gnyis gang gi rgyud yin dpyad pa'i gzhir snang gsungs pa
yang 'byung la/ yang sdom 'byung ni 'grel par/ bsdus rgyud kyang yin/ rgyud phyi ma yang

shog grangs 'di'i mdun med la rgyab gnyis 'dug pas zhib dpyod gnas rogs yin/ bshad rgyud kyang yin par bshad cing / phag mo dngos grub 'byung ba ni/ a bhi dha na'i le'u bcu
gsum pa zur du phyung ba'am/ de dang don 'dra ba zhig yod par bshad/ rgyud 'di nas phag mo zhal bzhi phyag bcu gnyis ma'i gtso bo byas pa'i lha so bdun pa thams cad phyed
gzugs su byas pa'i dkyil 'khor zhig bstan par bshad do/ /gzhan yang sgyu ma bde mchog dang / sangs rgyas mnyam sbyor la sogs pa rnams kyang spyir bde mchog gi rgyud yin
par 'ga' zhig las bshad la/ ma hA nam mkha' dang mnyam pa che chung gnyis dang / ra li nam mkha' dang mnyam pa ste gsum po 'di dag ni/ 'gyur byang du ga ya dha ra dang /
'brog mi lo tsa bas bsgyur zer ba'i dpe 'ga' zhig snang yang / don la brdzus mar bzhed/ de'i rgyu mtshan yang / de nyid las/ 'khor ba'i chos ni dge ba ste/ /de las langs
pa dge slong yin/ /zhes pa dang / dur khrod la/ dur zhes pa chos nyid/ khrod ces pa de rtogs pa'i ye shes la bshad pa sogs mdo rgyud gang nas ma bshad pa'i nor ba yod pa'i
rgyu mtshan gyis rgyud rnam dag ma yin/ gnyos lo tsa bas bzos par mkhas pa rnams gsungs so/ /de ltar bde mchog gi rgyud mang du bshad pa de dag bsdu na rtsa rgyud bshad
rgyud gnyis su 'du bar kha cig bzhed/ 'ga' zhig de gnyis kyi steng du cha mthun gyi rgyud dang gsum du 'du bar 'dod la/ ra lugs ni rtsa rgyud dang / bshad rgyud/ yan lag
gi rgyud dang gsum du dbye ba dang / bsdu na de gsum du 'du bar yang bzhed de/ slob dpon a lang ka las rdo rje phreng ba'i 'grel par/ rtsa ba'i rgyud/ bshad pa'i rgyud/
yan lag gi rgyud dang gsum du bshad pa dang mthun par bla ma gong ma dag bzhed pas so/ /des na rtsa ba'i rgyud rgyas 'bring bsdus gsum/ bshad pa'i rgyud sum cu so gnyis/
yan lag gi rgyud bsam gyis mi khyab pa yod par gsungs pa yin no/ /de ltar 'khor lo bde mchog gi bshad rgyud kyi rnam grangs 'di la/ bu ston rin po ches/ de la mi thub zla
bas/ mkha' 'gro 'byung ba kun spyod dang / /de bzhin mtshan mchog bla ma'i rgyud/ /kha sbyor rgyud dang bzhi po ni/ /bshad pa'i rgyud du shes par bya/ /zhes gsungs shing
/ jo bo rjes kyang bshad rgyud bzhi ru bzhed la/ na ro pas he ru ka mngon 'byung dang lngar bzhed/ de'i slob ma dha ri pa zhes pas mkha' 'gro rgya mtsho dang / rnal 'byor
ma bzhi kha sbyor ba gnyis bsnan nas bdun du bzhed do zhes grags la/ sdom 'byung / 'grel par bsdus rgyud kyang yin/ rgyud phyi ma yang yin/ yang rgyud kyang yin par bshad
la/ phag mo dngos grub 'byung ba rgyud nyid las bshad rgyud du bshad de/ de ltar dgur 'gyur ro zhes gsungs nas/ mi thub zla ba dang / jo bo rje bshad rgyud bzhi/ na ro
pa lnga/ de'i slob ma dhA ri pa bdun du bzhed pa de dag kyang zhal gyis bzhes/ de dag gi steng du sdom 'byung dang / phag mo dngos grub 'byung ba dang dgur bzhed/ de la
rang phyogs

kyi mkhas pa rnams kyis gnod byed kyi lung rigs mang du 'god par mdzad nas/ rang lugs mi thub zla bas/ 'byung dang mkha' 'gro kun spyod dang / /kha sbyor rgyud dang bla ma
ste/ /bshad rgyud rnam pa lngar 'dod do/ /zhes gsungs pas/ he ru ka mngon 'byung / mkha' 'gro/ rnal 'byor ma kun spyod/ sambu Ti'am/ kun tu kha sbyor/ mngon brjod bla ma'am/
a bhi dha na dang lnga po bshad rgyud rnam par dag pa dang / gzhan rnams bshad rgyud min pa lta bu zhig gsungs/ yang 'ga' zhig tu gsang mtha'i bshad rgyud la lnga po
der nges kyang / spyir bde mchog gi bshad rgyud la mang du yod par bshad pa yang 'byung la/ yang bdag gi bla ma mkhan chen thams cad mkhyen pa ngag dbang chos grags kyi 'khor
lo bde mchog gi dri bar/ bde mchog rtsa ba'i rgyud la rgyud gzhan gyi/ /'grel tshul rnam bzhir bzhed na mnyam sbyor dang / /sdom 'byung mkha' 'gro rgya mtsho rtsa rgyud
kyi/ /gang gi thad du dgongs pa ji ltar 'grel/ /'di gsum bde mchog rtsa ba'i bshad rgyud du/ /'jog na 'jog byed chos rnams tshang ngam ci/ /'on te phan 'dogs tsam gyi
rgyud yin na/ /de la phan ni 'dogs tshul ji ltar yin/ /zhes dri ba'i gsung bkod nas/ de'i rang lan du/ lan dngos ni bde mchog sdom 'byung dang / mkha' 'gro rgya mtsho gnyis
ni bde mchog rtsa rgyud le'u lnga bcu rtsa gcig pa 'di'i bshad rgyud yin te/ bdag nyid chen po sa paN gyi chag lo tsa ba la gnang ba'i dris

lan las/ bde mchog nyung ngu bshad pa'i rgyud/ /mkha' 'gro rgya mtsho la sogs bdun/ /zhes gsungs pas grub cing / na ro pa'i slob ma rgya gar dha ri ka pa yang / slob dpon skar
rgyal zla bas gsungs pa'i bshad rgyud lnga po de'i steng du rnal 'byor ma bzhi'i kha sbyor gyi rgyud ces bya ba dang / mkha' 'gro rgya mtsho dang gnyis bsnan pas na ro
pa la bshad bka' bzhugs pa'i bshad rgyud bdun du bzhed cing / sdom 'byung ni na ro pa la bshad bka' mi bzhugs pa yin no zhes bzhed pas so/ /zhes sogs dang / 'o na sangs
rgyas mnyam sbyor sogs gang yin snyam na/ 'di ni ma rgyud spyi tsam pa yin te/ mkha' 'gro ma rdo rje gur gyi le'u bcu gsum pa las/ bcom ldan 'das ji ltar na rdo rje rnal
