thun bzhi'i rnal 'byor las skad cig kyang mi 'da' ba'i ngang las rgyud sde dang 'brel ba'i thugs dam chag med du ma nyin mtshan gyi cha so sor bgos te byang sems kyi mdzad
pa rlabs po che rtag par mdzad pas/ dngos brgyud kyi bla ma rnams dang / yi dam gyi lha mang pos 'dzum zhal legs par bstan/ chos skyong srung ma rnams kyis ji ltar bsgos
pa'i 'phrin las bzhi thogs med du bsgrubs shing / de las kyang mchog tu gyur pa snang ba thams cad rgyal ba'i dkyil 'khor du nye bar gzigs pa'i gnyis med kyi ye shes mnga'
bas ji ltar ji snyed kyi don ma lus pa mngon du gyur pa nyid yin no/ /de ltar bstan pa rin po che la bshad pa dang sgrub pa gnyis sam/ 'chad rtsod rtsom gsum gyi bgyi ba
rlabs po che gzhal bar dka' ba zhig mdzad de/ dgung lo don bdun pa 'brug gi lo zla ba dang po'i nyer dgu'i tho rangs dgon gnas chen po bsam grub gling nas dag pa'i zhing
mchog bde ba can du gshegs so/ /rje btsun 'jam pa'i dbyangs 'di la slob ma'i mchog ches mang / 'dir gtso bor gyur pa ni/ rje btsun sa lo tsa ba chen po ste/ 'di ni dang
por 'phags pa 'jam dpal dang / bar du rigs ldan 'jam dpal grags pa/ tha mar bdag nyid chen po sa skya paNDi ta nyid slar yang rje btsun sa skya pa'i gdung gi rigs dam par
sprul te gdan sa chen por rtse gdong du sku bltams/ dgung lo bcu gcig pa'i tshe glo bo mkhan chen bsod nams lhun grub las dge bsnyen zhus/ rje dkon mchog 'phel bas rab
tu byung /

dgung lo bcu gnyis pa la nye ba'i tshe rgyal sras lam bzang gi dga' ston spel zhing / bzhi thog gi gdan seng ge'i khrir 'khod/ bco lnga pa'i tshe yongs 'dzin dkon mchog 'phel
gyi bka' stsal spyi bor blangs te kyai rdor dang / rdo rje phur pa/ gur mgon rnams kyi gsung bsnyen mdzad pas lha so so'i zhal gzigs te grangs dang mtshan ma'i bsnyen
pa mthar phyin/ nyi shu pa'i tshe mkhan po dkon mchog 'phel ba/ las slob 'jam dbyangs sangs rin/ gsang ston ra ston yon tan 'byung gnas rnams las bsnyen par rdzogs/ mkhan
slob de dag dang / gzhan yang zhwa lu lo chen/ chag lo rin chen chos rgyal sogs snga phyir yongs 'dzin mang po'i zhabs pad gus pas bsten so so'i zhal gyi bum pa las/ mdo
rgyud kyi zab gnad mang po'i bdud rtsi ngom par gsol/ yongs 'dzin dkon mchog 'phel/ 'jam dbyangs sangs rgyas rin chen/ mkhan chen 'jam pa'i dbyangs dang gsum po 'di bla
ma'i mchog tu bzung / de lta'i yongs 'dzin dag las mnos pa'i gsung gi gsang ba zab mo'i rgyun de/ slar yang skal ldan dag la legs par 'dom pa'i tshul ni/ blo bzang khyod
kyi mkhyen pa'i ded dpon gyis/ /mkhas grub zhal gyi chu gter las blangs pa'i/ /dbang lung man ngag yid bzhin rin chen gyis/ /zab yangs thugs kyi bang mdzod legs bkang nas/
/slar yang skye dgu'i dbul ba sel ba'i phyir/ /rgyud sde rnam bzhi'i dgongs don

rin chen mchog /rdo rje phreng ba kri ya sa munytsar/ /legs par bshad pa'i dkyil 'khor zhe lnga dang / /ngan song sbyong ba'i dkyil 'khor bcu dang gnyis/ /rnam dag zur bka'
lnga bcu rtsa gcig ste/ /smin byed dbang gi rnam grangs brgya dang brgyad/ /grol byed khrid kyi rim pa nyi shu bdun/ /snyan brgyud zab mo'i byin rlabs nyer gnyis lhag /rjes
su gnang ba'i bka' srol chen po gnyis/ /rjes gnang zur bkar grags pa bzhi bcu lhag /rgya bod mkhas pa'i dgongs 'grel dang bcas pa'i/ /zab rgyas rgyud sde'i bshad bka'
bcu gsum dang / /so thar byang sems sdom pa bslab byar bcas/ /sgra dang snyan ngag sdeb sbyor dkar rtsis dang / /bka' dang bstan bcos glegs bam rab 'byams kyi/ /dag gsal
lung gi bka' drin dang bcas pa/ /mtha' yas gdul bya'i bsam pa ji lta bar/ /stsol mdzad chos kyi sbyin bdag che ba po/ /zhes pa ltar ro/ /chos kyi rnam grangs de dag kyang
yang nas yang du ston par mdzad pas bstan 'dzin bskrun pa'i grangs ni bgrang bar mi spobs pa tsam byon la/ de lta'i skabs nas rgyud sde zab mo dang 'brel ba'i thugs dam
nyams bzhes kyi rim pa yang bsam gyis mi khyab pa zhig rtag par mdzad cing / khyad par bla med kyi lam gyi snying po rim pa gnyis kyi ting nge 'dzin la skad cig kyang g.yel
ba mi mnga' bas/ gnas skabs su bla ma yi dam chos skyong sogs kyis zhal bstan cing rjes su bzung ba'i mtshan ma yang bsam gyis mi khyab ste/ dgung lo nyi

shu rtsa grangs kyi skabs rtse gdong du rdo rje phur ba gtso bor gyur pa'i nyams bzhes mdzad skabs/ sa bir zhal sprod/ rdo rje phur pa/ bla ma dam pa bsod nams rgyal mtshan
rnams kyi zhal gzigs/ so gnyis pa'i tshe na lendrar gsung gi bdud rtsi stsal rjes gtsang phyogs la phebs pa'i yar lam srin po ri mjal dus srin po ri'i sku de bde mchog zhal
bzhi phyag bcu gnyis par gzigs/ yang skabs shig mus bsam gtan phug tu rje 'dis lo gcig gi sgrub pa mdzad pa'i tshe bde mchog lha lnga/ rje btsun rin po che/ mus chen
sangs rin birWa pa'i rnam par gzigs/ de dus gsung las/ rje sangs rgyas rin chen 'di dus kyi min pa/ sems dpa' chen po las kyang 'jigs pa 'dug gsungs/ dge sding mgon khang
du gur mgon lcam dral/ las mkhan pu tra chen po dang bcas pa gzigs te 'phrin las 'bad med du bsgrub pa'i mtshan ma byung nas/ mgon po 'khor bcas kyi bstod pa dang / lha
mo'i bskangs gso 'di yang de dus mdzad/ yang bse mgon gyi drung du thugs dam rgyun ring mdzad skabs shig sa bir gnyis kyis so so'i sku'i bkod pa drug gi ngo mtshar gyi gzigs
snang bstan de gnyis ngo bo gcig tu rtogs/ byas 'gyur rdo rje'i brag rdzong du rje btsun rin po che dang rdo rje lha mo sogs gzigs/ lhag par 'ja' 'od kyi gur khang du
chos rje sa skya paNDi tas 'dzum zhal bstan pas nyams 'phar te/ phyi rol tu sku

lus kyi rnam 'gyur ci yang zhig ston par mdzad/ gdan sa chen po'i mkha' spyod gzim chung du nub cig gi mtshan lam du sa chen dang / 'jam dbyangs paNDi ta'i cha lugs can zhig
birWa pa/ sa paN/ slob dpon nag po spyod pa ba rnams 'bel ba'i gtam mdzad pa'i drung du bdag nyid kyang 'khod de/ dam pa'i chos la the tshom gyi dra ba mang du bcad/ nag
po spyod pa nyid la bde mchog gi zab bcud du ma gsan/ gzhung drug rdzogs mtshams mnal sad/ yang lan cig rgod tshang phug par rnal 'byor ma'i zhal gzigs shing / phyis dus
mkha' spyod du gzim chung der nyams bzhes rgyun mi thung ba zhig mdzad pa'i skabs shig bde ba can gyi zhing khams na rgyal ba 'od dpag med dang / sa chen yab sras sogs
dang / rje sangs rgyas rin chen rnams bzhugs pa gzigs/ der khri gnyis 'dug pa'i gcig tu rje 'di bzhugs/ gcig tu gzhan zhig phebs rgyu yin zer/ de dus 'od gsal chen po'i ngang
du 'od dpag med la chos kyi bdud rtsi ci yang gsol/ slar ha cang mi ring ba na glo bo mkhan chen dag pa'i zhing du gshegs pas sngar gyi mnal lam de la lta ba 'dug gsungs/
lha sa'i jo bo mjal bar phebs dus chu bo chen po'i 'jigs pa byung ba/ bla ma dang chos skyong gi rnam 'phrul gyis de las grol ba dang / gzhan yang 'bab rong gi gnas
su dgun dus 'jam dbyangs me tog mtshar sdug mang po gsar du skyes te/ 'jam dbyangs dang thugs mi gnyis

pa'i mtshan ma yang bstan/ de ltar nges don du mgon po 'jam pa'i dbyangs nyid gnas lnga rig pa'i paNDi ta'i tshul bzung bas na chos rje 'di'i mkhas pa'i yon tan ni 'di'o zhes
so so skye bo dag gis nam yang brjod par mi spobs la/ btsun pa'i yon tan ni sdom pa gsum gyis bslab pa la nyes pa'i dri phra mos kyang ma gos shing / bzang po'i yon tan
ni bdag nyid bgrang bar mi nus pa'i yon tan kun gyi rtser son kyang / mngon par khengs pa'i dri tsam yang mi mnga' bar thugs mchog tu zhi bas gzhan gyi khro bo la 'di'i
sku mthong ba tsam gyis zhi 'gro ba zhig yin par 'dug go /de ltar mkhas btsun bzang gsum gyi yon tan dang ldan pa'i bdag nyid chen po de nyid kyis dgung lo bcu gcig nas
zhe brgyad kyi bar du bstan pa rin po che'i bya ba 'ba' zhig mdzad de/ zhe dgu pa chu sbrul zla ba drug pa'i yar tshes bcu'i nyin gdan sa chen po'i bla brang rin chen sgang
du zhi bar gshegs so/ /de la slob ma'i rnam grangs bgrang bar dka' ba zhig byon mod kyang / kun gyi gtsug rgyan dam par gyur pa ni sngags 'chang chos kyi rgyal po ngag
dbang kun dga' rin chen bkra shis grags pa rgyal mtshan dpal bzang po ste/ bstan pa'i nyi ma chen po de nyid me mo glang lor bltams/ dgung lo bcu bdun gyi bar du sa lo chen
po'i zhabs pad 'bral med du bsten/ gsung gi bdud rtsi ngom par gsol zhing bu gcig pa ltar bskyangs/ gzhan yang rje btsun mkhas pa'i dbang po dkon mchog lhun grub/ 'phags
chen dpal ldan

bkra shis/ spyan snga ngag dbang chos grags/ ngor chen sangs rgyas seng ge paN chen legs blo la sogs pa yongs 'dzin mang po'i zhabs pad spyi bo'i rgyan du bkod de/ dbang khrid
lung byin rlabs rjes gnang sogs grangs med pa zhig mnos te gsan pa rgya mtsho'i mdzod bzung / byas 'gyur rdo rje'i brag rdzong la sogs pa'i gnas mchog mang por bde kye/
yang phur sogs yi dam du ma dang / gur zhal sogs chos srung mang po'i grangs dang mtshan ma'i bsnyen pa mthar phyin par mdzad pas mthu stobs dang nus pa'i bdag nyid du
gyur/ dam can rgya mtsho bran bzhin 'khol/ spyi dang bye brag gi bstan pa'i dgra bgegs tshar bcad/ de dag gi ma 'ongs pa'i srid pa'i rgyun kyang bcad rjes su bzung / gzhan
yang rang snang du dag pa rab 'byams las ma g.yos kyang / gzhan snang du bstan 'gro'i phyir sku srog kyang gtong ba la mi zhum pa'i rgyal sras kyi spyod pa rlabs po che
khur du khyer te/ dka' spyad drag pos phyi nang gi bstan pa'i 'gal rkyen kun bsal nas lha mi thams cad dbang du bsdus/ rje btsun gong ma dag gi byin gyis brlabs pa'i bod
kyi rdo rje gdan dpal ldan sa skya'i gtsug lag khang rnams skye bo mi srun pa dag gi byed pas bar skabs su nyams pa dag gsos/ sku gsung thugs kyi rten dang / de dag mchod
pa'i yo byad kyang mang du phul/ gzhan yang gtsug lag khang dang / rten mchod ngo mtshar can mang po gsar du yang spel/ khyad

par bstan pa'i rtsa ba dge 'dun gyi sde chen po thub bstan lha chen dang / bde ba chen po'i gling sogs legs par btab/ bstan pa dang mkhas pa'i bya ba rnam pa drug gi sgo nas
rgyal bstan yar ngo'i zla ba ltar spel/ gzhan yang bla ma gong ma'i dgongs pa rdzogs thabs su bde dges gsang gsum yang phur sogs kyi dkyil 'khor sgrub mchod rgyud sde dang
mthun pa'i phyag len gyis brgyan pa mang po'i rgyun yang spel te/ mdor na zhi rgyas dbang drag gi 'phrin las bzhi'i thabs la mkhas pa sna tshogs pas gdul bya dag gang
la gang 'dul gyi tshul gyis legs par bskyangs te 'dzin ma'i khyon 'di rdzogs ldan gyi bde ba la bkod pas chos rgyal mes dbon sogs kyi rjes su bod kha ba can gyi ljongs 'dir
bstan pa'i bya ba rlabs chen mdzad pa la bdag nyid chen po 'di las ngo mtshar ba gzhan ma byung bar yongs su grags pa yin no/ /de ltar bstan pa dang sems can gyi don
bsam gyis mi khyab pa zhig mdzad de/ dgung lo re brgyad bzhes pa shing sprel zla ba bdun pa'i yar tshes bcu gnyis kyi nyin gdan sa chen po'i bla brang lha khang chen mo dang
nye ba'i lhun grub pho brang du zhi bar gshegs so/ /skyes chen de la slob bu mang du byon pa'i nang nas/ chos dang rigs sras kyi thu bo ni kho bo cag gi 'dren pa dam
pa grub pa'i dbang phyug puNya indra dang / rgyal sras sems dpa' chen po grags pa'i mtshan can

te/ yab sras 'di gsum gyi rnam thar rgyas pa ni kho bos logs su bkod yod pas rtogs par 'dod pa dag gis de dag tu blta'o/ /byang sems bo dhi sa twa'i rnam sprul yab rje sbas
pa'i sangs rgyas sngags 'chang grags pa'i mtshan can las kho bo cag gi 'dren pa dam pa sa bcu'i byang sems chen po budha ratna'i rnam par sprul pa rgyal ba mus pa chen po
rdo rje 'chang sangs rgyas rgyal mtshan zhes mtshan yongs su grags pa de nyid kyis 'khor lo bde mchog nag po lugs kyi smin byed kyi dbang bskur ba zab mo legs par gsan
cing / dam pa de nyid kyi drung du kho bo cag gis thob pa'i tshul ni 'og tu 'chad do/ /yang mus chen sems dpa' chen po dkon mchog rgyal mtshan la spyir bstan 'dzin gyi slob
bu nam mkha'i skar phran lta bu ches mang ba zhig byon zhing / khyad par 'khor lo bde mchog gi rgyud pa 'dzin pa yang yongs rdzogs mkhas pa'i dbang po go rams chen po/
grub pa'i sa la bzhugs pa dkon mchog blo gros/ snyan brgyud gdams pa'i gter chen zhwa lu ba sangs rgyas dpal bzang sogs mang du byon pa las/ kun mkhyen chen po ni ston pa
'das nas lo sum stong lnga brgya dang re gnyis lon pa'i tshe mdo khams su byon/ dgung lo bcu pa'i tshe byang sems kun dga' 'bum la rab tu byung / de nas dgung lo bcu dgu
bzhes kyi bar du mkhan po de dang / go ram shes rab dpal ba sogs bsten te/ gzhung chen bcu gsum mgrin pa'i lam nas rgyu zhing ldon par mdzad de/ go rab

'byams pa zhes snga mo nyid nas grags/ nyi shu pa'i tshe go rab shes rab dpal gyis/ rab 'byams la sogs bshes gnyen brgya rtsa gcig brgya 'bul gyi rnam grangs mang du bkod pa'i
dkyus kyi thog mar bkod de/ rong ston chen po dgung lo brgyad cu rtsa gnyis pa/ chos grwa na lendra btab nas lo bcu gsum lon pa'i tshe phul/ rong ston chen po'i gsung
gi bcud myangs te/ lo gnyis lon pa na rong ston chen po dag pa'i zhing du gshegs/ de'i tshe 'bras yul skyid tshal gyi chos grwa gsar du btsugs pa'i dus/ byams chen rab 'byams
pa'i zhabs kyi padmor gtugs/ lo ngo lnga la mdo phyogs kyi gnad ma lus pa'i sgro 'dogs bcad de/ nyer lnga pa'i lo e wa~M chos ldan du rdo rje 'chang kun dga' bzang
po'i zhabs pad bsten/ nyer gcig pa'i tshe ngor chen rdo rje 'chang / sems dpa' chen po dkon mchog rgyal mtshan/ sdom brtson sangs rgyas dpal bzang rnams kyis mkhan po dang
las gsang mdzad de bsnyen par rdzogs/ lo bzhi'i bar ngor chen nyid la gsung ngag sogs rgyud man ngag gsan/ nyer dgu pa'i tshe ngor chen dag pa'i zhing du gshegs nas/ sems
dpa' chen po sogs yongs 'dzin du ma las rgyud man ngag gi zab bcud blangs te lo ngo bzhi la rgyud man ngag gi sgro 'dogs bcad de/ so gnyis pa'i tshe mdo khams phyogs su
'byon pa'i dgongs pa gtad de/ 'bras yul du phebs pa na rab 'byams chos rjes thugs brtse'i lcags

kyus bzung ste/ so gsum pa nas so drug pa'i bar 'bras yul gyi zur 'chad pa mdzad de blo gsal dag gi yid gsos/ kyai rdo rje'i gzhi bsnyen dang / sdom gsum Tika chen/ yum don
rab gsal sogs rtsom pa'i sgo yang phye/ slar yang mus chen nyid kyi thugs rje'i zhags pas drangs te/ so bdun pa'i tshe mus su byon 'khor lo bde mchog gi chos skor sogs zab
chos mang du gsan/ gsang 'dus rtsod spongs sogs mdzad/ so brgyad pa'i tshe mus chen chos rgyal rnam rgyal grags bzang gis byang ngam ring du spyan drangs pa'i zhabs 'bring
du 'khod de/ blo gsal 'ga' la legs bshad kyi skyes dang / kun rig dang / kyai rdor rtsod spongs sogs rtsom gyi me tog kha phye/ lo de la blo gsal don gnyer bcu phrag
bzhi dang bcas rin spungs nang so dpon blon gyis mthun pa'i rkyen sbyar te rta nag gser gling du chos kyi grwa btsugs/ de nas bzung dgung lo zhe lnga'i bar lo brgyad kyi
ring la blo gsal ha cang mang ba ma yin pa'i don gnyer sha stag la 'chad pa'i dbyangs kyis ngal gsos/ zhe lnga pa de nyid la chos grwa chen po thub bstan rnam rgyal btab/
'dus pa'i tshogs chen po la mdo sngags kyi dga' ston ngo mtshar rmad du byung bas/ spyir bstan pa'i snying po khyad par sdom rig gi bstan pa rma med pa sor chud/ lnga bcu
rtsa lnga pa'i tshe e wa~M chos ldan gyi gdan sa mdzad de/ nga dgu'i bar lo ngo bzhir rdo rje 'chang yab sras kyi dgongs pa rdzogs par mdzad/ yongs 'dzin dkon mchog 'phel
rgyal tshab tu dbang bskur te/ slar yang thub

bstan rnam rgyal nyid du phebs skal ldan rnams la mdo sngags kyi bka' drin stsal/ re gcig pa'i tshe dpal ldan sa skyar chos kyi dga' ston spel/ tshur lam sngon mo rdzong du
chos kyi bdud rtsi stsol ba'i tshe zhi bar gshegs so/ /dam pa de nyid las yongs 'dzin dkon mchog 'phel bas 'khor lo bde mchog sogs rgyud man ngag gi bcud ngom par gsol zhing
/ 'di ni mkhas btsun bzang gsum gyi yon tan phul du brnyes shing / rdo rje 'chang gi gdan sar bzhugs te gsung ngag sogs chos tshul mtha' yas pa'i bshad sgrub kyi sgo
nas bstan pa'i 'dzin skyong dang / gdul bya skal ldan mang po smin grol la bkod/ rje btsun sa skya pa'i gdung rgyud mang po'i bla mar gyur pas 'phrin las kyang nam mkha'
dang mnyam pa'i yongs 'dzin dam pa gnyis ka yin no/ /yang grub chen dkon mchog blo gros ni/ sems dpa' chen po nyid kyi sku'i dbon po mus chen nyid las rab tu byung zhing
/ gsung gi bdud rtsi legs par gsol bas gsan pa rgya mtsho lta bu mnga'/ gling dga' bde ba can du 'chad nyan gyi sgo nas bstan 'gro'i don dpag tu med pa mdzad cing / sems
dpa' chen po la chos rgyal nam mkha' rdo rje bas/ rje'i zhal slob bdag tsho'i bla ma'i 'os mus na ci 'dra bdog zhus pas/ bdag gi tsha bo dkon mchog blo gros zhes pa dbang
dang byin rlabs bskur mkhas pa lam sna zin tsam zhig dang / slob dpon sangs rgyas dpal bzang zhes pa spyi dang bye brag gi chos la mkhas pa

zhig bdog pas de gnyis la bcol bas yong ba yod gsungs pas gdul bya'i snang ngor yang lam sna zin par yongs su grags shing / rim gnyis kyi nyams bzhes zab mo las skad cig kyang
g.yel ba mi mnga' bas ting nge 'dzin gyi rtogs pa brtan cing mngon par mkhyen pa thogs med du mnga' ba'i grub pa'i dbang phyug chen po 'khor lo bde mchog gi chos skor
'di la bka' drin mchog tu che ba zhig yin no/ /de ltar kun mkhyen chen po dang / yongs 'dzin dkon mchog 'phel/ grub chen dkon blo dang gsum char gyis rjes su bzung zhing
rgyud byin gyis brlabs pa ni 'jam dbyangs sangs rgyas rin chen te/ 'di ni mus chen sems dpa' chen po'i dbon po zhig gi sras yin zhing / chu mo bya lo mus stod gling skyar
'khrungs/ bcu gcig pa'i tshe sems dpa' chen po la dge tshul zhus gsung ngag lan gsum dang / bde mchog gsang 'dus sogs zab chos mang pos bdag blo'i bum pa gang bar mdzad/
kun mkhyen chen po'i drung du/ phar tshad 'dul ba sdom gsum sogs pa mang po la gsan sbyong dang / khyad par gsung ngag tshar gsum/ bde mchog gi dbang khrid rgyud bshad
sogs mang po'i bcud myangs/ grub chen dkon blo la lam 'bras tshar drug sogs zab dgu'i chos kyi dga' ston thob/ rgyun gyi nyams bzhes gtso bor lam 'bras kyi thun bzhi dang
'khor lo bde mchog la mdzad cing / rim gnyis kyi rtogs pa mchog tu brtan/ dngos dang

mnal lam du bla ma dang yi dam mang po'i zhal gzigs/ ma 'ongs pa mkhyen pa'i mngon shes mnga'/ bstan pa'i bya ba rgyud sde nas bshad pa'i dkyil 'khor zur bka' brgyad cu rtsa
gnyis tsam gyi dbang lan grangs du ma dang / gsung ngag lam 'bras tshar lnga bcu nga gcig gzhan byin rlabs rjes gnang lung bshad sogs bsam gyis mi khyab cing / rab byung
bsnyen rdzogs sogs mdzad pa ni bgrang bar mi bzod pas 'phrin las nam mkha' dang mnyam pa'i sgo nas skal ldan mang po smin par mdzad de/ dgung lo don gnyis pa shing pho
spre'u'i lo khrums zla ba'i tshes bcu'i tho rangs rgyud sde nas bshad pa'i 'da' kha ma zab mo gsal btab ste/ mdun gyi nam mkhar bla ma yi dam mkha' 'gro'i tshogs bzhugs pa
la spyan gyis gzigs nas nam mkha' mdzod kyi phyag rgya mdzad bzhin par dgongs pa 'od gsal phyag rgya chen po'i ngang du thim pa'i tshul bstan/ de nas tshes bcu gnyis kyi
tho rangs thugs dam las bzhengs nas thogs pa med par bde ba can na rje bla ma yab sras bzhugs pa'i drung du gshegs so/ /dam pa de nyid kyi drung du sa lo thams cad mkhyen
pas 'khor lo bde mchog gi chos skor kyang yongs su rdzogs pa gsan pa yin te/ sa lo nyid kyi gsung las/ 'jig rten dbang phyug budha ratna las/ /sngar gyi gdams ngag phal
cher bskyar nas zhus/ /zhes glo bo mkhan chen sogs la sngar gsan pa'i bde mchog gi chos skor rnams slar yang rje nyid la gsan par gsungs pas so/ /yang mus chen

sems dpa' chen po'i thugs sras snyan brgyud gdams pa'i gter chen zhwa lu ba sangs rgyas dpal bzang ni yon tan rin po che du ma'i 'byung gnas dpal sa skya nas shar phyogs su
dpag tshad 'ga' zhig bgrod pa'i cha dpal rnam zhes bya ba'i char 'khrungs/ dgung lo dgu pa'i tshe yongs 'dzin dpal skyong ba dang / slob dpon kun dga' dpal bzang / mkhas
dbang grags pa rgyal mtshan rnams las zhwa lur rab byung zhus/ bcu dgu'i bar du mkhan po de las lung rigs kyi bcud blangs/ nyi shu pa la sngar gyi mkhan slob sogs las bsnyen
rdzogs zhus/ slob dpon kun dpal ba'i drung du dbu ma/ mngon pa/ byams chos sogs sde snod la sbyangs pa lhur mdzad de gzhung chen bcu la grwa skor gyi dga' ston spel/
de lta'i skabs shig nas chos grwa brang mo che'i slob dpon lo bdun gyi bar mdzad/ slar byams mgon gnyis pa sems dpa' chen po gzhon nu rgyal mchog gi drung du gangs bu ler
byon/ thar pa'i rtsa ba byang chub kyi sems lugs gnyis kyi cho gas thugs su chud par mdzad/ sde snod kyi bshad pa'i bka' bgrang bar mi bzod pa zhig dang / pha rol tu phyin
pa'i lam gyi snying po'i zab khrid du ma'i bcud 'thungs shing rje de'i zhabs 'bring pa rgyun mi thung tsam zhus skabs/ rje mus chen sems dpa' chen po dang mjal/ thog
mar rong ston gyi phar phyin khrid yig gis lung khrid kyi chos kyi sgo phye/ de mtshams sems dpa'

chen po gzhon nu rgyal mchog dga' ldan du phebs pa na/ rdo rje theg pa'i myur lam du 'jug 'dod kyi 'dun pas bskul te mus su rje sems dpa' chen po dkon mchog rgyal mtshan bzhugs
pa'i drung du gdan btegs/ zhabs pad yun ring du bsten bde kye gsang gsum gtso bor gyur pa'i rgyud man ngag gi zab bcud ngoms par gsol/ dgung lo lnga bcu pa'i tshe yum
gshegs te rje sems dpa' chen po la der 'gro bar zhus pas/ phyin nas phan rgyu med/ de bas ma'i don du bde mchog gi bsnyen pa gyis gsungs pas bka'i cod pan spyi bor bcings
pas/ 'od gsal du yum 'khor ba nas drangs pa'i mtshan ma brnyes/ gzhan yang yon tan gyi khyad par bdag gzhan gyi bde sdug dngos su brje nus/ bskyed rim la brtan pa thob/
rdzogs rim mngon du gyur pas/ rje mus chen 'khor lo bde mchog tu gsal bar gzigs/ grub chen dkon blo la gur mgon bcu gnyis ma'i rjes gnang gi zab gnad nod pa'i tshe mgon
de gur mgon nyid du mngon sum du gzigs shing / de nyid kyis kyang rje 'di kye rdor du gsal bar snang ba sogs rtogs pa'i yon tan dpag tu med/ gzhan don mdzad pa'i tshe yang
dge bsnyen/ dge tshul/ dge slong sogs bskrun pa'i grangs ni bgrang ba las 'das shing / phar phyin lam gyi rtsa ba theg chen sems bskyed gsang sngags lam gyi rtsa ba smin
byed kyi dbang bskur ba/ grol byed kyi khrid ston pa/ rnam dag rgyud kyi bshad bka' sogs

kyang mtha' yas pa zhig stsol ba la thogs pa med pas lung gi yon tan gyi mdzod mnga'/ rje nyid ya ma'i gdan sar bzhugs dus/ rje sems dpa' chen pos kyang da lta ya ma phu na
bla mas 'chad shes/ slob mas nyan shes pa'i 'chad nyan rnam dag de yod pa yin zhes bstod bkur gyi bsngags pa'i sgra dbyangs sgrog par mdzad/ mdor na dgung lo dgu pa la rab
tu byung ba nas/ re bzhi pa'i bar du bstan pa rin po che'i bya ba kho na mdzad de/ sa phag hor zla bcu gnyis pa'i gnam stong gi nyin dpal ngam ring gi rgyal khab chen
por ngo mtshar rmad du byung ba'i rnam 'phrul mang po dang bcas te sku thim pa'i tshul bstan/ de nas cho 'phrul zla ba'i tshes brgyad kyi bar zhal dkyil gzi mdangs dang ldan
zhing 'od zer 'phro ba dang / ngam ring rtse shod thams cad drod kyis khyab ste yon chab dang zhal zas sogs kyang mi 'khyag pa dang / de nas tshes brgyad kyi tho rangs
thugs dam de las grol te/ rje sems dpa' chen po bzhugs pa'i drung bde ba can du gshegs so/ /de nas sngar bzhin yon chab sogs kyang 'khyag pa zhig byung bas kun gyis ngo
mtshar du 'dzin pa byung zhes thos so/ /de la slob ma'i mchog mang yang / dpal 'khor lo sdom pa'i bka' 'dzin pa ni mnga' ris pa dpal ldan rgyal po ste/ 'di ni chu mo glang
gi lo mnga' ris stod kyi phyogs su 'khrungs/ dgung lo dgu pa'i tshe bla ma bsam gtan dpal ba las rab tu byung / slob

dpon chos skyong rdo rje la phar tshad sogs bslabs te gdan sa chen por grogs nyis brgya tsam dang 'grogs te phar phyin la bshad pa'i dga' ston mdzad/ de dus rje ngor chen kun
dga'i mtshan dang mjal/ rnam par rgyal ma'i rjes gnang sogs mnos/ rje ngor chen gyis tshe ring ba sogs kyi lung bstan gyi bdud rtsi stsal/ rje de la mi phyed pa'i dad
pa thob/ 'di'i chos lugs dpyid phyin par mdzad dgongs pa'i dam 'cha' brtan po bzung / slar mnga' ris su byon slob dpon chos skyong rdo rje'i drung du 'dul ba sogs kyi gzhung
lugs 'ga' la gsan sbyongs mdzad/ bla ma bsam gtan dpal ba la bde mchog gi dbang byin rlabs sogs ci rigs gsan/ dgung lo bco brgyad pa'i tshe slar yang dbus gtsang du phebs
pa'i 'dun pa shar ba'i nub cig 'bum gyi po ti gsol ba dang / dung zhig bus pas sgras dbus gtsang khengs pa sogs snyan pa chen pos phyogs thams cad khyab pa'i mtshan
ma brnyes te/ dbus gtsang du byon kun mkhyen nam bsod chen po la phar tshad mngon 'dul byams chos sogs gsan sbyongs mdzad/ de lta'i bar skabs dag tu rje ngor chen la kye
rdor sogs kyi dbang bka' 'ga' re dang / mkhas grub bstan gsal las tshad ma gsan pa sogs mdzad/ de mtshams shig na rje nam bsod gshegs pa'i rjes kyi dgongs rdzogs sogs grub
par mdzad/ dgung lo so drug pa'i tshe sngar gyi

yi dam brtan po gsos btab ste/ rje ngor pa'i ring lugs las 'ongs pa'i zab bcud dag gsol bar dgongs nas/ gling dga' bde ba can na rje mus chen bzhugs pa'i drung du byon te/
thog mar rje sems dpa' chen pos mkhan po/ las slob rje kun dga' dbang phyug gsang ston grub chen dkon blo rnams las bsnyen par rdzogs/ de nas mkhan po de la gsung ngag sogs
zab bcud mang du mnos/ skabs der rje sems dpa' chen po gshegs pas/ sems dpa' chen po dkon mchog 'bangs dang dkon mchog rgyal mtshan gnyis kyi sras kyi thu bo/ rje sangs
rgyas dpal bzang ya ma bde ldan phug na bzhugs pa'i spyan sngar phebs te/ de nyid la 'khor lo bde mchog gtso bor gyur pa'i rgyud man ngag gi zab gnad bum pa gang byo'i
tshul du gsan/ spyir yang bde mchog gsan pa'i bla ma drug tsam bsten te chos skor 'di'i bdag po lta bur gyur/ gzhan yang bdag chen blo gros rgyal mtshan/ chos rje gung ru/
kun mkhyen chen po/ grub chen dkon blo/ rje dpal ldan rdo rje/ srad pa kun blo sogs yongs 'dzin du ma'i zhabs pad bsten gsan pa rgya mtsho'i mthar son/ de dag gi nang nas
srad pa kun blo 'di 'phral kun spyod rtsing ba 'dra zhig yod pas/ rje 'dis bla ma 'di la lam skor phyi ma gsan pa'i tshe thugs la 'di la ngor chen gyi man ngag snyan brgyud
ma chad pa rang e yod dam snyam pa zhig 'khrungs pa'i nub

mo mnal lam du rje ngor chen byon snye ma drung mo 'ga' yar zhig bsnams nas/ rtse mo rje 'di la gtad/ rtsa ba ngor chen rang gis bzung ste phar 'then tshur 'then mang du mdzad
kyang ma chad pa zhig byung bas snyan brgyud ma chad par yod pa thugs yid ches/ de ltar thos pa dag gi don yang / dben gnas bsam gtan phug ya ma bde ldan/ stag lung ri
khrod/ bsam lding / lung chung dpal gyi ri khrod sogs su sgom pa la rtse gcig tu bzhugs pa mang du mdzad pas tha mal gyi snang ba thams cad rang tshugs mi thub pa ban bun
mer mer du 'char ba sogs rtogs pa phul du byung ba thugs rgyud la 'khrungs/ bla ma dang lhag pa'i lhas zhal bstan pa'i tshul yang / nub cig mnal lam du mi sngon po thod
skam can cig byung nas/ nag po pa'i dbang dgos na mgyogs par shog zer ba zhig byung nas/ nangs par ya mar rje sangs rgyas dpal bzang bzhugs pa'i drung du phyin pas/ der
rje de nyid nag po pa'i dbang bskur gyi kha gso'i bsnyen pa la bzhugs te/ nangs par nag po pa'i sta gon gnang rgyu'i skabs su 'byor te yi dam gyis lung bstan par dgongs/
de ltar thugs dam nyams bzhes la skad cig kyang mi g.yel ba'i ring nas gsung ngag lan grangs bcu bdun/ dag pa gsum gyi khrid tshar lnga/ bde mchog lU nag dril gsum gyi bskyed
rdzogs kyi khrid tshar mang po/ gzhan yang blo sbyong sogs kyi khrid bka' dang / bde dges

gnyis sogs rgyud bshad du ma dang bcas 'chad pa'i dga' ston spel ba yang dpag tu med/ bshad pa de rnams kyang gong ma'i gsung dang mi 'gal zhing / tshig don bzung sla go bde
chod che ba sogs 'chad pa'i yon tan du ma dang ldan pa zhig yin no zhes thos la/ mdor na dgung lo don gsum gyi bar du bstan pa'i bya ba kho na mdzad de/ lo de nyid kyi
tshe sa skya pa chen po rje sangs rgyas dpal bzang gi rnam par byon te/ da lo khyod zhing gzhan du 'gro gsungs pa dang / yang nub cig mkha' 'gro ma gnyis byung nas/ rnal
'byor pa khyod ni nub phyogs kyi zhing du 'gro'o zhes zer zhing glu gar gyi bsu ba dang bcas/ 'khor lo bde mchog gi bskyed rdzogs lam zab mo bla ma'i rnal 'byor/ na ro mkha'
spyod kyi bskyed rdzogs sogs thugs dam zab mo la rtse gcig pa'i ngang nas zla ba dang po'i nyer gcig la zhi bar gshegs/ de nas gnam gang gi bar thugs dam nyid la zhugs/
de las grol ba na me tog gi char dang / 'ja'i gur phub pa sogs dang / spur sbyangs pa'i tshe gdung rus dag la ston pa sangs rgyas dang / rdo rje rnal 'byor ma'i sku shin
tu gsal ba dag dang / ring bsrel gyi grangs kyang mang bar byon pa sogs ches ngo mtshar ba du ma byung ngo / /de la slob bu mang du byon pa'i nang nas thugs sras rgyud
'dzin gyi gtso bo ni/ mkhas grub chen po bzang po dpal ba ste/ dam pa 'di ni sa pho spre'u'i

lo mus kyi sa nag bya bar bltams/ gzhon nu nyid nas rdo rje nag po chen po'i zhal mngon sum du gzigs/ dgung lo brgyad pa'i tshe grub chen dkon mchog blo gros dang / rje dpal
rin pa las rab tu byung / de nas rdzong dga' ldan rtser dka' spyad drag po'i sgo nas gsan sbyong rgyun mi thung tsam mdzad skabs grogs 'ga' zhig dang bcas bsod snyoms la
ljongs rgyu tshe nam mkha'i dbyings nas 'jam dbyangs kyi mkhyen pa'i ngo bo ral gri 'od 'bar ba zhig 'ur sgra chen po dang bcas byung ba rje 'di'i dbu'i gtsug nas thim
pa'i snang ba byung / de man blo gros kyi padmo kha phye ste chos gang la yang 'bad rtsol mi dgos par thos pa tsam gyis mngon du gyur pa zhig byung nas/ dgung lo bcu gcig
pa'i tshe dpal ldan sa skyar tshad ma'i snying po rigs gter la bshad ston mdzad/ de nas grub chen dkon blos lugs gnyis kyis brtse bas bskyangs te/ thub bstan rnam rgyal
gyi chos grwar kun mkhyen chen po yab sras kyi drung du lan gnyis byon/ sde snod kyi gzhung lugs mang po'i bcud myangs ste/ gdan sa chen por slar yang bshad pa'i dga' ston
spel/ ka bcu zhes pa'i mtshan gyi dge legs gsol/ dgung lo sum cu so gcig pa'i tshe/ mkhan po kun mkhyen dpal ldan rgyal po/ las slob cung pa mkhas grub sangs rgyas 'phel/
gsang ston rje byams pa chos legs

sogs las bsnyen par rdzogs/ de gong dgung lo bcu gcig pa tsam nas bzung / grub chen dkon blo/ kun mkhyen chen po/ sangs rgyas bzang po/ 'jam dbyangs sangs rgyas rin chen/ rje
byams pa chos legs/ byang sems legs pa rgyal mtshan/ mkhas grub sangs rgyas 'od zer/ 'jam dbyangs dpal ldan rin chen/ rje sangs rgyas 'phel ba sogs yongs 'dzin du ma'i
zhabs pad bsten/ snga phyir mdo sngags kyi zab gnad mang pos thugs yid tshim par blangs/ khyad par kun mkhyen dpal ldan rgyal po lo nyi shu rtsa bzhi tsam gyi bar 'bral
med du gus pas bsten/ yang zab 'khor lo bde mchog gtso bor gyur pa'i rgyud man ngag gi bdud rtsi ngoms par gsol/ mgon des thugs sras bu chen kun gyi mchog tu brtse bas bzung
/ thos don de dag kyang dben gnas bsam lding / ngang pa brag khung sogs su rtse gcig tu nyams su bzhes pas nang du thugs rgyud la rtogs pa dpag med 'khrungs/ phyi rol
tu skal ldan gyi gdul bya dag la 'khor lo bde mchog dang / kyai rdor sogs kyi rnam sprul sna tshogs pa'i ngo mtshar gyi ltad mo bstan/ dgung lo zhe lnga pa'i tshe snga gong
nas rmi lam du bshad pa bas sgrub pa mdzad pa khyad che ba'i ltas yod pa dang / lhag par rnal 'byor ma la sgrub pa byas na tshe 'di la mkha' spyod du 'gro ba'i ltas shig
yod pas sgrub pa kho na la thugs gtad pa zhig mdzad kyang / de dus bod na che ba 'gos rngog pa 'khon gsum zhes grags pa'i rngog gi rgyud

ta si chen po'i drung chen dpal 'byor ba bya ba mched kyis 'jam dbyangs sangs rin la zhu ngo zhus par brten/ rje des dpal chos sgo'i gdan sa mdzad dgos pa'i bka'i cod pan spyi
bor bcings te lo du ma'i bar chos sgor bzhugs te 'dus pa'i tshogs la dam pa'i chos kyi dga' ston ci yang zhig spel/ de tsam nas ji srid ma gshegs kyi bar du nang du ting
nge 'dzin gyi nyams bzhes las mi g.yo bzhin du/ phyi rol tu legs bshad kyi dga' ston rgyun ma chad par stsol bar mdzad/ zhing gzhan du gshegs pa'i tshe rje btsun sa skya
pa gong ma lnga'i gzhan rnams cung zad mi gsal ba'i tshul dang / rje btsun chen po na bza' dngul mdog bzhes pa zhig gsal por byon nas/ mi lus srad sred mig la ras bkab
pa 'dra ba 'di la gnas pa ngal ba las med/ de bas byang phyogs gser mdog can du phyin pa legs zhes gsungs pa'i lung bstan dang / bde mchog gi lha mo bzhi bud med tha mal
pa bzhi'i tshul du byas te dag pa'i zhing du byon zer zhing yang yang g.yob pa byed pa sogs mkha' 'gro'i bsu ba dang bcas yos lo hor zla gsum pa'i gnam stong gi tshe mda'
kha ma'i gdams pa'i ngang nas gshegs so/ /'di la slob ma'i mchog shin tu mang yang / dpal 'khor lo sdom pa'i bka' bab cing rgyud pa 'dzin pa ni paN chen nam mkha' dbang
phyug ste/ dam pa 'di ni chos ldan gyi yab yum la lcags pho rta'i lo ngo mtshar ba'i dge mtshan du ma dang bcas te sku bltams/ dgung lo bcu grangs

la mkhan slob mtshan nyid dang ldan pa dag las rab tu byung / de nas thub bstan yangs can du phar tshad/ 'dul mngon/ dbu ma/ sdom rig sogs sde snod kyi gzhung chen rnams la
bslab sbyangs cher mdzad pas mkhas pa'i phul du phyin/ nyi shu rtsa grangs la dpal sa skya/ ngam ring / gsang phu sogs dbus gtsang gi chos grwa chen po rnams su bshad gsar
gyi dga' ston spel/ yongs 'dzin gyi bla ma yang mus chen sangs rgyas rin chen/ sa lo 'jam pa'i rdo rje/ bdag chen kun dga' bkra shis/ lo nas spyan snga rin po che ngag
dbang chos grags/ thub bstan yangs can gyi mkhan chen chos rje sogs mang du bsten te mdo sngags rig gnas kyis bsdus pa'i gsan pa rgya mtsho'i pha mthar son/ gling dga' bde
ba can du thos bsam dang 'chad nyan spel mar mdzad pa'i ring nas 'jam dbyangs sangs rgyas rin chen gyi drung du byon gsungs pa bzhin byon pas/ rje des rgya'i rdo rje dang
dril bu cha/ shing sgam che ba zhig ja khug cig rnams gnang nas/ khyod rang dbus su gshegs la smor dgon pa'i bla ma mdzod/ shing sgam 'di na bzas khongs/ ja khug 'dir
gsol ja rnams tshags mdzod/ rgya'i rdo rje dril bu 'di snoms la dbang bskur sogs bstan pa la phan nges pa'i chos 'chad rem la mdzod/ ces gsungs pa ltar dgung lo sum cu rtsa
grangs nas lo grangs du ma'i bar du dam pa'i chos kyi 'khor lo bskor bas bstan pa rin po che 'phel rgyas dang / rje rang la yang de phyogs

kyi skye bo rnams dang 'dun mchog tu gyur te/ na bza' gsol ja sogs zang zing gi 'bul nod tshad med pa byung bas/ sngar gyi bla ma'i gsung de lung bstan du dgongs nas mi phyed
pa'i dad pa 'khrungs/ lnga bcu rtsa lnga pa'i tshe gling dga' bde ba can gyi dgon gnas chen por rje btsun sems dpa' chen po dkon mchog rgyal mtshan yab sras kyi rgyal
tshab tu mnga' gsol/ de nas bzung lo grangs nyi shu tsam gyi bar du chos grwa chen po der bde kye gsang gsum/ yo ga bya spyod dang bcas pa'i dbang khrid lung man ngag rgyud
kyi bshad bka' sogs kyi chos char phab ste 'chad nyan dmar ba'i tshad du gyur/ rje 'di mdo sngags zung 'jug gi dge ba'i bshes gnyen gzhung lugs gang la yang mkhyen pa
rgyas pas paN chen nam mkha' dbang phyug ces phyogs kun du snyan par grags/ thugs sras bstan 'dzin gyi slob bu yang mang du byon/ bdag gi bla ma rje btsun mus pa chen po
de nyid kyis kyang sku gzhon nu'i dus paN chen de la bka' gdams lha bzhi'i khrid dang / gzhung drug gi lung sogs gsan pa yin la/ rtogs pa'i yon tan ni gling dga' bde ba can
gyi gdan sa mdzad dus/ ma rungs pa 'ga' zhig gis dgon pa'i ri rgya la tho 'tshams kyi las byas dus/ rje nyid kyis chos khri'i steng nas chos skyong rnams la dmod bcol
dang bcas phyag brdabs pa tsam gyis ngan pa rnams la rtags mtshan drag po de ma thag byung ba sogs mtha' yas shing / mthar dgung lo don bzhi pa chu mo lug lo zla ba brgyad
pa'i tshes gsum gyi tshe gling dga' dgon

pa'i bla brang du sku la snyung ba med bzhin du rnal 'byor ma'i 'pho ba chig brgyud ma gsal btab te/ mkha' spyod nyid du thogs pa med par gshegs/ de dus 'ja' 'od dang me tog
gi char sogs ngo mtshar ba'i ltas dpag tu med pa byung bas skye bo thams cad dad pa'i spu long ches cher g.yos par gyur to/ /rje 'di la slob ma'i mchog mang du yod pa'i
nang nas dam chos rgyud 'dzin gyi gtso bo ni rje btsun dam pa chos dbang phyug ste/ dam pa 'di ni ston pa 'das nas lo sum stong drug brgya dang zhe lnga lon pa chu pho spre'u'i
lo mus stod rta mo shar gyi bde legs kyi la rgyab kyi khud bya ba'i lhas su bltams/ dgung lo bcu pa'i tshe 'jam dbyangs sangs rgyas rin chen dang / rje dkon mchog
rin chen/ chos rje nam rgyal ba rnams las rab tu byung / bcu gcig pa'i tshe bde mchog lU nag dril gsum/ gsang 'dus mi bskyod pa/ 'jam rdor/ gur/ kye rdor yab bka' yum bka'
sogs bla med kyi sgrub dkyil mang po'i tshig don thugs la chud/ bcu gnyis pa'i tshe brtag gnyis la bshad ston spel/ bcu bzhi pa'i tshe lam 'bras kyi khrid yig dngos grub
'byung gter sogs lam 'bras kyi yig cha mang po dang / kun tu dgos pa'i gzhung bdun sogs rgyud kyi yig cha mang po'i tshig don thugs su chud te rgyugs 'bul kyang mdzad/
bco brgyad pa'i tshe kye rdor gzhi bsnyen dang / kun rig gi bsnyen pa sogs mdzad/ sum cu pa'i tshe mkhan po paN chen nam mkha' dbang phyug las gsang chos rje nam mkha' sangs
rgyas/ grib chod pa don grub rin chen/

kha skongs pa spyan snga dkon mchog rgya mtsho rnams las gling dga' bde ba can du bsnyen par rdzogs/ dgung lo bcu skor nas bzung / 'jam dbyangs sangs rgyas rin chen/ mtshungs
med dkon mchog rin chen/ bdag chen kun dga' bkra shis/ bla ma nam mkha' sangs rgyas/ ngor chen dkon mchog lhun grub/ paN chen nam mkha' dbang phyug sogs yongs 'dzin du
ma'i zhabs pad gus pas bsten zhal gyi bum bzang las/ rgyud man ngag gi bdud rtsi ngoms par gsol/ khyad par paN chen 'di la 'khor lo bde mchog gtso bor gyur pa'i mdo sngags
kyi zab gnad bum pa gang byo'i tshul du mnos/ bka' drin che ba'i yongs 'dzin mchog tu bzung / yongs 'dzin mang po'i zhal las 'ongs pa'i dam chos zab mo de dag kyang dben
gnas mang por sgom pa'i nyams bzhes rtse gcig tu mdzad pas/ so so nas bshad pa'i nyams rtogs dag kyang ci rigs par shar/ gzhan yang snga gong nas sgrub pa kho na la thugs
gtad pa nas/ smon lam 'debs pa'i tshe yang mi tshe sgrub pa dang mnyam pa'i 'dun pa kho na dang / gnas skabs su yang sgrub pa'i bsngags pa kho na mdzad pa zhig yod pas/
paN chen nam mkha' dbang phyug gis dgon pa'i gdan sa mdzad dgos pa'i bka' stsal kyang thabs mkhas kyis dgongs pa bkrol nas ma mdzad/ de mtshams nas yi dam gyi lha 'khor
lo bde mchog gi lung bstan byung nas gsang sngags rdo rje gling gi gdan

sar gdan btegs/ lo nyer lnga tsam bzhugs te der 'dus sogs skal ldan mang po smin grol la bkod/ lnga bcu nga gnyis pa'i tshe sle lung gi gdan seng ge'i khrir 'khod/ 'dus pa'i
tshogs la zab rgyas kyi chos kyi char rtag par phab/ bla ma gong ma'i rnam thar dang / blo sbyong sogs gsungs pa'i tshe bshum pa 'ba' zhig mdzad de byang sems chen po dad
pa dang nges 'byung gzhan pas che ba zhig yin par grags/ mdor na gzhon nu nyid nas chos kyi bag chags sad pa byams dang snying rje'i mnga' bdag mngon par shes pa thogs
med du mnga' ba/ bla ma dang yi dam gyi lha mang pos zhal bstan cing rjes su bzung ba'i grub pa'i dbang phyug chen po bskyed rdzogs kyi ting nge 'dzin dang thugs yid gcig
tu 'dres pa zhig yin la/ zhing gzhan du gshegs pa'i tshe yang sku la snyung ba sogs gang yang med par bu slob rnams la shar phyogs mngon par dga' ba'i zhing du phebs pa'i
zhal bzhes dang bcas bde mchog gi rgyud nas bshad pa'i rnal 'byor pa 'pho ba'i tshe 'byung ba'i ngo mtshar gyi ltas rnams mngon du mdzad pa yin no/ /rje btsun dam pa de
la slob ma'i mchog mang po zhig byon kyang / dpal 'khor lo bde mchog gi zab bcud rnams bum pa gang byo'i tshul du mnos shing / thugs sras kyi gtso bor gyur pa ni bdag cag
gi yongs 'dzin dam pa rgyal ba mus pa chen po rdo rje 'chang sangs rgyas rgyal mtshan te/ dam pa 'di ni chu pho stag gi lo dol smad kyi 'brog seb tu bltams/ dgung

lo bcu gnyis pa'i tshe mdog lo mkhan po dpal ldan rin chen pa las dge bsnyen zhus/ dpal mgon rin chen pa gnas kyi slob dpon du mdzad de gling dga' bde ba can du bde kye gsang
gsum yo ga bya spyod dang bcas pa'i rgyud dang rgya bod kyi gzhung / de dag gi spyi Tika sgrub dkyil man ngag gzhung phran la sogs pa'i yig cha mang po la gsan sbyongs
mdzad/ rje dkon mchog rgya mtsho'i drung du mdo sngags kyi gzhung dang 'brel ba shog bu mda' tshad stong phrag gnyis tsam zhig ljags thog gcig tu rgyugs 'bul mdzad/ dgung
lo nyi shu pa'i tshe mkhan po spyan snga dkon mchog rgya mtsho/ las slob rje btsun chos dbang phyug gsang ston grub chen rin chen bzang po sogs las bsnyen par rdzogs/ dus
de tsam nas mkhan slob de dag dang / gzhan yang paN chen nam mkha' dbang phyug chos rje grags pa mtha' yas/ zhe dgon pa chos rgyal mtshan/ kho bo cag gi yab rje sbas pa'i
sangs rgyas sngags 'chang grags pa blo gros rje 'gyur med bde chen/ rje rin chen chos 'phel/ mkhas dbang byams pa rab brtan/ mkhan chen chos 'od zer sogs mkhas shing
grub pa brnyes pa'i yongs 'dzin du ma las zab rgyas gsan pa rgya mtsho'i pha rol tu son par mdzad/ thos don zab mo sgom pa'i rim pas nyams bzhes su bstar bas/ bla ma dang
lhag pa'i lha mang pos rjes su bzung / rmad du byung ba'i lung bstan gyi bdud rtsi mang du brnyes/ 'od gsal gyi ngang nas skal ldan gyi gdul bya

'gro 'ongs sogs dus gsum sgrib med du gzigs te/ skal ba dang ldan pa dag la ma 'ongs pa na 'di ltar 'byung gi lung bstan gyi bdud rtsi stsal ba rnams ji lta ba bzhin mngon
du gyur pa sogs rtogs pa'i yon tan dpag med mnga'/ lung gi yon tan kyang mdo rgyud bstan bcos thams cad kyi tshig don kun la byang chub pas sde snod rin po che rnam pa gsum
dang rgyud sde bzhi nas bshad pa'i rnam dag cho gas sdom pa 'bogs pa'am/ smin byed dbang gi chu rgyun 'bebs pa'am/ grol byed khrid kyis gdams ngag ston pa'am/ mtha' drug
tshul bzhi'i rgyud don 'byed pa'am/ snyan rgyud zab mo'i byin rlabs stsol ba la sogs pa gang la yang / tshig gzhan gyis bzung sla zhing rna bar snyan don zab cing nges
pa la 'bab/ tshig don gnyis ka 'brel legs pa sogs 'chad pa'i yon tan thams cad tshang zhing / yid chags sdang gi 'chad pa dang / brjod pa mtho dman can sogs 'chad pa'i skyon
cung zad tsam kyang mi mnga' bar/ blo chen rnams la zab rgya che/ /blo chung bzung bde go sla ba/ /phyi nas tshig don 'brel chags pa/ /don phra 'gal 'brel dpyod cing
bshad/ /ces pa ltar bshad bya gang yin de'i tshig don thams cad zhib tu bshad nas/ mthar de thams cad kyi snying po bsdus pa ni 'di yin no zhes mkhas rmongs kun gyi blo
la 'char bde zhing / lag par bzung rgyu yod pa lta bu'i don gyi 'bras bu zhig ston par mdzad pas na 'chad pa'i tshul gang la yang bdag nyid chen po 'di lta bu gzhan la yod
pa ma mthong zhing / lhag par thun mong dang thun mong ma

yin pa'i zab khrid mi 'dra ba mang po ston pa kun la sla bcos dang / rigs 'dra rung mthun sbyor ba rang bzo sogs dang bral ba ste/ de rang gi skabs su bab pa rnams cung zad
kyang ma lus pa ma lhag pa ma nor ba/ ma gab par gsal zhing 'brel chags par gsungs/ de bzhin du dbang bskur bar mdzad pa rnams kyang ngag 'don bshar sbyang gi lung nyan
lta bu ma yin pa 'dag bya dag byed mtha' dag zhib tu ngo sprod cing / byin rlabs kyi zil dang ldan pas nyams kyi 'gyur ba mnan gyis mi thub pa dang / dbang de grol ba dang
/ da lan nga'i rgyud la sngags sdom rnam dag cig nges par skyes byung snyam pa gting tshugs pa 'byung / tha na rjes gnang deng bzlas lung chung ngu zhig gnang na'ang /
de'i rtsa ba'i yi ge 'di yin/ bshad srol mi 'dra ba 'di ltar yod/ bla ma gong ma dag gis nyams bzhes mdzad pas ngo mtshar gyi ltas byung ba'i lo rgyus 'di lta bu yod/ spyir
'di la yig sna 'di tsam mchis/ da lta lag len 'di'i thog nas byed/ bla ma'i zhal shes 'di ltar yod gsungs pa sogs dpyod ldan dag gi blo la 'di kho nas don 'grub pa 'dug
snyam pa'i bla ma dang / lha dang gdams ngag la dus de nyid du mi phyed pa'i dad pa thob pa zhig 'byung la/ mdor na chos gang gnang yang gsung gi gdangs thos pa tsam gyis
tha mal gyi rnam rtog rags pa rnams nyal gyis 'gro/ dmigs pa'i mtshams mtshams su 'di ltar byed ces rje de nyid kyang cung zad re mnyam par 'jog pa mdzad pa na/ ji skad
gsungs pa bzhin rgyud la skyes byung snyam pa dang /

de kha las ma 'das pa thag chod du 'dug snyam pa ma gtogs/ ci yin nam snyam pa'i blo sbram thang nger sdod pa ni mi srid pa nyams su myong bas/ gzhan du lo zlar bsgoms pa bas/
dam pa 'di'i gsung thos pa don che bar mthong la/ de ltar 'chad pa'i gnas skabs thams cad du/ zhum la gzengs bstod rgod pa la/ /'khor ba'i nyes dmigs legs par bshad/
/rmongs pa rnams la ngo mtshar gyi/ /gtam bshad nas ni mnyan du gzhug /ces pa ltar shin tu ngo mtshar ba'i lo rgyus dang / ku re dang bzhad gad nyams 'char ba dag gi sgo
nas kyang spro ba bskyed par mdzad/ gnas skabs thams cad du 'khor ba'i nyes dmigs dang / tshul khrims dang thos bsam gyi phan yon/ dge ba'i bshes gnyen gyi rtogs brjod/ khyad
par rje btsun sa skya pa yab sras bstan 'dzin dang bcas pa rnams kyi che ba'i yon tan dang bstan pa'i srol gtod tshul sogs snyan zhing 'jebs pa'i gsung gis gdul bya
dag gi dad pa dang blo gros kyi dbang po kun nas rgyas par mdzad pa zhig yin no/ /tshul de lta bu'i sgo nas dge bsnyen dge tshul dge slong gi sdom pa 'bog pa/ byang sems
kyi bslab pa/ smin byed kyi dbang / grol byed kyi khrid/ gzhan yang mdo sngags kyi bshad bka'/ lung bka' rjes gnang byin rlabs sogs zab pa dang rgya che ba'i chos tshul bgrang
ba las 'das pa zhig stsal te/ skal ldan bstan 'dzin gyi slob bu yang ches mang ba zhig bskrun nas rgya mtsho'i gos can ma lus pa khyab pa mdzad

pa yin la/ de ltar dgung lo bcu gnyis pa'i tshe dge bsnyen gyi brtul zhugs la gnas par mdzad pa de tsam nas bzung / bdun cu don bdun gyi bar du bstan pa rin po che'i bya ba
rnam pa gsum gtso bor gyur pa'i ngo mtshar rmad du byung ba'i mdzad pa kho nas dus 'da' bar mdzad cing / khyad par gnas skabs thams cad du 'khor lo bde mchog gi bskyed rdzogs
zab mo la rtse gcig tu nyams bzhes mdzad pas/ nyams myong ting nge 'dzin gyi yon tan gyi tshogs bsam gyis mi khyab pa thugs rgyud la 'khrungs te/ rtogs pa'i gdeng dang
ldan pa'i gsung las kyang / nged bde mchog gi rnal 'byor pa rnams 'chi ba'i tshe/ rtsa rgyud las/ rnal 'byor pa rnams 'pho ba'i tshe/ /dpal ldan khrag 'thung sogs mkha'
'gro/ /lag na me tog sna tshogs thogs/ /rol mo'i sgra ni sna tshogs dang / /sna tshogs glu yi mchod pas mchod/ /'chi ba zhes bya'i rnam rtog ni/ /mkha' la spyod pa'i gnas
su khyer/ /zhes gsungs pa ltar na rgyu med pa'i 'chi ba zhig yong ba yin/ nged kyi bla ma chos dbang pa la'ang byung / nged la yang de ltar yong gsungs pa bzhin/ sku
tshe'i mjug tu bsam gtan phug tu bug sgo mdzad de sgrub pa la rtse gcig tu bzhugs nas zhing gshegs kha'i tshe/ cung zad bsnyel ba'i tshul bstan pa'i dus skabs re sku 'dar
shig shig mdzad pa la/ sku mi bde ba mi 'dug lags sam zhus pas/ mi bde ba ma mchis nang gi rtsa mdud rnams grol ba'i rtags su

gda' gsungs/ yang lan cig rje'i gzim phug na phyag phyi ba su yang med pa la gsung gleng di ri ri mdzad pa/ dbon po gzim phug gi phyi na yod pas thos nas ci yin nam snyam drung
du phyin pas/ mkha' 'gro ma tsho rang byon mdzod cig gsungs pa gsal por thos pa dang / gzhan yang mkha' 'gro ma lA ma ni lta ba rang dga' zer ba 'dug de de ka yin gsungs
shing thugs bde nyams chen po mdzad pa dang / yang gshegs par nye ba'i tshe/ zla ba shar bar 'dug gam thams cad 'od dkar pos gang 'dug gsungs pa dang / da ni nyi ma
yang shar byung zhes pa dang / yang DA ki ma 'od gsal ma bu 'phrod byung gsungs pa sogs mdor na dus der rdo rje lus kyi rtsa mdud thams cad grol te bde stong lhan cig skyes
pa'i ye shes thugs rgyud la 'khrungs pa'i mod la ngo mtshar ba'i gsung de lta bu byon pa ni mya ngan las 'da' khar 'bras bu sangs rgyas kyi go 'phang mngon du mdzad pa'i
thun mong ma yin pa'i rtags su shes par bya ste/ 'di lta bu ni sngon dpal ldan bla ma dam pa bsod nams rgyal mtshan zhing gzhan du gshegs pa'i tshe ting nge 'dzin khyad
par can thugs rgyud la 'khrungs nas/ gsung las/ 'di 'dra'i bde ba/ mi 'gyur ba'i bde ba/ stong pa'i bde ba/ 'dzag med kyi bde ba zhes gsungs te/ dus der phyag rgya chen
po mchog gi dngos grub mngon du mdzad par de nyid kyi rnam thar rnams las 'byung ba dang mtshungs pa nyid yin no/ /de nas mya ngan las 'da' ba'i

tshul ston pa'i tshe thugs dam gyi ngang nas phyag phreng ring ba phud nas sku 'khris kyi bang khar 'jog par mdzad/ thung ba phyag na yod bzhin par dam rdzas ril bu cung zad
cig gsol/ yud pa zhig mnyam bzhag mdzad de/ gzod phaTa? ces pa'i sgra che ba gnyis dang / yang phaTa? kyang gsungs pa 'dra ba/ hika kyang gsungs pa 'dra ba chung ngu zhig
gsungs pa'i mod la sku 'khrug tsam dang dbu skyod tsam zhig mdzad de tsheg sgra che ba dang bstun dbu las rlangs pa skya bun pa dang bcas te 'da' kha ma'i gdams pa zab
mo gsal 'debs par mdzad pa'i sgo nas/ dgung lo bdun cu don bdun bzhes pa zla ba lnga pa'i nyer gcig la dben gnas bsam gtan phug nas mkha' spyod chen po 'og min du gshegs
pa'i tshul bstan to/ /de ma dag sku 'khor ba rnams kyis dbu la bltas pas/ sngar nas 'pho ba 'byongs pa'i rtags dbu gtsug ting sgong sham ma'i tshad tsam zhig 'bur por yod
pa'i dbus der bug pa zangs thal du dod pa'i nang nas rtsa sbubs stong sbom phra snyug ma 'bring po tsam gyi tshad tsam zhig rgyangs gyis 'thon pa la byang sems kyi zil
pa nyel le ba dang bcas 'dug pa der yod kun gyis mthong bar gyur to/ /de dang dus mtshungs par 'ja' dkar po ras yug brkyangs pa 'dra ba'i mtha' 'ja' sngon pos rgyan pa zhig
gzim phug gi thad nas byung ste bar snang la yal song ba skal ldan 'ga' res mthong ba byung 'dug pa/ 'di lta bu ni sngon paN chen ga ya dha ra 'pho ba'i rnal

'byor gyi gshegs pa'i tshe dbu gtsug nas 'od ril ma tsam zhig bar snang la song ba kun gyis mthong ba'i rnam thar dang tshul mtshungs par mngon no/ /de ltar bdag nyid chen
po 'di nyid zhing gzhan du gshegs pa'i dus de dang ha cang mi ring ba'i skabs shig rje bla ma mkhan chen thams cad mkhyen pa ngag dbang chos kyi grags pa nyid rtse lnga'i
bla brang rdzong dang / mang mkhar gyi dgon pa bde ba can sogs su shin tu dben pa'i thugs dam bcad rgya la yun ring du bzhugs pa'i dus shig gi tshe rgyal ba mus pa chen
po dang mjal 'dod kyi thugs 'dun lhag par g.yos nas/ de nub mnal lam bzung nas byang phyogs kyi nam mkha' rgyang ring po la 'phur byon pas gling dga' bla brang du phebs byung
ba na de'i tshoms kyi bzhugs khri la rje mus chen bzhugs 'dug pa dang mjal bas thugs dges spro dpag med 'khrungs shing / rje'i gsung las/ sa skya nas zhabs drung bla
brang gi yangs rtse na bzhugs pas de la mjal ba mdzod ces gsungs byung ba bzhin de ltar mdzad nas/ mnal lam zin pa de ka'i ngang nas gling dga' mgon khang der phebs pas
dgon pa'i chos skyong gnas par grags pa'i gur mgon gyi zhal 'bag rje 'jam dbyangs sangs rgyas rin chen gyi phyag nas bzhugs pa zhig yod pa de sku mdun du bub pa'i tshul du
'dug pa 'di cis lan gsungs pas/ de na yod pa'i mi 'ga' zhig na re/ mgon khang gi zhal 'bag 'gyel ba 'di ka da lo grub chen ti lo pa gnas gzhan du gshegs pa'i snga ltas
su

'dug zer byung bas/ mnal sad ma thag thugs ma bde zhing myur du sku mtshams sangs nas rje bla ma mjal bar mus phyogs su phebs bzhed kyang / de nas yun ring ma lon par rje btsun
rdo rje 'chang de nyid zhing gzhan du gshegs pa'i kha skad gsan pa na/ phan tshun thugs yid gcig 'dres kyi bla ma de dang / mjal 'dod thugs kyi lhag mar lus bzhin du/
de ma thag 'khor lo bde mchog nag po lugs kyi dkyil 'khor zhal phye ste bdag 'jug brgya rtsa bzhes pa sogs kyi sgo nas dgongs pa chos dbyings su rdzogs par mdzad do zhes
thos la/ mtshan ltas ngo mtshar can de lta bu 'byung ba ni/ bdag cag gi bla ma rgyal ba mus pa chen po de nyid dus kyi dbang gis gdul bya rnams kyi snang ngor dge slong
rdo rje 'dzin pa'i tshul bzung ba tsam ma gtogs don la 'phags yul gyi grub chen ti lo pa dang spangs rtogs kyi yon tan mnyam pa'am/ rnam par sprul pa yin pa'i nges pa'i
mtshan ma yang dag par kho bos nges shes snying nas rnyed pas na rjes 'jug skal bzang rnams kyis de ltar du dgongs par mdzod cig de lta bu'i yongs 'dzin 'brel tshad don ldan
de nyid kyi drung du/ kho bo cag rang lo bcu bdun du slebs pa/ rje nyid dgung lo bdun cu rtsa gnyis su phebs pa glang gi lo gling dga' bde ba can gyi chos grwa chen por
mjal ba nas bzung / lo grangs du ma zhig gi bar dad pa dang gus pa chen po'i sgo nas rje 'di'i zhabs pad spyi bo'i gtsug tu bsten/ 'bad pa dang rtsol ba chen

pos zhal gyi bum bzang las/ bstan pa'i rtsa ba sdom pa gsum gyi bka' drin dang / gzhan yang dbang / byin rlabs/ rjes gnang / bka' gtad kyi rigs mang po/ lung gi tshogs du ma/
gsang sngags rdo rje theg pa gtso bor gyur pa'i zab khrid lnga phrag gsum tsam dang / de dag dang 'brel ba'i mdo sde dang rgyud sde/ rgya gzhung dang bod gzhung 'grel
pa 'grel bshad dang bcas pa sogs chos tshul rgya mtsho lta bu'i bdud rtsi ngoms par 'thungs/ khyad par du rgyud sde'i nges gsang / mkha' 'gro'i gsang tshig rje btsun sa skya
pa rnams kyi yab chos thugs kyi nying khu mkha' spyod bsgrub pa'i nye lam/ yang zab 'khor lo bde mchog lU nag dril gsum/ na ro mkha' spyod dang bcas pa'i dbang dang /
byin rlabs kyi bka'/ bskyed rdzogs kyi khrid bka' zab mo/ man ngag zhar byung phra mo tshun chad dang bcas pa/ de dag gi rgyab rten rgyud dang / rgya bod kyi gzhung tshad
ldan du ma'i bshad lung sogs mdor na rnal 'byor gsang mtha'i chos skor mtha' dag bum pa gang byo'i tshul du legs par stsal cing thugs rje'i spyan ras kyis bu gcig pa ltar
'tsho bar mdzad de dus gsum sgrib med du gzigs pa'i rje btsun mus pa chen po 'khor lo sdom pa de nyid dang / dad ldan gyi slob bu bdag cag kyang byang chub bar du mi 'bral
ba'i zhal bzhes kyi bdud rtsi snying la sim pas/ des na kho bo cag bu slob rjes 'brangs dang bcas pa rnams tshe rabs gtan legs kyi 'dun ma zin par gor ma chag go /e
ma mkha' 'gro'i zhal rlangs

ma yal chos/ /chos zab bde mchog rnal 'byor gsang mtha'i lam/ /lam 'di chos dang rigs las skyes pa'i bu/ /bu mchog rnams la lan brgyar spel bar  'dod pa'i bsam pa 'di skyabs
gnas kun 'dus bla ma'i thugs rjes yid bzhin du 'grub par shog /ces smon gnas 'grub pa'i dge legs kyi tshig brjod pa dang bcas te/ de ltar de dag gis ni dpal sa skya pa'i
yab chos kyi nying khu 'khor lo sdom pa'i dam pa'i chos byung ba'i tshul legs par bshad pa bde mchog chos kun gsal ba'i nyin byed ces bya ba ma tshang ba med pa bstan zin
to/ /'dir smras pa/ dus gsum rgyal ba'i rnam 'phrul sngags 'chang rje/ /gang gi thugs sras grub mchog dbang po dang / /yab rje sbas pa'i sangs rgyas grags pa'i mtshan/
/'gran bral yab sras gsum gyis slar yang skyongs/ /dang por spangs rtogs mthar phyin rdzogs sangs rgyas/ /bar du 'jam dbyangs buddha ratna'i zhabs/ /tha mar dus gsum mkhyen
pa'i bshes gnyen che/ /rje btsun mus pas byang chub bar du srungs/ /rgyal dang de sras ngo bor ro gcig kyang / /gdul bya'i snang ngor tha dad tshul 'dzin pa'i/ /spyan
snga mkhan chen thams cad mkhyen pa sogs/ /drin chen bla ma rnams kyis dge legs mdzod/ /'khor lo sdom pa'i dam chos byung ba'i tshul/ /legs bshad sngon med nyi ma 'di shar
bas/ /zab yang bde mchog chos tshul ma lus kun/ /mthong bar 'gyur ro ltos shig blo gsal rnams/ /sngon dus 'phags pa'i yul dang gangs ljongs 'dir/ /rim

bzhin byon pa'i skyes chen bgrang yas rnams/ /rnal 'byor gsang mtha'i nye lam 'dir zhugs nas/ /mkha' spyod nyams dga'i zhing khams dog por byas/ /bdag kyang sngon gyi las 'phro
mi dman pas/ /'khor lo sdom pa ngur smrig bla gos can/ /yongs 'dzin buddha'i zhal gyi bum bzang las/ /bde mchog chos tshul rgya mtsho'i bdud rtsi mnos/ /rang gi sngon
bsags rmad byung las 'phro dang / /tshe 'dir nyams len brtson 'grus nyer len rkyen/ /'dzoms na mkha' spyod bde ba'i grong khyer der/ /tshegs med myur du bgrod la som nyi
ci/ /de lta na yang le lo'i dbang gyur tam/ /sems dang nyams len 'dres pa'i ting 'dzin la/ /skad cig tsam yang gnas pa'i skabs bral ba'i/ /bdag 'dra 'chi ba'i tshe na a
tsa ma/ /'on kyang bla ma'i byin rlabs sems la zhugs/ /ci byas bstan dang 'gro ba'i don chen 'grub/ /sdig bshags nyams len zab mos mtshams sbyar nas/ /phyi ma bde ldan zhing
du skye bar smon/ /'di sbyar dge bas bdag cag dpon slob kyi/ /dus gsum bsags pa'i sdig sgrib kun byang nas/ /gnas skabs rdo rje'i lus 'dres dbang po gsal/ /tshe la bar
chad med par mthar phyin shog /bstan pa 'dzin pa'i chos dang rigs kyi bu/ /bgrang yas 'byung zhing rgyun chad med pa dang / /dpon slob kun kyang phyi ma lhan cig par/
/zhing mchog bde ba can du skye bar shog /slar yang gang 'dul sprul pa sna tshogs kyis/ /

spyi dang bye brag dpal ldan sa skya pa'i/ /bstan pa rin chen srid mthar spel ba la/ /kun gyis 'gran zla bral ba'i mthu ldan shog /chos kun gdod nas spros bral stong nyid dang
/ /snang ba 'gag med 'char ba'i gsal cha gnyis/ /ye nas bral med zung 'jug blo 'das dang / /brjod bral nges don bde mchog zhal mthong shog /e ma nyams len zab mo'i gnad
'di 'dra/ /shes pas 'di phyi bar do'i gnas skabs su/ /lan cig 'khrul yang de yi rang mtshang de/ /rig pa'i mod la ye shes 'char bar shog /'khrul zad bla ma rnams kyi thugs
rje dang / /lhag bsam dag pa'i mthu dang chos kyi dbyings/ /bden pa'i stobs kyis 'di dang phyi ma'i don/ /yid la bsam pa ji bzhin 'grub gyur cig /ces dpal sa skya pa'i
yab chos kyi nying khu 'khor lo bde mchog gi dam pa'i chos byung ba'i tshul legs par bshad pa bde mchog chos kun gsal ba'i nyin byed ces bya ba 'di yang / khams gsum chos
kyi rgyal po grub pa'i 'khor los bsgyur ba padma'i rnam 'phrul 'jam pa'i dbyangs bsod nams dbang po dang / byang chub sems dpa' zhi ba mtsho'i rnam par sprul pa rgyal
sras sbas pa'i rnal 'byor dpal sa skya pa chen po sngags 'chang grags pa blo gros te 'jam pa'i dbyangs sku mched las lugs 'di'i sgrub dkyil gyi lung dang / cho ga'i phyag
khrid sogs kyi bka' drin zhib rgyas su mnos shing / khyab bdag 'khor lo'i mgon rgyal ba mus pa chen po rdo rje 'chang

mi'i gzugs can rje btsun dam pa sangs rgyas rgyal mtshan las dpal sa skya pa'i yab chos kyi nying khu 'khor lo bde mchog lU nag dril gsum na ro mkha' spyod dang bcas pa'i dbang
byin rlabs/ bskyed rdzogs kyi zab khrid/ rgyud dang rgya bod kyi gzhung mang po'i bshad lung sogs mdor na rnal 'byor gsang mtha'i gdams pa rgya mtsho lta bu'i bka' drin
mnos pa'i skal ba bzang por gyur cing / gzhan yang sprul pa'i sku lo nas spyan snga rin po che kun dga'i mtshan can dang / mkhan chen thams cad mkhyen pa ngag dbang chos
kyi grags pa la sogs te/ yongs 'dzin chos bzhin du spyod pa du ma'i zhabs rdul spyi bos len pa shrI sa skya pa shAkya'i dge bsnyen paNDi tamkhas pa rigs sngags 'chang
ba ngag dbang kun dga' bsod nams grags pa rgyal mtshan dpal bzang pos/ sngon dus byon pa'i skyes chen rnams kyi rnal 'byor gsang mtha'i chos skor mtha' dag dar rgyas su
mdzad pa'i tshul rnams la dad pa bcos min skyes pa dang / da dung kho bo cag rjes 'brangs dang bcas pa la brten nas rnal 'byor gsang mtha'i bstan pa dar rgyas su gyur na
ci ma rung snyam pa'i lhag bsam dag pas kun nas bslangs te/ zab mo'i yang rtse dpal 'khor lo bde mchog gi chos tshul rgya mtsho lta bu la yun ring mo nas 'dris par byas te/
rang gi bgrang gzhi bcu phrag bzhi dang nyag ma gnyis lon pa/ rgya gar 'phags pa'i yul na ba hu dha nyaHste 'bru mang po zhes grags shing rgya nag lugs la sa pho stag
gi lo bye pA Shi zhes pa'i zla ba'i dkar phyogs rdzogs pa dang

po'i tshes la gu na yon tan rin chen 'byung gnas dpal sa skya'i ratna ka raHshrI wan bhu mi paNDu ka'i gnas mchog bzhi thog bla brang chen mo'i gtsug lag khang gi yang steng
sngon med gsar du bskrun pa'i li ma lha khang rdo rje'i gdan dang / rgya nag lha khang ri bo rtse lnga'i bya 'dabs dpe khang chos mdzod chen mor legs par sbyar ba'o/ /yang
smras pa/ 'di ltar bgyis pa'i yi ge'i 'du byed mkhan/ /rang dang nyer gnas dge slong rdo rje 'dzin/ /gzhung lugs kun la rnam dpyod blo rgyas pa'i/ /rab 'byams smra ba
bsam gtan rgya mtshos bgyis/ /bstan bcos 'di la nongs pa'i cha mchis na/ /mchog gzigs dam pa rnams kyi spyan sngar bshags/ /bdag dang mkha' mnyam sems can ma lus pa'i/ /sngon
bsags sdig dang lhan cig sbyang du gsol/ /legs bshad 'di don 'dzin dang sems pa dang / /ri mor 'bri sogs blo gsal don gnyer ba/ /de dag rnams la bsrung zhing skyob
pa dang / /chos 'di spel ba nor u rgyan mkha' 'gro'i gling na bzhugs pa'i skyong pho mos mdzod/ /'dis bdag cag dpon slob rnams kyi 'di phyi'i don thams cad yid la re ba bzhin
'bad med lhun grub tu 'byung ba'i rgyur gyur cig /sarba mangga laM/thams cad bkra shis/ ka lya dge legs 'phel bar gyur cig na wandhantu/ dharme chos 'di dar bar gyur
cigu da ya mastu/ i 'dis bstan pa dang sems can la phan thogs par gyur cigdam
